❯ You are in PLAN MODE for a refactor of the NOC Agent’s case-handling,         
  operational memory, and self-learning loop.                                   
                                                                                
  Do not implement code yet.                                                    
  Do not edit files yet.                                                        
  First inspect the repository and produce a concrete implementation plan with  
  file/function-level detail, migration steps, test strategy, risks, acceptance 
  criteria, and a learning-loop architecture.                                   
                                                                                
  This refactor has two linked goals:                                           
                                                                                
      1. Operational correctness:                                               
         Make cases the authoritative state machine so the NOC Agent stops      
  duplicating work, flapping, and false-resolving concerns when scans jitter.   
                                                                                
      2. Institutional learning:                                                
         Turn every useful case, operator correction, diagnosis, handoff,       
  suppression, and resolution into durable learning signal that can eventually  
  feed the institutional `hyrule-knowledge` repository.                         
                                                                                
  Important context                                                             
  -----------------                                                             
                                                                                
  We have an institutional knowledge repository named:                          
                                                                                
      hyrule-knowledge                                                          
                                                                                
  It contains ODF-formatted operational knowledge.                              
                                                                                
  The desired architecture should feed operationally useful knowledge into      
  `hyrule-knowledge` over time, while also allowing the NOC Agent to retrieve   
  relevant `hyrule-knowledge` content during future case handling.              
                                                                                
  Treat `hyrule-knowledge` as the governed, durable, model-independent          
  institutional memory of the NOC.                                              
                                                                                
  The model is replaceable.                                                     
  The case state, traces, evals, operator feedback, and `hyrule-knowledge` are  
  the durable IP.                                                               
                                                                                
  High-level thesis                                                             
  -----------------                                                             
                                                                                
  The opportunity is not merely picking the best generalist model.              
                                                                                
  The opportunity is building a learning loop on top of interchangeable models, 
  where human capital and token capital compound over time.                     
                                                                                
  A company should be able to switch the underlying generalist model without    
  losing the “company veteran” expertise accumulated by the NOC Agent.          
                                                                                
  Therefore:                                                                    
                                                                                
      The model is replaceable.                                                 
      IncidentMemory, traces, evals, feedback, workflow policy, and             
  `hyrule-knowledge` are durable.                                               
                                                                                
  The design must pass this model-swap test:                                    
                                                                                
      If we swapped the underlying LLM tomorrow, would the NOC Agent retain its 
  operational memory, learned workflows, prior diagnoses, suppression           
  semantics, eval history, and institutional NOC judgment?                      
                                                                                
  If the answer is no, the design is too model-centric.                         
                                                                                
  Current problem                                                               
  ---------------                                                               
                                                                                
  The current NOC Agent loop is effectively architected as stateless            
  re-derivation on every cycle:                                                 
                                                                                
      scan → rank → gate → investigate → report → handoff                       
                                                                                
  Because the loop re-derives state each cycle, it has accumulate               
  ──── (1822 lines hidden) ──────────────────────────────────────────────────── 
  at.                                                                           
      - Any risk of stale or unreviewed knowledge becoming authoritative.       
      - Any risk of leaking sensitive operational data into knowledge           
  artifacts.                                                                    
      - Any need for human review before knowledge promotion.                   
      - Any decisions that need human confirmation before coding.               
                                                                                
  ## 13. Acceptance Criteria                                                    
                                                                                
  The refactor is successful when:                                              
                                                                                
      - IncidentMemory/cases are the authoritative state for active concerns.   
      - A missed/skipped scan never causes false all-clear.                     
      - A case resolves only on positive clean observation or operator close.   
      - Duplicate reports are prevented by case state, not cycle-local          
  signatures.                                                                   
      - Reassertions are case-grounded.                                         
      - Investigations are skipped when prior diagnosis is recent and signals   
  are unchanged.                                                                
      - Reinvestigations include prior diagnosis/recommendations as context.    
      - Handoff never opens a duplicate when the case already has an issue      
  URL/ID.                                                                       
      - Snooze/ack/suppression state lives on the case with TTL semantics.      
      - The five existing ad-hoc anti-duplication mechanisms are either removed 
  or reduced to temporary compatibility fallbacks.                              
      - No new ad-hoc anti-duplication memory mechanism is introduced.          
      - Case events and decision traces are structured enough for replay/eval.  
      - Operator feedback attaches to case IDs and trace IDs.                   
      - `hyrule-knowledge` can be retrieved during investigation/report/handoff 
  decisions.                                                                    
      - Retrieved `hyrule-knowledge` is cited in traces with document           
  path/version/revision where available.                                        
      - Resolved or corrected cases can produce candidate ODF knowledge         
  updates.                                                                      
      - Candidate knowledge updates are review-gated before becoming            
  authoritative.                                                                
      - Approved `hyrule-knowledge` survives model swaps.                       
      - Private evals can replay cases with frozen case state and frozen        
  knowledge revisions.                                                          
      - Tests cover scan jitter, clean observation, dedup, investigation reuse, 
  handoff idempotency, suppression TTL, migration, knowledge retrieval,         
  candidate knowledge generation, and model-swap behavior.                      
                                                                                
  Final instruction                                                             
  -----------------                                                             
                                                                                
  Return a concrete implementation plan only.                                   
                                                                                
  Do not write implementation code.                                             
                                                                                
  Be specific. Include file paths, function names, classes, and exact code      
  areas to change after inspecting the repository.                              
                                                                                
  If the repository already partially implements this design, identify what     
  exists and plan only the missing pieces.                                      
                                                                                
  If any part of this prompt is wrong relative to the code, explicitly say so   
  and adjust the plan accordingly.

  What I found

  The work is not in this repo. The cwd hyperliquid-trading-agent contains zero
  NOC concepts. The refactor targets two siblings:
  - /home/svag/Dev/hyrule-noc-agent (remote AS215932/noc-agent) — the loop +
  cases
  - /home/svag/Dev/knowledge (remote AS215932/knowledge) — the institutional
  repo your prompt calls "hyrule-knowledge"

  Three findings that change the plan vs. the prompt's assumptions:

  1. Two parallel worlds, one already a real state machine. The reactive path
  (app/incident_memory.py) already has a durable, well-built case state machine
  — statuses
  investigating/waiting_approval/recovered_pending/resolved/expired/linked,
  parent↔child topology linking (downstream_victims, linked_parent_case,
  _find_open_parent_case, _link_cases), and crucially it already resolves only 
  on positive recovery + cooldown, never on absence (recovered_pending→resolved
  after RECOVERY_COOLDOWN_SECONDS; idle→expired is a distinct status). The
  proactive loop (app/proactive/loop.py) is the stateless re-derivation problem
  you described, and its 5 anti-dup side stores are keyed by hotspot fingerprint
  (sha256(rule_id|key)[:16]) while cases are keyed by alert-identity 
  fingerprint — so the side stores and the case live in different keyspaces and
  never share state. The core refactor is to ground the proactive stages in
  IncidentMemory cases and fold the 5 side stores into case fields/events. The
  reactive parent/child linking + correlate() is the natural seed for
  meta-cases.
  2. Cases are not on-disk files. NOC-20260617-006 is a display case_number;
  cases live in Redis (prod) or in-memory (local/test) with TTLs. There's no
  cases/*.json to migrate, and in local mode cases are not durable across
  restarts.
  3. It's OKF, not ODF. The knowledge repo is OKF (Markdown + YAML frontmatter +
  deterministic JSONL/SQLite exports) — no OpenDocument anywhere. The promotion
  artifact is a learning_ledger_v1 JSON event
  (schema/learning-event.schema.json, with a noc_shadow producer and
  lesson_candidate type already defined) → ledger/proposed/ → human review →
  ledger promote-pr → okf/curated/. Retrieval tooling (retrieval.py,
  context_pack.py, an MCP server, SQLite/JSONL exports) exists, but the
  NOC↔knowledge bridge today is fixtures-only (app/knowledge_shadow.py) — no
  live retrieval or promotion is wired. #31's carry-forward fix is already
  merged to main.

  Four decisions will materially shape the plan:

● User answered Claude's questions:
  ⎿  · This session's cwd is `hyperliquid-trading-agent`, but the refactor lives
     in `hyrule-noc-agent` (loop/cases) and `knowledge` (the OKF 
     'hyrule-knowledge' repo). How should I target the work? (The plan file 
     stays here either way.) → Proceed cross-repo now (Recommended)
     · After preserving the already-merged #31 carry-forward fix, what should 
     the plan sequence first? → Operational consolidation first (Recommended)
     · IncidentMemory cases are durable only on Redis; the local backend is 
     in-memory (lost on restart). For proactive case state to be 
     authoritative/durable in production, what's the assumption? → Do not 
     require Redis for the refactor. Use Postgres as the authoritative 
     production backend for IncidentMemory, meta-cases, observations, case 
     events, handoffs, suppressions, feedback, trace references, and LangGraph 
     checkpoints. Redis/Valkey may be introduced later only as an optional 
     hot-path optimization for queues, pub/sub, short-lived dedup/rate-limit 
     windows, or high-volume storm correlation. No production behavior should 
     silently depend on Redis as a second source of truth.
     · How should the NOC agent retrieve approved hyrule-knowledge during 
     correlation/investigation? The knowledge repo exposes both an MCP server 
     and deterministic SQLite/JSONL exports. → Hybrid, but export-authoritative 
     for prod: the NOC Agent should retrieve approved hyrule-knowledge from a 
     pinned deterministic SQLite/JSONL export during correlation/investigation, 
     with document path, status, and repo revision cited in traces. The 
     hyrule-knowledge MCP server may be used as a read-only noc role for richer 
     context-pack/resolve workflows, development, validation, and optional 
     online enrichment, but production decisions and replay/evals must be 
     reproducible from the pinned export. If MCP is unavailable, behavior should
     not degrade except for optional enrichment.

     Knowledge retrieval must be replayable. Every investigation/correlation 
     trace must record the exact hyrule-knowledge document path, document ID, 
     approval status, section if available, and repo revision/export version 
     used.

     │ Case-Grounded Self-Learning Loop Refactor Plan                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Context                                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Why this change. The NOC Agent's proactive loop                         │
     │ (hyrule-noc-agent/app/proactive/loop.py) re-derives state every cycle   │
     │ (scan → rank → gate → investigate → report → handoff/resolve) and has   │
     │ accreted five separate anti-duplication side stores to stop flapping,   │
     │ duplicate reports, duplicate tickets, and false all-clears. None of     │
     │ them share one notion of "the current state of a concern," and —        │
     │ critically — they are keyed by hotspot fingerprint                      │
     │ (sha256(rule_id|key)[:16], models.py:Hotspot.fingerprint) while the     │
     │ durable case is keyed by alert-identity fingerprint                     │
     │ (incident_memory.py:fingerprint_alert). The proactive loop therefore    │
     │ makes its don't-duplicate decisions outside the case.                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Meanwhile the reactive path already has the state machine we want:      │
     │ IncidentMemory (app/incident_memory.py) keeps durable cases with a real │
     │ lifecycle, parent↔child topology linking, and                           │
     │ resolve-only-on-positive-recovery semantics. The refactor's thesis —    │
     │ the case is the authoritative state machine — is already half-true; we  │
     │ must extend the case to own the proactive stages too, add meta-cases    │
     │ for notification storms, and wire a replayable, governed                │
     │ hyrule-knowledge learning loop so institutional NOC judgment survives a │
     │ model swap.                                                             │
     │                                                                         │

     │ the │                                                                   │
     │ │            │  graph via synthetic alert)                              │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ ├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ Report     │ loop.py:_report_decision, _safe_report, _default_report, │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │            │ _hotspot_field, _case_for_hotspot                        │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ ├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ Handoff    │                                                          │
     │ app/proactive/handoff.py:GitHubHandoff.ensure_candidate_is │            │
     │ │            │ sue (issue #-marker search)                              │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ ├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ Resolve /  │ loop.py:_merge_with_carried + _report_decision           │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │ all-clear  │ (proactive); incident_memory.py:_expire_*_cases          │
     │ (reactive) │                                                            │
     │ ├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ Snooze /   │ app/proactive/suppressions.py:SuppressionStore;          │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │ ack /      │ loop.py:_apply_suppressions, _auto_snooze;               │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │ suppress   │ app/icinga_ack.py                                        │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ └────────────┴───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┘                                                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Memory / state                                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - IncidentMemory (app/incident_memory.py): Redis or in-memory           │
     │ _LocalIncidentMemory. Case dict from _new_case (incident_id,            │
     │ case_number, fingerprint, identity, resource_id, status,                │
     │ downstream_victims, linked_parent_case, recovered_at,                   │
     │ latest_transition, event_count, source_excerpt, …). Indices:            │
     │ fingerprint_index, case_number_index, resource_open_cases,              │
     │ topology_parents, noc:case:expiry zset. Statuses:                       │
     │ OPEN_CASE_STATUSES={investigating,waiting_approval,recovered_pending}   │
     │ plus resolved/expired/linked.                                           │
     │ - ProactiveMemory (app/proactive/memory.py): lessons/ (md), proposals/  │
     │ (CandidateLesson json), observations.jsonl, journal/. A learning        │
     │ flywheel (evaluate_outcomes), not operational truth — correct already.  │
     │ - Budget ledger (app/proactive/ledger.py): per-day ledger-{day}.json    │
     │ (cycles/investigations/cost/handoffs) — cost control, not learning.     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Fingerprint logic                                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Hotspot: models.py:Hotspot.fingerprint =                              │
     │ sha256(f"{rule_id}|{key}")[:16].                                        │
     │ - Case: incident_memory.py:fingerprint_alert(payload)=sha256(alert_iden │
     │ tity(payload)). A hotspot becomes a case via                            │
     │ models.py:hotspot_to_alert_payload (source="proactive") → intake_alert. │
     │ The two keyspaces never meet except in loop.py:_case_for_hotspot        │
     │ (advisory digest linking).                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Eval / trace / feedback / model abstraction (what exists)               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Decision context: models.py:DecisionContext (decision_id, cycle_id,   │
     │ manifest_hash, ruleset_version, model_chain, budget_state,              │
     │ injected_lesson_ids) — built per cycle, but only decision_id is         │
     │ persisted (onto the report); no queryable trace store.                  │
     │ - Journal/observations: per-cycle journal/{cycle_id}.md +               │
     │ observations.jsonl + evaluate_outcomes (predictions vs reactive         │
     │ alerts).                                                                │
     │ - Feedback: graph_runtime.record_operator_decision via Discord          │
     │ /noc_decide, web POST /control/incidents/{id}/decision, app/nocctl.py.  │
     │ - Model abstraction: app/model_config.py (AgentModelConfig,             │
     │ FallbackModel, active_model_chain), app/model_metrics.py (token usage,  │
     │ fallback counters). Versioned via ruleset_version, manifest_hash,       │
     │ model_chain. No prompt_version/policy_version yet.                      │
     │ - Knowledge integration: fixtures only — app/knowledge_shadow.py        │
     │ validates evals/knowledge_shadow/ context-pack + learning_ledger_v1     │
     │ fixtures. No live retrieval, no live promotion.                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ hyrule-knowledge (current)                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ OKF Markdown + YAML frontmatter under okf/{curated,generated,observed}; │
     │ deterministic exports                                                   │
     │ exports/{knowledge.sqlite,*.jsonl,manifest.json};                       │
     │ schema/{frontmatter,learning-event,…}.schema.json; knowledge-policy.yml │
     │ (roles incl. noc_shadow); ledger/{fixtures,proposed,reviews};           │
     │ src/hyrule_knowledge/{retrieval,context_pack,store,learning_ledger,prom │
     │ otion,policy,mcp_server}.py; CI request-promotion/ingest open           │
     │ review-gated PRs (never auto-merge). Authority tiers A0–A5.             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 2. Existing Side-Store Inventory                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ #: A                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Report dedup                                                 │
     │ File / structure: loop.py _last_report_signature,_last_report_ts        │
     │ (in-mem                                                                 │
     │   frozenset[(fp,sev)])                                                  │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp+sev                                                  │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: process lifetime; reassert report_reassert_s=3600         │
     │ Gates: whether to post digest                                           │
     │ Failure mode: restart loses dedup → re-post; per-cycle set jitter       │
     │ Replacement on the case: case.last_reported_signature/at,               │
     │ last_reasserted_at;                                                     │
     │   report-worthiness derived from case transitions                       │
     │ Removal: Migrate (Phase 3)                                              │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: B                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Investigation cooldown                                       │
     │ File / structure: investigations.json {fp:ts}                           │
     │   (_recent_investigation_fps/_record_investigations)                    │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp                                                      │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: investigation_cooldown_s=21600                            │
     │ Gates: skip re-investigation                                            │
     │ Failure mode: file loss → re-investigate; not case-aware                │
     │ Replacement on the case: case.last_investigated_at +                    │
     │ diagnosis_signature +                                                   │
     │   reinvestigate_after                                                   │
     │ Removal: Migrate→remove (Phase 4)                                       │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: C                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Handoff idempotency                                          │
     │ File / structure: handoff.py GitHub search for body marker              │
     │   proactive-fingerprint:{fp} + label loop:candidate                     │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp (in issue body)                                      │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: GitHub lifetime                                           │
     │ Gates: create vs refresh issue                                          │
     │ Failure mode: GitHub search miss/rate-limit → dup issue; no local       │
     │ record                                                                  │
     │ Replacement on the case: case.issue_url/issue_id/handoff_status; marker │
     │ search                                                                  │
     │   demoted to fallback                                                   │
     │ Removal: Migrate→fallback (Phase 5)                                     │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: D                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Suppression                                                  │
     │ File / structure: suppressions.json via SuppressionStore                │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp prefix                                               │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: expires_at (timed) or until-resolved                      │
     │ Gates: drop from digest+investigation                                   │
     │ Failure mode: file is the only record; not on case; prefix matching     │
     │ Replacement on the case:                                                │
     │ case.suppressed_until/snoozed_until/suppression_source/reason           │
     │   + suppression events                                                  │
     │ Removal: Migrate→fallback (Phase 6)                                     │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: E                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Resolve carry-forward (#31)                                  │
     │ File / structure: loop.py _last_deep_hotspots,_last_effective (in-mem   │
     │ lists)                                                                  │
     │ Keying: rule_id / hotspot fp                                            │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: process lifetime                                          │
     │ Gates: merge deep/degraded scans; block false all-clear                 │
     │ Failure mode: restart loses carry → transient false all-clear window    │
     │ Replacement on the case: case.last_evaluated_at vs last_observed_clean; │
     │ absence                                                                 │
     │   never resolves                                                        │
     │ Removal: Replace by observation events (Phase 2); keep in-mem as        │
     │   belt-and-braces until Phase 2 lands                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Additional state discovered (not in the "five"):                        │
     │ - app/proactive/ledger.py daily budget JSON — keep (cost control), but  │
     │ mirror into Postgres for replay.                                        │
     │ - IncidentMemory Redis keys / _LocalIncidentMemory — the durable case   │
     │ store itself; becomes Postgres (D3).                                    │
     │ - app/graph/checkpointing.py LangGraph saver (Redis/in-mem) — becomes   │
     │ Postgres saver (D3).                                                    │
     │ - app/golden_state.py + app/prompts/golden_state_manifest.json — static │
     │ intended-state context (orthogonal; manifest_hash already recorded).    │
     │ - ProactiveMemory lessons/proposals/observations/journal — learning     │
     │ flywheel (keep; bridge to knowledge).                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 3. Proposed Case State Model                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Approach: keep the existing reactive case shape and extend it;          │
     │ introduce a kind discriminator so atomic and meta cases are one durable │
     │ family. Persist in Postgres (D3). Map to existing fields wherever they  │
     │ exist (do not duplicate). Introduce typed models in                     │
     │ app/incident_memory.py (or a new app/cases/models.py) but keep dict     │
     │ round-tripping for back-compat during migration.                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ AtomicCase (extends today's _new_case dict)                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Identity (exists): incident_id, case_number, fingerprint, identity,   │
     │ resource_id, title. Add: kind="atomic", origin∈{reactive,proactive},    │
     │ rule_id, detector (proactive rule_id/reactive alertname),               │
     │ customer/site/service (best-effort from labels/topology).               │
     │ - Observation state (add): first_seen(=created_at),                     │
     │ last_seen(=last_event_at), last_observed_unhealthy,                     │
     │ last_observed_clean, last_evaluated_at, last_scan_cycle_id,             │
     │ signal_snapshot(evidence dict), signal_signature(hash of evidence),     │
     │ prev_signal_signature, severity. Absence of evaluation must never set   │
     │ last_observed_clean.                                                    │
     │ - Lifecycle (exists): status, created_at/opened_at, updated_at,         │
     │ recovered_at, plus add resolved_at, closed_at, resolution_reason.       │
     │ - Reporting (add): last_reported_at, last_reported_signature,           │
     │ last_reasserted_at, child_reports_suppressed_count; history via case    │
     │ events.                                                                 │
     │ - Investigation (add): last_investigated_at, last_diagnosis,            │
     │ diagnosis_signature, recommendations, investigation_status,             │
     │ investigation_error, reinvestigate_after, prior_diagnosis_refs,         │
     │ covered_by_meta_case(bool).                                             │
     │ - Handoff (add): issue_url, issue_id, handoff_status, last_handoff_at.  │
     │ - Suppression (add): acknowledged_by, acknowledged_at, snoozed_until,   │
     │ suppressed_until, suppression_reason,                                   │
     │ suppression_source∈{operator,agent}.                                    │
     │ - Learning (add): trace_ids[], feedback_ids[], eval_case_ids[],         │
     │ lesson_ids[], knowledge_citations[] (each: doc_path, doc_id,            │
     │ review_status, section, repo_revision, export_version),                 │
     │ candidate_knowledge_update_ids[], model_chain, prompt_version,          │
     │ policy_version, ruleset_version, tool_version, token_cost,              │
     │ operator_outcome_label, post_resolution_outcome.                        │
     │ - Relationship (exists+extend): downstream_victims, linked_parent_case  │
     │ → reused; add meta_case_id (zero or one active meta-case).              │
     │ - History/schema: append-only case events (exists, case_events); add    │
     │ schema_version.                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ MetaCase (new kind="meta")                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Identity: meta_case_id, event_fingerprint, title, summary,            │
     │ suspected_primary_entity, suspected_site/customer/service,              │
     │ event_type∈{router_down,link_failure,routing_reconvergence,monitoring_f │
     │ ailure,power_event,unknown}.                                            │
     │ - Scope: child_case_ids[] (reuse downstream_victims machinery),         │
     │ notification_ids[], observation_ids[],                                  │
     │ affected_entities/sites/customers/interfaces[], blast_radius_summary.   │
     │ - Correlation: correlation_reason, correlation_confidence,              │
     │ correlation_features[], root_cause_hypothesis, supporting_evidence[],   │
     │ disconfirming_evidence[], manually_attached_by/detached_by,             │
     │ split_from_meta_case_id, merged_into_meta_case_id.                      │
     │ - Lifecycle: status (see §4), opened_at, first_notification_at,         │
     │ last_notification_at, last_child_update_at, stabilized_at, resolved_at, │
     │ closed_at, resolution_reason.                                           │
     │ - Storm: notification_count, child_case_count, peak_rate,               │
     │ storm_started_at, storm_last_seen_at, storm_quiet_since,                │
     │ stabilization_window_until.                                             │
     │ - Investigation/Reporting/Handoff/Learning: event-level mirrors of the  │
     │ atomic fields (event_level_diagnosis, recommended_event_level_action,   │
     │ last_event_reported_at/signature, issue_url/issue_id,                   │
     │ child_issue_urls[], relevant_knowledge_citations[], storm_pattern_id,   │
     │ candidate_knowledge_update_ids[], final_root_cause_label,               │
     │ final_correlation_quality_label).                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 4. Proposed State Machine                                               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Atomic case (reconcile with existing statuses; do not invent a parallel │
     │ enum)                                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Keep investigating → waiting_approval → recovered_pending → resolved,   │
     │ plus expired, linked, and add acknowledged/snoozed as suppression       │
     │ attributes (not lifecycle status) and handed_off as a handoff_status    │
     │ attribute. Key transitions:                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Trigger: Unhealthy observation                                          │
     │ Evidence: rule evaluated unhealthy                                      │
     │ Case writes: last_observed_unhealthy, signal_snapshot/signature,        │
     │ severity; open                                                          │
     │   if new                                                                │
     │ Event: case_observed_unhealthy                                          │
     │ Report?: on open / sev / signature change                               │
     │ Investigate?: yes (if gate)                                             │
     │ Handoff?: if warrants_change                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Clean observation                                              │
     │ Evidence: rule evaluated clean                                          │
     │ Case writes: last_observed_clean, last_evaluated_at                     │
     │ Event: case_observed_clean                                              │
     │ Report?: on transition                                                  │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Skipped rule / no observation                                  │
     │ Evidence: rule not evaluated                                            │
     │ Case writes: last_scan_cycle_id only (optional                          │
     │ case_not_observed_this_cycle) —                                         │
     │   never touch lifecycle                                                 │
     │ Event: low-noise                                                        │
     │ Report?: no                                                             │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: optional                                                        │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Signal changed                                                 │
     │ Evidence: signal_signature≠prev                                         │
     │ Case writes: update snapshot/sev                                        │
     │ Event: case_signal_changed                                              │
     │ Report?: yes                                                            │
     │ Investigate?: re-eligible                                               │
     │ Handoff?: maybe                                                         │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Stale diagnosis                                                │
     │ Evidence: now>reinvestigate_after                                       │
     │ Case writes: —                                                          │
     │ Event: —                                                                │
     │ Report?: no                                                             │
     │ Investigate?: re-eligible                                               │
     │ Handoff?: —                                                             │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Operator ack/snooze/close                                      │
     │ Evidence: operator action                                               │
     │ Case writes: suppression fields / closed_at                             │
     │ Event: case_snoozed/case_closed                                         │
     │ Report?: confirm                                                        │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes (+feedback)                                                 │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Issue created / exists                                         │
     │ Evidence: handoff result                                                │
     │ Case writes: issue_url/issue_id / no-op                                 │
     │ Event: handoff_created_issue / handoff_skipped_existing_issue           │
     │ Report?: maybe                                                          │
     │ Investigate?: —                                                         │
     │ Handoff?: idempotent                                                    │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Suppression expiry                                             │
     │ Evidence: now>suppressed_until                                          │
     │ Case writes: clear fields                                               │
     │ Event: case_suppression_expired                                         │
     │ Report?: re-eligible                                                    │
     │ Investigate?: re-eligible                                               │
     │ Handoff?: —                                                             │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Reassert TTL                                                   │
     │ Evidence: now-last_reported_at≥report_reassert_s                        │
     │ Case writes: last_reasserted_at                                         │
     │ Event: case_reasserted                                                  │
     │ Report?: yes                                                            │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Investigation skipped (same signature)                         │
     │ Evidence: recent diagnosis + unchanged                                  │
     │ Case writes: prior_diagnosis_refs                                       │
     │ Event: investigation_skipped_recent_same_signature                      │
     │ Report?: no                                                             │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Resolve (positive clean)                                       │
     │ Evidence: clean observation + (recovery cooldown)                       │
     │ Case writes: resolved_at, resolution_reason                             │
     │ Event: case_resolved_positive_clean                                     │
     │ Report?: once                                                           │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: close issue                                                   │
     │ Trace?: yes → lesson candidate                                          │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: False positive / false all-clear                               │
     │ Evidence: operator label                                                │
     │ Case writes: operator_outcome_label                                     │
     │ Event: operator_feedback_recorded                                       │
     │ Report?: maybe                                                          │
     │ Investigate?: —                                                         │
     │ Handoff?: —                                                             │
     │ Trace?: yes → eval + candidate                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Invariant (subsumes #31): resolve requires positive clean observation   │
     │ (proactive) or recovery event + RECOVERY_COOLDOWN_SECONDS (reactive) or │
     │ operator close or an explicit, named stale policy. Absence from a scan  │
     │ set, a skipped deep rule, or a degraded scan must not resolve or        │
     │ all-clear.                                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Meta-case states                                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ candidate_event → active_event → investigating_event →                  │
     │ monitoring_recovery → stabilized → resolved → closed, plus split /      │
     │ merged. Transitions per the prompt; enforced rules: (a) active_event    │
     │ only when correlation confidence ≥ threshold or operator-confirmed; (b) │
     │ monitoring_recovery → stabilized only after all required positive       │
     │ clean observations or a stability window with no recurrence; (c) a      │
     │ meta-case must not resolve merely because notifications stopped — root  │
     │ child stays active while the asset is down; (d) child cases may resolve │
     │ individually while the meta-case persists.                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 5. Stage-by-Stage Refactor Plan                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Observe / scan — loop.py:run_once after scan: for each hotspot          │
     │ resolve→get_or_open_case(hotspot) (new                                  │
     │ app/proactive/case_grounding.py), then record an observation event on   │
     │ the case (unhealthy/clean), updating last_observed_*, signal_signature. │
     │ Rules not scanned this cycle are simply not touched. This replaces      │
     │ _merge_with_carried's in-memory carry (E): a deep rule not scanned has  │
     │ no fresh clean observation, so its case stays active by construction.   │
     │ Observation events are the replay/eval substrate (§9).                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Rank / gate — governance.evaluate_gate takes cases (status/severity/sig │
     │ nal_signature/suppression/handoff/reinvestigate_after) instead of raw   │
     │ hotspots; suppressed/handed-off/recently-diagnosed cases drop out of    │
     │ eligible without losing visibility. Inject relevant hyrule-knowledge    │
     │ (§6) and ProactiveMemory pattern matches as advisory ranking inputs     │
     │ (never overriding case truth). Emit a gate trace per decision.          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Investigate — loop.py:_investigate consults the case first: skip when   │
     │ last_investigated_at recent and diagnosis_signature==signal_signature   │
     │ (replaces B/investigations.json), recording                             │
     │ investigation_skipped_recent_same_signature with the reused diagnosis   │
     │ ref. Re-investigate on signal/severity/topology change, stale           │
     │ diagnosis, operator request, or prior failure. Investigation context is │
     │ seeded with prior diagnosis/recommendations + retrieved knowledge       │
     │ citations (§6); output is structured (root cause, confidence,           │
     │ supporting/disconfirming evidence, citations, recommended actions,      │
     │ escalation, unresolved questions, model/prompt/policy versions, token   │
     │ cost) and appended to the case.                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Report — replace _report_decision signature math (A) with               │
     │ case-transition detection: report on open/sev/status/material-signal    │
     │ change, reassert-TTL, resolution, handoff/suppression update, or        │
     │ learning-driven recommendation change. last_reported_* live on the      │
     │ case. Each report links the case state, signals, reused diagnosis,      │
     │ knowledge citations, and model/prompt/policy versions to a trace;       │
     │ operator accept/ignore/correct/reject attaches back as feedback.        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Handoff — handoff.py:ensure_candidate_issue checks                      │
     │ case.issue_url/issue_id first (C): present → comment/skip per policy;   │
     │ absent + conditions met → create, then atomically store                 │
     │ issue_url/issue_id on the case + append handoff_created_issue. The body │
     │ marker search remains a safety fallback only. Handoff outcomes          │
     │ (accepted/closed-dup/edited/re-severitied/routed) become eval signal.   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Snooze / ack / suppress — SuppressionStore becomes a thin adapter over  │
     │ case suppression fields/events (D); operator vs agent via               │
     │ suppression_source; TTL via suppressed_until/snoozed_until; expiry      │
     │ evaluated from the case (no side-store cleanup). _auto_snooze writes    │
     │ agent suppression onto the case. Reasons feed candidate                 │
     │ known-benign/maintenance knowledge.                                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Resolve — proactive resolution now flows through the same               │
     │ recovered_pending→resolved machinery the reactive path uses             │
     │ (incident_memory.py:_expire_*_cases), gated on a positive clean         │
     │ observation; expired (idle) stays distinct from resolved. Resolution    │
     │ emits a structured outcome → lesson candidate (§6).                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Knowledge extraction — on resolve/operator-confirm,                     │
     │ app/knowledge/promotion.py builds a learning_ledger_v1 candidate        │
     │ (event_type lesson_candidate or noc_shadow_eval_summary, producer       │
     │ noc_shadow, status proposed, authority A4) from the case + traces,      │
     │ written to a sanitized outbox for review-gated import into              │
     │ knowledge/ledger/proposed/ (§6). Never auto-promoted.                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 6. hyrule-knowledge Integration Plan                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Repository shape (confirmed). OKF Markdown+frontmatter (okf/); exports  │
     │ exports/knowledge.sqlite (tables concepts, concept_fts FTS5,            │
     │ source_refs(repo,path,commit_sha,url), claims, context_packs,           │
     │ learning_events, …) + *.jsonl + manifest.json                           │
     │ (retrieval_version=retrieval_v1, policy_version=knowledge_policy_v1,    │
     │ run_id, source_shas); policy knowledge-policy.yml; ledger lifecycle +   │
     │ promotion.py; CI opens review-gated PRs.                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Retrieval bridge (export-authoritative + replayable, D4). New           │
     │ app/knowledge/retrieval.py in noc-agent:                                │
     │ - Pin a knowledge export at a known revision: vendor/sync               │
     │ knowledge.sqlite (+ manifest.json) to a path the agent reads read-only; │
     │ record export_version = manifest.run_id + knowledge git commit. A       │
     │ small app/knowledge/sync.py (or CI artifact) refreshes the pin          │
     │ deliberately.                                                           │
     │ - Query concepts/concept_fts/source_refs scoped by case context         │
     │ (fingerprint, rule_id, resource/site/customer, vendor/platform,         │
     │ symptoms, signal_signature, topology, issue labels). Return candidates  │
     │ with doc_path(concepts.path), doc_id(concepts.id), review_status,       │
     │ authority, source_refs.commit_sha, FTS score. Filter to                 │
     │ approved/authoritative tiers; mark deprecated/stale as                  │
     │ non-authoritative.                                                      │
     │ - Cite in every trace: doc_path, doc_id, review_status, section,        │
     │ repo_revision, export_version. Production decisions + replay/evals are  │
     │ reproducible from the pin alone.                                        │
     │ - Optional enrichment: add the knowledge MCP server as a noc MCP source │
     │ (a new read-only noc role in knowledge-policy.yml, modeled on           │
     │ noc_shadow) for richer context_pack.generate/resolve. If MCP is         │
     │ unavailable, only optional enrichment degrades — never core behavior.   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Promotion bridge (review-gated). app/knowledge/promotion.py emits       │
     │ learning_ledger_v1 events (validated against                            │
     │ knowledge/schema/learning-event.schema.json; forbidden data classes     │
     │ screened:                                                               │
     │ secret/credential/raw_log/packet_capture/command_output/live_trace)     │
     │ carrying case ids, sanitized timeline, suspected/final root cause,      │
     │ blast radius, what was symptom vs action, stabilization window,         │
     │ counterexamples, operator feedback, confidence, source citations. Flow: │
     │ resolved/confirmed case → sanitized event → knowledge/ledger/proposed/  │
     │ → human ledger --review / promote-pr → okf/curated/{lessons,summaries}  │
     │ (A1/A2). Statuses live in frontmatter + learning-event metadata         │
     │ (existing convention) — no new metadata scheme.                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Safety / model sovereignty. Unreviewed events stay A4 and are never     │
     │ retrieved as authoritative; promotion is PR-gated; retrieval and        │
     │ citation are model-agnostic and reproducible from the pinned export, so │
     │ a model swap keeps identical institutional inputs.                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 7. Migration Plan                                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 1. Stand up Postgres (net-new). Add app/db/{engine,models}.py (async    │
     │ SQLAlchemy 2.0 + asyncpg), alembic/ migrations, DATABASE_URL/NOC_PG_*   │
     │ config in app/config.py. Tables: cases (atomic+meta via kind),          │
     │ case_events, observations, handoffs, suppressions, feedback, traces,    │
     │ knowledge_citations, plus LangGraph checkpoint tables                   │
     │ (langgraph-checkpoint-postgres).                                        │
     │ 2. Add a Postgres IncidentMemory backend. Introduce a CaseStore         │
     │ protocol; implement PostgresIncidentMemory (authoritative) alongside    │
     │ existing local/Redis. IncidentMemory becomes a facade selecting backend │
     │ by config; no production path depends on Redis. One-shot importer       │
     │ backfills any open Redis/in-mem cases on first boot.                    │
     │ 3. Postgres LangGraph checkpointer. Extend                              │
     │ app/graph/checkpointing.py:build_checkpointer to prefer a Postgres      │
     │ saver (DATABASE_URL), Redis/in-mem only as fallback.                    │
     │ 4. Fold side stores (transitional dual-read). New writes go to case     │
     │ state; old investigations.json/suppressions.json/in-mem signatures are  │
     │ read as fallback until Phases 3–6 land, then removed. Handoff issue_url │
     │ backfilled by one marker-search per open proactive case.                │
     │ 5. Classify ProactiveMemory entries: operational state (none) /         │
     │ candidate lesson (proposals/ → ledger candidates) / durable knowledge   │
     │ (validated lessons → OKF promotion) / stale-noisy (drop). No bulk write │
     │ to approved knowledge.                                                  │
     │ 6. Schema versioning: schema_version on every case; lazy upgrade on     │
     │ load; alembic for DB. Keep back-compat dict round-trip through the      │
     │ transition.                                                             │

     │ 8. Testing Plan                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Add/extend under hyrule-noc-agent/tests/ (mirroring                     │
     │ test_proactive_loop.py, test_incident_memory*,                          │
     │ test_proactive_suppressions.py, test_proactive_handoff.py,              │
     │ test_proactive_investigate.py, test_knowledge_shadow.py):               │
     │ - False all-clear prevention: case exists; next cycle skips/degrades    │
     │ the rule → case stays active; no resolve/all-clear (regression-locks    │
     │ #31 at the case level).                                                 │
     │ - Positive clean resolve: rule evaluated clean → resolves once; one     │
     │ resolve report.                                                         │
     │ - Report dedup / reassert: stable unhealthy state → one report then     │
     │ reassert only after TTL; per-cycle jitter posts nothing.                │
     │ - Signal change: material signal change flips report/investigation      │
     │ eligibility.                                                            │
     │ - Investigation reuse: same signal_signature+recent → skip with reused  │
     │ diagnosis; changed → reinvestigate with prior diagnosis in context.     │
     │ - Handoff idempotency: issue_url present → never duplicates; absent →   │
     │ creates+stores; partial-failure retry safe.                             │
     │ - Snooze/ack TTL: snoozed until TTL; expiry restores visibility;        │
     │ operator ack survives scan jitter; repeated benign snooze → candidate   │
     │ lesson.                                                                 │
     │ - Meta-case suite: router-down cascade (one meta-case, children         │
     │ attached, one report, one issue); self-healing reconvergence            │
     │ (→monitoring_recovery/stabilized, root stays active, resolve only on    │
     │ clean); unrelated simultaneous alerts (no false grouping); operator     │
     │ split/merge captured as feedback+eval; existing child issue linked, no  │
     │ dup.                                                                    │
     │ - Knowledge retrieval: matching case retrieves approved doc; deprecated │
     │ not authoritative; trace cites                                          │
     │ path/id/status/section/revision/export_version; stable across model     │
     │ adapters; reproducible from pinned export with MCP down.                │
     │ - Knowledge candidate: resolved meta-case emits A4 candidate with       │
     │ case/trace ids, timeline, blast radius, counterexamples; not approved   │
     │ without review; rejected not retrieved.                                 │
     │ - Migration: old JSON side stores read as fallback; existing cases      │
     │ readable; ProactiveMemory not blind-promoted; knowledge export          │
     │ indexed/read without mutation.                                          │
     │ - Postgres backend: CRUD + concurrency/atomicity (intake lock           │
     │ equivalent), no-Redis run is fully durable.                             │
     │ - No sixth memory: assert no new ad-hoc anti-dup file is introduced.    │
     │ - Model-swap: same case state + same pinned knowledge + same policy →   │
     │ acceptable behavior under an alternate model_chain.                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │

     │ a candidate policy/model/prompt/toolchain → compare                     │
     │ decisions/non-decisions/report/handoff/resolve and cost against         │
     │ expected. Build fixtures from real case_events + traces (sanitized).    │
     │ Metrics: false all-clear rate, duplicate report/handoff rate,           │
     │ investigation-reuse accuracy, correct reinvestigation on change,        │
     │ knowledge-use correctness, severity/blast accuracy, storm detection     │

     │ RL training in this refactor. Cross-check against the knowledge repo's  │

     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 12. Risks and Open Questions                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Postgres is net-new in noc-agent (only                                │
     │ redis/langgraph-checkpoint-redis exist today). Phase 1 is the largest   │
     │ and gates everything; needs DB provisioning on the NOC VM and an        │
     │ async-SQLAlchemy concurrency model replicating the current Redis        │
     │ noc:intake:lock atomicity (incident_memory.py:_intake_alert_redis).     │
     │ - Fingerprint duality. Proactive hotspot fp vs alert-identity case fp;  │
     │ grounding must define one durable mapping (extend                       │
     │ hotspot_to_alert_payload/_case_for_hotspot) so side-store keys and case │
     │ keys finally coincide.                                                  │
     │ - Ephemeral→durable shift. Today cases TTL out (CASE_HISTORY_SECONDS);  │
     │ Postgres makes them durable — define explicit retention/close policy so │
     │ expired vs resolved stays meaningful and tables don't grow unbounded.   │
     │ - Storm correlation precision. Topology data comes from                 │
     │ infra:parent:*/topology_parents; sparse topology risks mis-grouping →   │
     │ keep confidence thresholds + operator split/merge as first-class        │
     │ corrections.                                                            │
     │ - Knowledge pin freshness. Export-authoritative retrieval can serve     │
     │ stale knowledge; surface export_version/repo_revision in traces and add │
     │ a staleness warning + deliberate refresh.                               │
     │ - Sensitive-data leakage into candidates — enforce                      │
     │ learning-event.schema.json data-class screening + redaction before any  │
     │ ledger write; promotion stays human-gated.                              │
     │ - Scope. Sections 8–11 of the prompt (meta-cases) are large; Phases     │
     │ 8–12 may each split further. Confirm whether meta-cases must ship this  │
     │ cycle or can trail the operational consolidation.                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 13. Acceptance Criteria                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - IncidentMemory cases (Postgres-backed) are authoritative for active   │
     │ concerns; a missed/skipped/degraded scan never causes false all-clear;  │
     │ resolve only on positive clean / recovery / operator close / explicit   │
     │ stale policy.                                                           │
     │ - Duplicate reports prevented by case state; reassertions               │
     │ case-grounded; investigations skipped on recent same-signature          │
     │ diagnosis and reinvestigations include prior context.                   │
     │ - Handoff never duplicates when issue_url/issue_id exists;              │
     │ snooze/ack/suppression live on the case with TTL semantics.             │
     │ - The five side stores are removed or reduced to temporary fallbacks;   │
     │ no new anti-dup mechanism introduced; no production behavior depends on │
     │ Redis as a second source of truth.                                      │
     │ - Case events + decision traces are replay/eval-ready; operator         │
     │ feedback attaches to case+trace ids.                                    │
     │ - Notification storms produce one durable meta-case (first-class        │
     │ IncidentMemory record) with linked children; self-healing handled       │
     │ without premature all-clear; operators can                              │
     │ merge/split/attach/detach/confirm/reject and those corrections become   │
     │ learning signal.                                                        │
     │ - hyrule-knowledge is retrieved during                                  │
     │ correlation/investigation/report/handoff from a pinned export, cited in │
     │ traces with path/id/status/section/revision/export_version,             │
     │ reproducible with MCP unavailable; resolved/confirmed cases yield       │
     │ review-gated OKF/learning_ledger_v1 candidates; approved knowledge      │
     │ survives a model swap.                                                  │
     │ - Tests cover scan jitter, clean resolve, dedup, investigation reuse,   │
     │ handoff idempotency, suppression TTL, migration, Postgres durability,   │
     │ storms, knowledge retrieval+candidates, and model-swap.                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ Verification (how to test end-to-end)                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Unit/integration: cd /home/svag/Dev/hyrule-noc-agent && uv run pytest │
     │ (focused: tests/test_proactive_loop.py,                                 │

● Good correction — that's a real layering fix. My draft leaned too much logic
  into ProactiveLoop and implied the graph would touch case state. The
  authoritative state machine must be a shared CaseService/CorrelationService
  that both the proactive scan path and the reactive webhook path call; the loop
  becomes a scheduler and the LangGraph graph an investigation
  consumer/producer that never writes case truth. Let me revise the plan
  accordingly.
