     ╭─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
     │ Case-Grounded Self-Learning Loop Refactor Plan                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Context                                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Why this change. The NOC Agent's proactive loop                         │
     │ (hyrule-noc-agent/app/proactive/loop.py) re-derives state every cycle   │
     │ (scan → rank → gate → investigate → report → handoff/resolve) and has   │
     │ accreted five separate anti-duplication side stores to stop flapping,   │
     │ duplicate reports, duplicate tickets, and false all-clears. None of     │
     │ them share one notion of "the current state of a concern," and —        │
     │ critically — they are keyed by hotspot fingerprint                      │
     │ (sha256(rule_id|key)[:16], models.py:Hotspot.fingerprint) while the     │
     │ durable case is keyed by alert-identity fingerprint                     │
     │ (incident_memory.py:fingerprint_alert). The proactive loop therefore    │
     │ makes its don't-duplicate decisions outside the case.                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Meanwhile the reactive path already has the state machine we want:      │
     │ IncidentMemory (app/incident_memory.py) keeps durable cases with a real │
     │ lifecycle, parent↔child topology linking, and                           │
     │ resolve-only-on-positive-recovery semantics. The refactor's thesis —    │
     │ the case is the authoritative state machine — is already half-true; we  │
     │ must extend the case to own the proactive stages too, add meta-cases    │
     │ for notification storms, and wire a replayable, governed                │
     │ hyrule-knowledge learning loop so institutional NOC judgment survives a │
     │ model swap.                                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Targets (confirmed cross-repo). This plan is implemented against:       │
     │ - /home/svag/Dev/hyrule-noc-agent (remote AS215932/noc-agent) — the     │
     │ loop, cases, side stores.                                               │
     │ - /home/svag/Dev/knowledge (remote AS215932/knowledge) — the            │
     │ institutional repo the prompt calls "hyrule-knowledge".                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Confirmed decisions shaping this plan:                                  │
     │ 1. Proceed cross-repo now; this plan file stays in the current project. │
     │ 2. Sequence: preserve #31 → operational consolidation (5 side stores    │
     │ onto the case) → meta-cases/storms → knowledge loop.                    │
     │ 3. Postgres is the authoritative production backend for IncidentMemory, │
     │ meta-cases, observations, case events, handoffs, suppressions,          │
     │ feedback, trace references, and LangGraph checkpoints. Redis/Valkey is  │
     │ optional hot-path only (queues, pub/sub, short-lived dedup/rate-limit   │
     │ windows, storm correlation). No production behavior may silently depend │
     │ on Redis as a second source of truth.                                   │
     │ 4. Knowledge retrieval is export-authoritative + replayable: production │
     │ correlation/investigation reads a pinned deterministic SQLite/JSONL     │
     │ export of hyrule-knowledge; the knowledge MCP server is optional        │
     │ noc-role enrichment only. Every trace records the exact document path,  │
     │ document id, approval status, section, and repo revision / export       │
     │ version used.                                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Architectural principle (ownership). The ProactiveLoop is demoted to a  │
     │ scheduler/orchestrator — it paces cycles, runs scanners, and executes   │
     │ side effects, but owns no durable case lifecycle. The authoritative     │
     │ state machine lives in a shared case/correlation service layer          │
     │ (CaseService/CorrelationService over a CaseStore) used identically by   │
     │ proactive scan observations and reactive webhook alerts, so there is    │
     │ one notion of a concern. LangGraph investigation is a consumer of       │
     │ case/meta-case/knowledge context and a producer of structured           │
     │ investigation results — it must not own case status, suppression,       │
     │ handoff, resolve, reporting dedup, or correlation truth. Do not bury    │
     │ any of that in the loop or the graph.                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Discrepancies vs. the original prompt (repo wins):                      │
     │ - OKF, not ODF. hyrule-knowledge stores Markdown + YAML frontmatter     │
     │ with deterministic JSONL/SQLite exports (knowledge/okf/,                │
     │ knowledge/exports/knowledge.sqlite). There are no .odt/.ods/.fodt       │
     │ files. "Candidate ODF artifact" → OKF concept + learning_ledger_v1 JSON │
     │ event.                                                                  │
     │ - Cases are not on-disk files. NOC-20260617-006 is a case_number        │
     │ display string; cases live in Redis (prod today) or in-memory           │
     │ (dev/test). We are moving authority to Postgres.                        │
     │ - #31 is already merged to main (234a92d, ee55528). We preserve it, not │
     │ re-merge it. The reactive path already embodies its principle (resolve  │
     │ only on positive recovery + cooldown).                                  │
     │ - No meta-cases exist today — but parent/child linking +                │
     │ IncidentMemory.correlate() are the seed.                                │
     │ - ProactiveMemory is already non-authoritative                          │
     │ (lessons/proposals/observations/journal) — it does not need demoting,   │
     │ only wiring into the knowledge promotion bridge.                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ Architecture Invariants                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Hard rules every PR and test must enforce (mirrored in §8 boundary      │
     │ tests and §13 acceptance):                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - ProactiveLoop may orchestrate cycles, run scanners, call services,    │
     │ and do scheduled work — it must not own durable case lifecycle state.   │
     │ - LangGraph may investigate and return structured InvestigationResult   │
     │ objects — it must not mutate case status, suppression, handoff,         │
     │ resolve, report-dedup, or correlation truth.                            │
     │ - Reporters may render/send notifications only from CaseService report  │
     │ intents (via the outbox).                                               │
     │ - Handoff code may create/update external issues only from CaseService  │
     │ handoff intents (via the outbox).                                       │
     │ - CaseService is the only owner of atomic case lifecycle state.         │
     │ - CorrelationService is the only owner of meta-case grouping,           │
     │ attach/detach, merge/split, and storm lifecycle state.                  │
     │ - CaseStore/Postgres is the authoritative production state store.       │
     │ - Any Redis/Valkey use is optional and transient only (hot-path         │
     │ cache/queue/dedup-window) — never a second source of truth.             │
     │ - No new JSON/file/local-cache side store may become an                 │
     │ anti-duplication mechanism.                                             │
     │                                                                         │

     │ 2. Existing Side-Store Inventory                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ #: A                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Report dedup                                                 │
     │ File / structure: loop.py _last_report_signature,_last_report_ts        │
     │ (in-mem                                                                 │
     │   frozenset[(fp,sev)])                                                  │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp+sev                                                  │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: process lifetime; reassert report_reassert_s=3600         │
     │ Gates: whether to post digest                                           │
