     │ Replacement on the case: case.last_reported_signature/at,               │
     │ last_reasserted_at;                                                     │
     │   report-worthiness derived from case transitions                       │
     │ Removal: Migrate (Phase 3)                                              │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: B                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Investigation cooldown                                       │
     │ File / structure: investigations.json {fp:ts}                           │
     │   (_recent_investigation_fps/_record_investigations)                    │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp                                                      │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: investigation_cooldown_s=21600                            │
     │ Gates: skip re-investigation                                            │
     │ Failure mode: file loss → re-investigate; not case-aware                │
     │ Replacement on the case: case.last_investigated_at +                    │
     │ diagnosis_signature +                                                   │
     │   reinvestigate_after                                                   │
     │ Removal: Migrate→remove (Phase 4)                                       │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: C                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Handoff idempotency                                          │
     │ File / structure: handoff.py GitHub search for body marker              │
     │   proactive-fingerprint:{fp} + label loop:candidate                     │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp (in issue body)                                      │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: GitHub lifetime                                           │
     │ Gates: create vs refresh issue                                          │
     │ Failure mode: GitHub search miss/rate-limit → dup issue; no local       │
     │ record                                                                  │
     │ Replacement on the case: case.issue_url/issue_id/handoff_status; marker │
     │ search                                                                  │
     │   demoted to fallback                                                   │
     │ Removal: Migrate→fallback (Phase 5)                                     │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: D                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Suppression                                                  │
     │ File / structure: suppressions.json via SuppressionStore                │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp prefix                                               │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: expires_at (timed) or until-resolved                      │
     │ Gates: drop from digest+investigation                                   │
     │ Failure mode: file is the only record; not on case; prefix matching     │
     │ Replacement on the case:                                                │
     │ case.suppressed_until/snoozed_until/suppression_source/reason           │
     │   + suppression events                                                  │
     │ Removal: Migrate→fallback (Phase 6)                                     │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: E                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Resolve carry-forward (#31)                                  │
     │ File / structure: loop.py _last_deep_hotspots,_last_effective (in-mem   │
     │ lists)                                                                  │
     │ Keying: rule_id / hotspot fp                                            │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: process lifetime                                          │
     │ Gates: merge deep/degraded scans; block false all-clear                 │
     │ Failure mode: restart loses carry → transient false all-clear window    │
     │ Replacement on the case: case.last_evaluated_at vs last_observed_clean; │
     │ absence                                                                 │
     │   never resolves                                                        │
     │ Removal: Replace by observation events (Phase 2); keep in-mem as        │
     │   belt-and-braces until Phase 2 lands                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Additional state discovered (not in the "five"):                        │
     │ - app/proactive/ledger.py daily budget JSON — keep (cost control), but  │
     │ mirror into Postgres for replay.                                        │
     │ - IncidentMemory Redis keys / _LocalIncidentMemory — the durable case   │
     │ store itself; becomes Postgres (D3).                                    │
     │ - app/graph/checkpointing.py LangGraph saver (Redis/in-mem) — becomes   │
     │ Postgres saver (D3).                                                    │
     │ - app/golden_state.py + app/prompts/golden_state_manifest.json — static │
     │ intended-state context (orthogonal; manifest_hash already recorded).    │
     │ - ProactiveMemory lessons/proposals/observations/journal — learning     │
     │ flywheel (keep; bridge to knowledge).                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 3. Proposed Case State Model                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Approach: keep the existing reactive case shape and extend it;          │
     │ introduce a kind discriminator so atomic and meta cases are one durable │
     │ family. Persist in Postgres (D3). Map to existing fields wherever they  │
     │ exist (do not duplicate). The model is owned by the shared CaseService  │
     │ over a CaseStore (app/cases/), not by the loop or the LangGraph graph;  │
     │ introduce typed models in app/cases/models.py and keep dict             │
     │ round-tripping for back-compat during migration.                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ AtomicCase (extends today's _new_case dict)                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Identity (exists): incident_id, case_number, fingerprint, identity,   │
     │ resource_id, title. Add: kind="atomic", origin∈{reactive,proactive},    │
     │ rule_id, detector (proactive rule_id/reactive alertname),               │
     │ customer/site/service (best-effort from labels/topology).               │
     │ - Observation state (add): first_seen(=created_at),                     │
     │ last_seen(=last_event_at), last_observed_unhealthy,                     │
     │ last_observed_clean, last_evaluated_at, last_scan_cycle_id,             │
     │ signal_snapshot(evidence dict), signal_signature(hash of evidence),     │
     │ prev_signal_signature, severity. Absence of evaluation must never set   │
     │ last_observed_clean.                                                    │
     │ - Lifecycle (exists): status, created_at/opened_at, updated_at,         │
     │ recovered_at, plus add resolved_at, closed_at, resolution_reason.       │
     │ - Reporting (add): last_reported_at, last_reported_signature,           │
     │ last_reasserted_at, child_reports_suppressed_count; history via case    │
     │ events.                                                                 │
     │ - Investigation (add): last_investigated_at, last_diagnosis,            │
     │ diagnosis_signature, recommendations, investigation_status,             │
     │ investigation_error, reinvestigate_after, prior_diagnosis_refs,         │
     │ covered_by_meta_case(bool).                                             │
     │ - Handoff (add): issue_url, issue_id, handoff_status, last_handoff_at.  │
     │ - Suppression (add): acknowledged_by, acknowledged_at, snoozed_until,   │
     │ suppressed_until, suppression_reason,                                   │
     │ suppression_source∈{operator,agent}.                                    │
     │ - Learning (add): trace_ids[], feedback_ids[], eval_case_ids[],         │
     │ lesson_ids[], knowledge_citations[] (each: doc_path, doc_id,            │
     │ review_status, section, repo_revision, export_version),                 │
     │ candidate_knowledge_update_ids[], model_chain, prompt_version,          │
     │ policy_version, ruleset_version, tool_version, token_cost,              │
     │ operator_outcome_label, post_resolution_outcome.                        │
     │ - Relationship (exists+extend): downstream_victims, linked_parent_case  │
     │ → reused; add meta_case_id (zero or one active meta-case).              │
     │ - History/schema: append-only case events (exists, case_events); add    │
     │ schema_version.                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ MetaCase (new kind="meta")                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Identity: meta_case_id, event_fingerprint, title, summary,            │
     │ suspected_primary_entity, suspected_site/customer/service,              │
     │ event_type∈{router_down,link_failure,routing_reconvergence,monitoring_f │
     │ ailure,power_event,unknown}.                                            │
     │ - Scope: child_case_ids[] (reuse downstream_victims machinery),         │
     │ notification_ids[], observation_ids[],                                  │
     │ affected_entities/sites/customers/interfaces[], blast_radius_summary.   │
     │ - Correlation: correlation_reason, correlation_confidence,              │
     │ correlation_features[], root_cause_hypothesis, supporting_evidence[],   │
     │ disconfirming_evidence[], manually_attached_by/detached_by,             │
     │ split_from_meta_case_id, merged_into_meta_case_id.                      │
     │ - Lifecycle: status (see §4), opened_at, first_notification_at,         │
     │ last_notification_at, last_child_update_at, stabilized_at, resolved_at, │
     │ closed_at, resolution_reason.                                           │
     │ - Storm: notification_count, child_case_count, peak_rate,               │
     │ storm_started_at, storm_last_seen_at, storm_quiet_since,                │
     │ stabilization_window_until.                                             │
     │ - Investigation/Reporting/Handoff/Learning: event-level mirrors of the  │
     │ atomic fields (event_level_diagnosis, recommended_event_level_action,   │
     │ last_event_reported_at/signature, issue_url/issue_id,                   │
     │ child_issue_urls[], relevant_knowledge_citations[], storm_pattern_id,   │
     │ candidate_knowledge_update_ids[], final_root_cause_label,               │
     │ final_correlation_quality_label).                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Durable substrate (Postgres tables)                                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Beyond the cases/meta_cases projections, the authoritative store        │
     │ includes an ingestion inbox, an append-only event log, an identity      │
     │ alias registry, a side-effect outbox, and correlation evidence. All     │
     │ writes for one observation happen in one transaction (§7 concurrency).  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ observation_inbox — durable landing zone for every raw webhook /        │
     │ scanner result / notification, so duplicate delivery, retries, source   │
     │ replay, and crash-before-apply are safe: inbox_id, source,              │
     │ source_event_id, source_fingerprint, dedup_key (unique), received_at,   │
     │ payload_ref (or compact raw payload), normalization_status,             │
     │ normalized_observation_id, error, schema_version.                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ observations — normalized evidence fed to CaseService: observation_id,  │
     │ source, detector (rule/check),                                          │
     │ entity/resource/interface/service/site/customer, severity,              │
     │ status∈{firing,clean,resolved,unknown}, observed_at, received_at,       │
     │ signal_snapshot, signal_signature,                                      │
     │ observation_confidence∈{high,medium,low}, scan_cycle_id?,               │
     │ source_health∈{healthy,degraded,unknown,failed}. A skipped detector     │
     │ produces no row; a clean observation must be explicit (status=clean),   │
     │ never inferred from absence.                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ case_events — append-only audit/replay truth; cases/meta_cases are      │
     │ query-optimized projections written atomically with the event:          │
     │ event_id, case_id?, meta_case_id?, event_type,                          │
     │ actor_type∈{system,operator,monitor,graph,migration,replay}, actor_id,  │
     │ source, occurred_at, observed_at, correlation_id, causation_id,         │
     │ policy_version, payload, schema_version. (No full event-sourcing        │
     │ required — but every lifecycle-relevant change appends an event, and    │
     │ replay/eval is built from case_events + observations + traces.)         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ case_identity_aliases — resolves fingerprint/identity drift so case_id  │
     │ is stable and fingerprints are matching evidence / compat aliases:      │
     │ alias_id, case_id, alias_type∈{hotspot_fp,alert_fp,source_fp,source_eve │
     │ nt_id,rule_entity,issue_marker,legacy_case_number,external_issue_id},   │
     │ alias_value, source, confidence, created_at, retired_at. Absorbs old    │
     │ investigations.json/suppressions.json keys, GitHub issue markers,       │
     │ Alertmanager/Icinga fingerprints, proactive hotspot fps, legacy case    │
     │ numbers, and future detector/rule renames.                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ side_effect_outbox (see §5) — outbox_id, intent_type∈{report,meta_repor │
     │ t,handoff,knowledge_candidate,issue_comment,discord_update}, case_id?,  │
     │ meta_case_id?, idempotency_key (unique), state_signature, payload,      │
     │ status∈{pending,in_progress,succeeded,failed,abandoned}, attempts,      │
     │ next_attempt_at, created_at, completed_at, external_id/external_url?,   │
     │ error.                                                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ meta_case_correlation_evidence (see §4) — meta_case_id,                 │
     │ observation_id?, case_id?, evidence_type, feature, value, confidence,   │
     │ source, created_at.                                                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Policy model (versioned)                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ All thresholds/TTLs are policy-driven and versioned (new                │
     │ app/cases/policy.py:CasePolicy + policy_version): report-reassert TTL,  │
     │ investigation cooldown, reinvestigate-stale window, storm correlation   │
     │ window, storm confidence threshold, stabilization window, suppression   │
     │ TTL, auto-snooze policy, handoff threshold, knowledge authority filter, │
     │ source-health confidence policy, child-suppression-under-meta-case      │
     │ policy. Every case_event and decision trace records the active          │
     │ policy_version; replay/eval compares behavior by policy_version (§9).   │
     │ This is the single versioned source that replaces the scattered         │
     │ constants in config.py:ProactiveLoopSettings.                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 4. Proposed State Machine                                               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Implemented in CaseService (over CaseStore) as the single owner of      │
     │ these transitions for both proactive scans and reactive webhooks. The   │
     │ loop, webhook ingress, and the LangGraph graph are clients that submit  │
     │ observations/results and read context — never status.                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Atomic case (reconcile with existing statuses; do not invent a parallel │
     │ enum)                                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Keep investigating → waiting_approval → recovered_pending → resolved,   │
     │ plus expired, linked, and add acknowledged/snoozed as suppression       │
     │ attributes (not lifecycle status) and handed_off as a handoff_status    │
     │ attribute. Key transitions:                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Trigger: Unhealthy observation                                          │
     │ Evidence: rule evaluated unhealthy                                      │
     │ Case writes: last_observed_unhealthy, signal_snapshot/signature,        │
     │ severity; open                                                          │
     │   if new                                                                │
     │ Event: case_observed_unhealthy                                          │
     │ Report?: on open / sev / signature change                               │
     │ Investigate?: yes (if gate)                                             │
     │ Handoff?: if warrants_change                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Clean observation                                              │
     │ Evidence: rule evaluated clean                                          │
     │ Case writes: last_observed_clean, last_evaluated_at                     │
     │ Event: case_observed_clean                                              │
     │ Report?: on transition                                                  │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Skipped rule / no observation                                  │
     │ Evidence: rule not evaluated                                            │
     │ Case writes: last_scan_cycle_id only (optional                          │
     │ case_not_observed_this_cycle) —                                         │
     │   never touch lifecycle                                                 │
     │ Event: low-noise                                                        │
     │ Report?: no                                                             │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: optional                                                        │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Signal changed                                                 │
     │ Evidence: signal_signature≠prev                                         │
     │ Case writes: update snapshot/sev                                        │
     │ Event: case_signal_changed                                              │
     │ Report?: yes                                                            │
     │ Investigate?: re-eligible                                               │
     │ Handoff?: maybe                                                         │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Stale diagnosis                                                │
     │ Evidence: now>reinvestigate_after                                       │
     │ Case writes: —                                                          │
     │ Event: —                                                                │
     │ Report?: no                                                             │
     │ Investigate?: re-eligible                                               │
     │ Handoff?: —                                                             │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Operator ack/snooze/close                                      │
     │ Evidence: operator action                                               │
     │ Case writes: suppression fields / closed_at                             │
     │ Event: case_snoozed/case_closed                                         │
     │ Report?: confirm                                                        │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes (+feedback)                                                 │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Issue created / exists                                         │
     │ Evidence: handoff result                                                │
     │ Case writes: issue_url/issue_id / no-op                                 │
     │ Event: handoff_created_issue / handoff_skipped_existing_issue           │
     │ Report?: maybe                                                          │
     │ Investigate?: —                                                         │
     │ Handoff?: idempotent                                                    │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Suppression expiry                                             │
     │ Evidence: now>suppressed_until                                          │
     │ Case writes: clear fields                                               │
     │ Event: case_suppression_expired                                         │
     │ Report?: re-eligible                                                    │
     │ Investigate?: re-eligible                                               │
     │ Handoff?: —                                                             │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Reassert TTL                                                   │
     │ Evidence: now-last_reported_at≥report_reassert_s                        │
     │ Case writes: last_reasserted_at                                         │
     │ Event: case_reasserted                                                  │
     │ Report?: yes                                                            │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Investigation skipped (same signature)                         │
     │ Evidence: recent diagnosis + unchanged                                  │
     │ Case writes: prior_diagnosis_refs                                       │
     │ Event: investigation_skipped_recent_same_signature                      │
     │ Report?: no                                                             │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Resolve (positive clean)                                       │
     │ Evidence: clean observation + (recovery cooldown)                       │
     │ Case writes: resolved_at, resolution_reason                             │
     │ Event: case_resolved_positive_clean                                     │
     │ Report?: once                                                           │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: close issue                                                   │
     │ Trace?: yes → lesson candidate                                          │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: False positive / false all-clear                               │
     │ Evidence: operator label                                                │
     │ Case writes: operator_outcome_label                                     │
     │ Event: operator_feedback_recorded                                       │
     │ Report?: maybe                                                          │
     │ Investigate?: —                                                         │
     │ Handoff?: —                                                             │
     │ Trace?: yes → eval + candidate                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Invariant (subsumes #31): resolve requires positive clean observation   │
     │ (proactive) or recovery event + RECOVERY_COOLDOWN_SECONDS (reactive) or │
     │ operator close or an explicit, named stale policy. Absence from a scan  │
     │ set, a skipped deep rule, or a degraded scan must not resolve or        │
     │ all-clear.                                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Meta-case states                                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ candidate_event → active_event → investigating_event →                  │
     │ monitoring_recovery → stabilized → resolved → closed, plus split /      │
     │ merged. Transitions per the prompt; enforced rules: (a) active_event    │
     │ only when correlation confidence ≥ threshold or operator-confirmed; (b) │
     │ monitoring_recovery → stabilized only after all required positive       │
     │ clean observations or a stability window with no recurrence; (c) a      │
     │ meta-case must not resolve merely because notifications stopped — root  │
     │ child stays active while the asset is down; (d) child cases may resolve │
     │ individually while the meta-case persists.                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Meta-case correlation (deterministic-first, LLM-second)                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ CorrelationService groups via layered evidence, each layer written to   │
     │ meta_case_correlation_evidence; the LLM is explanatory only and is      │
     │ never the sole authority for durable attach/detach:                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 1. Source-native: Alertmanager group labels, Icinga host/service        │
     │ relationships, source fingerprints, firing/clear pairs.                 │
     │ 2. Topology/dependency: same router/switch/site/customer/service,       │
     │ parent/child (topology_parents/infra:parent:*), upstream/downstream,    │
     │ interface bundle/LAG, circuit, peer, route adjacency.                   │
     │ 3. Temporal storm heuristics: burst windows, peak rate, notification    │
     │ sequence, simultaneous fire/clear patterns.                             │
     │ 4. Approved hyrule-knowledge patterns: known reconvergence windows,     │
     │ router/link/site failure runbooks, monitoring-cascade notes,            │
     │ customer/site patterns (retrieved + cited per §6).                      │
     │ 5. LLM hypothesis: grouping/root-cause proposal only; cannot by itself  │
     │ create durable attach/detach.                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Every attach records correlation_reason, correlation_confidence, and    │
     │ correlation_features.                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Child suppression under a meta-case (reversible, evidence-based)        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ An attached child may carry covered_by_meta_case=true,                  │
     │ independent_action_required=false,                                      │
     │ child_report_suppressed_reason="explained_by_meta_case". It must become │
     │ independently reportable/investigable again when any of: severity       │
     │ increases; signal materially changes; child persists after the          │
     │ meta-case stabilizes; a new customer/site/service is affected; the      │
     │ root-cause hypothesis is rejected; operator marks                       │
     │ independent_action_required; correlation confidence drops below         │
     │ threshold; the child no longer fits the meta-case evidence. (Tests per  │
     │ §8.)                                                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Source-health / monitoring-failure awareness                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Storms can come from the network or from monitoring itself.             │
     │ Observations carry source_health + observation_confidence; meta-cases   │
     │ support event_type=monitoring_failure. Rules: if                        │
     │ source_health∈{degraded,failed}, absence of alerts or sudden clears is  │
     │ not strong clean evidence and lowers auto-resolution confidence; a      │
     │ monitoring-region failure can itself open a meta-case; clean            │
     │ observations are source-aware and detector-aware. (Tests:               │
     │ monitoring-system outage; source-degraded false all-clear prevention.)  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 5. Stage-by-Stage Refactor Plan                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Layering (the spine). The authoritative state machine lives in a new    │
     │ shared case/correlation service — app/cases/service.py:CaseService and  │
     │ app/cases/correlation.py:CorrelationService, over                       │
     │ app/cases/store.py:CaseStore (Postgres). Everything else is a thin      │
     │ client:                                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Component: app/proactive/loop.py:ProactiveLoop                          │
     │ Role: Scheduler/orchestrator: paces cycles, runs scanners, executes     │
     │ side                                                                    │
     │   effects (Discord, GitHub, kick off investigation). No durable         │
     │ decision state.                                                         │
     │ Writes case truth?: No — calls CaseService                              │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Component: app/main.py:/webhook/* (reactive)                            │
     │ Role: Ingress: normalizes notifications                                 │
     │ Writes case truth?: No — calls CaseService.observe_notification         │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Component: app/graph/* (LangGraph)                                      │
     │ Role: Investigation consumer/producer: reads case+meta-case+knowledge   │
     │ context,                                                                │
     │   returns a structured InvestigationResult                              │
     │ Writes case truth?: No — results applied via                            │
     │   CaseService.record_investigation_result                               │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Component: app/cases/service.py:CaseService                             │
     │ Role: Owns lifecycle, observation truth, reporting dedup, investigation │
     │ reuse,                                                                  │
     │   suppression, handoff idempotency, resolve                             │
     │ Writes case truth?: Yes (sole owner)                                    │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Component: app/cases/correlation.py:CorrelationService                  │
     │ Role: Owns storm detection + meta-case                                  │
     │   create/attach/detach/merge/split/stabilize                            │
     │ Writes case truth?: Yes (sole owner)                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Both proactive scan observations and reactive webhook alerts enter      │
     │ through the same CaseService.observe* API and the same                  │
     │ CorrelationService — one concern, one record. The LangGraph graph never │
     │ flips case status/suppression/handoff/resolve/correlation; today's      │
     │ in-graph correlate_and_dedupe and intake-driven status transitions move │
     │ into the service. Each stage is therefore a service interaction (loop   │
     │ = caller):                                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Observe / scan — the loop scans, then writes each result to the durable │
     │ observation_inbox (idempotent on dedup_key); a normalizer produces      │
     │ observations that CaseService.observe(...) applies in one transaction   │
     │ (unhealthy/clean). A skipped rule writes no inbox row → no clean        │
     │ observation. The service maps the observation to a case, appends an     │
     │ observation event, updates last_observed_*/signal_signature, and        │
     │ decides lifecycle. This replaces the loop's _merge_with_carried carry   │
     │ (E): a deep rule not scanned has no fresh clean observation, so its     │
     │ case stays active in the service — no in-memory list, preserving #31.   │
     │ Observation events are the replay/eval substrate (§9).                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Rank / gate — governance.evaluate_gate becomes a pure function over     │
     │ CaseService.eligible(...) (status/severity/signal_signature/suppression │
     │ /handoff/reinvestigate_after); suppressed/handed-off/recently-diagnosed │
     │ cases drop out without losing visibility. Relevant hyrule-knowledge     │
     │ (§6) and ProactiveMemory patterns are advisory inputs only. The loop    │
     │ executes the budgeted subset; the service records the gate trace.       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Investigate — the loop asks CaseService.eligible_for_investigation();   │
     │ for each it runs the LangGraph graph as a consumer (seeded by the       │
     │ service with prior diagnosis + knowledge citations) and hands the       │
     │ structured result back via CaseService.record_investigation_result().   │
     │ The skip/reuse decision (recent last_investigated_at and                │
     │ diagnosis_signature==signal_signature; replaces B/investigations.json)  │
     │ and the investigation_skipped_recent_same_signature trace live in the   │
     │ service, not the loop or graph. Result schema: root cause, confidence,  │
     │ supporting/disconfirming evidence, citations, recommended actions,      │
     │ escalation, unresolved questions, model/prompt/policy versions, token   │
     │ cost.                                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Report — CaseService.report_decisions(cycle) returns report-worthy      │
     │ transitions (open/sev/status/material-signal/reassert-TTL/resolution/ha │
     │ ndoff/suppression/recommendation-change) and owns last_reported_*       │
     │ (replaces A). It enqueues a side_effect_outbox report intent            │
     │ (idempotency report:{case_id}:{state_signature}) inside the             │
     │ transaction; an outbox worker renders + sends and records the result    │
     │ via CaseService.mark_reported(...) — a crash/retry never double-posts.  │
     │ Child reports under an active meta-case are suppressed by               │
     │ CorrelationService. Each report trace links case state, signals, reused │
     │ diagnosis, knowledge citations, and versions; operator                  │
     │ accept/ignore/correct/reject attaches back as feedback.                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Handoff — CaseService.handoff_intent(case) returns create/comment/skip  │
     │ from case.issue_url/issue_id (replaces C); it enqueues a                │
     │ side_effect_outbox handoff intent (idempotency                          │
     │ handoff:{case_id}:{handoff_policy_version}); an outbox worker performs  │
     │ the GitHub call and records the result via                              │
     │ CaseService.record_handoff(...), which atomically stores                │
     │ issue_url/issue_id + appends handoff_created_issue. Body-marker search  │
     │ is a safety fallback only. Meta-case handoff is one issue; existing     │
     │ child issues are linked, not duplicated. Outcomes                       │
     │ (accepted/closed-dup/edited/re-severitied/routed) become eval signal.   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Snooze / ack / suppress — operator and agent suppression go through     │
     │ CaseService.suppress(...)/ack(...) (replaces D); SuppressionStore       │
     │ becomes a read-fallback shim. Operator vs agent via suppression_source; │
     │ TTL via suppressed_until/snoozed_until; expiry evaluated in the         │
     │ service from the case (no side-store cleanup). _auto_snooze calls the   │
     │ service. Reasons feed candidate known-benign/maintenance knowledge.     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Resolve — CaseService.resolve(...) requires a positive clean            │
     │ observation (proactive) or recovery+RECOVERY_COOLDOWN_SECONDS           │
     │ (reactive), reusing the existing recovered_pending→resolved machinery   │
     │ now hosted in the service (incident_memory.py:_expire_*_cases moves     │
     │ under CaseStore/CaseService); expired (idle) stays distinct. The loop   │
     │ never resolves.                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Correlate (storm) — after observe, both the loop and the webhook path   │
     │ call CorrelationService.correlate(observations); meta-case              │
     │ creation/attachment/stabilization is entirely service-owned (§4         │
     │ meta-case states).                                                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Knowledge extraction — on resolve/operator-confirm, CaseService (not    │
     │ the loop or graph) emits a sanitized learning_ledger_v1 candidate via a │
     │ knowledge_candidate outbox intent (idempotency                          │
     │ knowledge_candidate:{case_id|meta_case_id}:{event_id}) →                │
     │ app/knowledge/promotion.py (event_type                                  │
     │ lesson_candidate/noc_shadow_eval_summary, producer noc_shadow, status   │
     │ proposed, authority A4) → review-gated import into                      │
     │ knowledge/ledger/proposed/ (§6). Never auto-promoted.                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Ingestion & side effects (inbox → service → outbox)                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ One transactional spine for both proactive scans and reactive webhooks: │
     │ raw webhook / scanner result / notification → observation_inbox         │
     │ (durable, dedup_key) → normalized observation → CaseService transaction │
     │ {update projection + append case_event + insert outbox intent} →        │
     │ outbox worker performs side effect (FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED) → result    │
     │ written back via CaseService.                                           │
     │ The inbox absorbs duplicate delivery, retries, source replay,           │
     │ crash-before-apply, bursts, and storm-replay fixtures, and preserves    │
     │ raw-vs-normalized for audit. The outbox makes                           │
     │ reports/tickets/candidates idempotent across crashes/retries (keys      │
     │ above). Neither service performs a network side effect inside a state   │
     │ transition.                                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Operator control surfaces                                               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Every correction attaches to case_id/meta_case_id, trace_id?, actor,    │
     │ reason, timestamp and becomes a case_event (+ feedback), mutating state │
     │ only via CaseService/CorrelationService. Map to existing surfaces       │
     │ where present (today: nocctl decide; Discord /noc_ack /noc_unack        │
     │ /noc_acks /noc_pending /noc_status /noc_decide /noc_investigate; HTTP   │
     │ /control/proactive/ack|unack, /control/incidents/{id}/decision); add    │
     │ meta-case verbs:                                                        │
     │ - CLI (nocctl): case merge|split|attach|detach|confirm-root-cause|rejec │
     │ t-root-cause|mark-independent-action-required|suppress|ack|close.       │
     │ - Discord:                                                              │
     │ /noc_case_merge|split|attach|detach|confirm|reject|independent_action.  │
     │ - HTTP: POST /control/cases/{id}/merge|split|attach|detach|feedback.    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 6. hyrule-knowledge Integration Plan                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Repository shape (confirmed). OKF Markdown+frontmatter (okf/); exports  │
     │ exports/knowledge.sqlite (tables concepts, concept_fts FTS5,            │
     │ source_refs(repo,path,commit_sha,url), claims, context_packs,           │
     │ learning_events, …) + *.jsonl + manifest.json                           │
     │ (retrieval_version=retrieval_v1, policy_version=knowledge_policy_v1,    │
     │ run_id, source_shas); policy knowledge-policy.yml; ledger lifecycle +   │
     │ promotion.py; CI opens review-gated PRs.                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Retrieval bridge (export-authoritative + replayable, D4). New           │
     │ app/knowledge/retrieval.py in noc-agent:                                │
     │ - Pin a knowledge export at a known revision: vendor/sync               │
     │ knowledge.sqlite (+ manifest.json) to a path the agent reads read-only; │
     │ record export_version = manifest.run_id + knowledge git commit. A       │
     │ small app/knowledge/sync.py (or CI artifact) refreshes the pin          │
     │ deliberately.                                                           │
     │ - Query concepts/concept_fts/source_refs scoped by case context         │
     │ (fingerprint, rule_id, resource/site/customer, vendor/platform,         │
     │ symptoms, signal_signature, topology, issue labels). Return candidates  │
     │ with doc_path(concepts.path), doc_id(concepts.id), review_status,       │
     │ authority, source_refs.commit_sha, FTS score. Filter to                 │
     │ approved/authoritative tiers; mark deprecated/stale as                  │
     │ non-authoritative.                                                      │
     │ - Cite in every trace: doc_path, doc_id, review_status, section,        │
     │ repo_revision, export_version. Production decisions + replay/evals are  │
     │ reproducible from the pin alone.                                        │
     │ - Optional enrichment: add the knowledge MCP server as a noc MCP source │
     │ (a new read-only noc role in knowledge-policy.yml, modeled on           │
     │ noc_shadow) for richer context_pack.generate/resolve. If MCP is         │
     │ unavailable, only optional enrichment degrades — never core behavior.   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Promotion bridge (review-gated). app/knowledge/promotion.py emits       │
     │ learning_ledger_v1 events (validated against                            │
     │ knowledge/schema/learning-event.schema.json; forbidden data classes     │
     │ screened:                                                               │
     │ secret/credential/raw_log/packet_capture/command_output/live_trace)     │
     │ carrying case ids, sanitized timeline, suspected/final root cause,      │
     │ blast radius, what was symptom vs action, stabilization window,         │
     │ counterexamples, operator feedback, confidence, source citations. Flow: │
     │ resolved/confirmed case → sanitized event → knowledge/ledger/proposed/  │
     │ → human ledger --review / promote-pr → okf/curated/{lessons,summaries}  │
     │ (A1/A2). Statuses live in frontmatter + learning-event metadata         │
     │ (existing convention) — no new metadata scheme.                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Safety / model sovereignty. Unreviewed events stay A4 and are never     │
     │ retrieved as authoritative; promotion is PR-gated; retrieval and        │
     │ citation are model-agnostic and reproducible from the pinned export, so │
     │ a model swap keeps identical institutional inputs.                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Retrieval authority rules                                               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Approved/curated OKF (authority∈{canonical,advisory},                 │
     │ review_status=approved) may influence operational recommendations.      │
     │ - Candidate/shadow knowledge (A4, proposed) may be retrieved only as    │
     │ non-authoritative context, labeled as such.                             │
     │ - Deprecated/rejected knowledge must not be used as guidance except to  │
     │ avoid known-bad recommendations.                                        │
     │ - Every retrieved item cites doc_path, doc_id, review_status, authority │
     │ tier, section, repo_revision, export_version. (Test §8:                 │
     │ deprecated/rejected present but never used authoritatively.)            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 7. Migration Plan                                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 1. Stand up Postgres (net-new). Add app/db/{engine,models}.py (async    │
     │ SQLAlchemy 2.0 + asyncpg), alembic/ migrations, DATABASE_URL/NOC_PG_*   │
     │ config in app/config.py. Tables: cases (atomic+meta via kind),          │
     │ case_events, observations, handoffs, suppressions, feedback, traces,    │
     │ knowledge_citations, plus LangGraph checkpoint tables                   │
     │ (langgraph-checkpoint-postgres).                                        │
     │ 2. Add the shared case service + Postgres backend. Introduce            │
     │ app/cases/{store,service,correlation,models}.py: a CaseStore protocol + │
     │ PostgresCaseStore (authoritative; local/in-mem for dev/test) and the    │
     │ CaseService/CorrelationService that own the state machine. Refactor     │
     │ IncidentMemory to delegate to CaseStore/CaseService; route reactive     │
     │ intake_alert and proactive observe through CaseService. No production   │
     │ path depends on Redis. One-shot importer backfills any open             │
     │ Redis/in-mem cases on first boot.                                       │
     │ 3. Postgres LangGraph checkpointer. Extend                              │
     │ app/graph/checkpointing.py:build_checkpointer to prefer a Postgres      │
     │ saver (DATABASE_URL), Redis/in-mem only as fallback.                    │
     │ 4. Fold side stores (transitional dual-read). New writes go to case     │
     │ state; old investigations.json/suppressions.json/in-mem signatures are  │
     │ read as fallback until Phases 3–6 land, then removed. Handoff issue_url │
     │ backfilled by one marker-search per open proactive case.                │
     │ 5. Classify ProactiveMemory entries: operational state (none) /         │
     │ candidate lesson (proposals/ → ledger candidates) / durable knowledge   │
     │ (validated lessons → OKF promotion) / stale-noisy (drop). No bulk write │
     │ to approved knowledge.                                                  │
     │ 6. Schema versioning: schema_version on every case; lazy upgrade on     │
     │ load; alembic for DB. Keep back-compat dict round-trip through the      │
     │ transition.                                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Postgres concurrency & locking                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Replace app/main.py:_try_acquire_proactive_lock with a Postgres       │
     │ advisory lock (pg_advisory_lock) for the single-cycle guard.            │
     │ - Unique constraints for observation idempotency                        │
     │ (observation_inbox.dedup_key) and source dedup; outbox idempotency_key  │
     │ unique.                                                                 │
     │ - SELECT … FOR UPDATE for case/meta-case projection updates;            │
     │ row_version/updated_at compare-and-swap for optimistic concurrency      │
     │ where contended.                                                        │
     │ - FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED for outbox workers.                            │
     │ - Explicit transaction boundaries around observation → case_event →     │
     │ projection → outbox (replaces the Redis noc:intake:lock semantics in    │
     │ incident_memory.py:_intake_alert_redis).                                │
     │ - Never silently fall back to in-memory state in production — fail loud │
     │ if DATABASE_URL is unset. Tests for crash/retry/idempotency.            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Retention, partitioning & payload storage                               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Postgres durability replaces Redis TTLs, so retention is explicit:      │
     │ - cases/meta_cases: durable, long retention.                            │
     │ - case_events: durable; partition by month/time window if volume        │
     │ warrants.                                                               │
     │ - observations: retain normalized for the replay window;                │
     │ compact/archive older routine data.                                     │
     │ - Raw payloads: do not store large blobs in core tables — keep in       │
     │ object/file storage or compressed archive, referenced by payload_ref.   │
     │ - traces: retain eval-worthy long-term; compact routine.                │
     │ - side_effect_outbox: short retention after success, longer for         │
     │ failures.                                                               │
     │ - Knowledge candidates: governed by the knowledge repo review policy.   │
     │ - Sensitive-data redaction runs before any trace or knowledge candidate │
     │ is emitted (reuse the learning-event.schema.json data-class             │
     │ screening).                                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 8. Testing Plan                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Add/extend under hyrule-noc-agent/tests/ (mirroring                     │
     │ test_proactive_loop.py, test_incident_memory*,                          │
     │ test_proactive_suppressions.py, test_proactive_handoff.py,              │
     │ test_proactive_investigate.py, test_knowledge_shadow.py):               │
     │ - False all-clear prevention: case exists; next cycle skips/degrades    │
     │ the rule → case stays active; no resolve/all-clear (regression-locks    │
     │ #31 at the case level).                                                 │
     │ - Positive clean resolve: rule evaluated clean → resolves once; one     │
     │ resolve report.                                                         │
     │ - Report dedup / reassert: stable unhealthy state → one report then     │
     │ reassert only after TTL; per-cycle jitter posts nothing.                │
     │ - Signal change: material signal change flips report/investigation      │
     │ eligibility.                                                            │
     │ - Investigation reuse: same signal_signature+recent → skip with reused  │
     │ diagnosis; changed → reinvestigate with prior diagnosis in context.     │
     │ - Handoff idempotency: issue_url present → never duplicates; absent →   │
     │ creates+stores; partial-failure retry safe.                             │
     │ - Snooze/ack TTL: snoozed until TTL; expiry restores visibility;        │
     │ operator ack survives scan jitter; repeated benign snooze → candidate   │
     │ lesson.                                                                 │
     │ - Meta-case suite: router-down cascade (one meta-case, children         │
     │ attached, one report, one issue); self-healing reconvergence            │
     │ (→monitoring_recovery/stabilized, root stays active, resolve only on    │
     │ clean); unrelated simultaneous alerts (no false grouping); operator     │
     │ split/merge captured as feedback+eval; existing child issue linked, no  │
     │ dup.                                                                    │
     │ - Knowledge retrieval: matching case retrieves approved doc; deprecated │
     │ not authoritative; trace cites                                          │
     │ path/id/status/section/revision/export_version; stable across model     │
     │ adapters; reproducible from pinned export with MCP down.                │
     │ - Knowledge candidate: resolved meta-case emits A4 candidate with       │
     │ case/trace ids, timeline, blast radius, counterexamples; not approved   │
     │ without review; rejected not retrieved.                                 │
     │ - Migration: old JSON side stores read as fallback; existing cases      │
     │ readable; ProactiveMemory not blind-promoted; knowledge export          │
     │ indexed/read without mutation.                                          │
     │ - Postgres backend: CRUD + concurrency/atomicity (intake lock           │
     │ equivalent), no-Redis run is fully durable.                             │
     │ - No sixth memory: assert no new ad-hoc anti-dup file is introduced.    │
     │ - Model-swap: same case state + same pinned knowledge + same policy →   │
     │ acceptable behavior under an alternate model_chain.                     │
     │ - Service ownership: a proactive scan and a reactive webhook for the    │
     │ same concern converge on one case via CaseService; the LangGraph graph  │
     │ mutates no case truth (status/suppression/handoff/resolve), only        │
     │ returns InvestigationResult; the loop holds no durable decision state.  │
     │ - Observation inbox: duplicate webhook delivery / scanner retry /       │
     │ source replay yields one observation + one case effect; crash before    │
     │ apply re-processes safely.                                              │
     │ - Side-effect outbox: crash/retry never double-posts a report, ticket,  │
     │ or knowledge candidate; idempotency keys hold; failed intents retry     │
     │ with backoff.                                                           │
     │ - Identity aliases: old investigations.json/suppressions.json keys,     │
     │ issue markers, and proactive/reactive fingerprints all resolve to one   │
     │ stable case_id.                                                         │
     │ - Append-only events: projection + case_event written atomically;       │
     │ replay rebuilds state from case_events + observations.                  │
     │ - Child suppression reversibility: each trigger (severity up, signal    │
     │ change, persists-after-stabilize, new site/customer, root-cause         │
     │ rejected, operator override, confidence drop, evidence mismatch)        │
     │ re-surfaces the child.                                                  │
     │ - Monitoring-failure: source-degraded/failed → no false clean evidence; │
     │ monitoring-region outage opens a monitoring_failure meta-case.          │
     │ - Policy version: decisions/events record policy_version; replay        │
     │ compares behavior across versions.                                      │
     │ - Deprecated knowledge: present but never used authoritatively;         │
     │ citations recorded.                                                     │
     │ - Concurrency: advisory-lock single-cycle guard; FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED │
     │ outbox; optimistic-concurrency conflict handling.                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Architecture boundary tests (regression guard)                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - ProactiveLoop cannot directly mutate case status.                     │
     │ - LangGraph graph cannot mutate                                         │
     │ lifecycle/suppression/handoff/resolve/correlation state.                │
     │ - Reporter cannot send without a CaseService report intent; Handoff     │
     │ cannot create an issue without a CaseService handoff intent.            │
     │ - SuppressionStore and investigations.json are read-only fallbacks      │
     │ during migration.                                                       │
     │ - No new anti-dup JSON side store appears; no local in-memory report    │
     │ signature is authoritative.                                             │
     │ - Proactive scan + reactive webhook for the same concern converge       │
     │ through CaseService; meta-case attach/detach only through               │
     │ CorrelationService.                                                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 9. Private Eval / Replay Plan                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Add hyrule-noc-agent/evals/replay/ and a nocctl replay path. A replay = │
     │ time-ordered notification/observation stream + frozen case states +     │
     │ pinned knowledge export revision + frozen ProactiveMemory → run through │
     │ a candidate policy/model/prompt/toolchain → compare                     │
     │ decisions/non-decisions/report/handoff/resolve and cost against         │
     │ expected. Build fixtures from real case_events + traces (sanitized).    │
     │ Metrics: false all-clear rate, duplicate report/handoff rate,           │
     │ investigation-reuse accuracy, correct reinvestigation on change,        │
     │ knowledge-use correctness, severity/blast accuracy, storm detection     │
     │ latency, grouping precision/recall/false-grouping/missed-grouping,      │
     │ premature-resolution rate, operator-correction rate, time-to-diagnosis, │
     │ token/tool cost per useful case, regression on known incidents. This    │
     │ is the data+eval substrate for later RL/prompt/policy optimization — no │
     │ RL training in this refactor. Cross-check against the knowledge repo's  │
     │ own deterministic evals (knowledge/evals/, noc_shadow suite).           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 10. Observability Plan                                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Structured app.log events (low-noise) + trace records: case_created,    │
     │ case_observed_unhealthy/clean, case_skipped_no_observation,             │
     │ case_report_suppressed_no_state_change, case_reasserted,                │
     │ investigation_skipped_recent_same_signature,                            │
     │ investigation_started_changed_signature, hyrule_knowledge_retrieved (+  │
     │ path/id/status/section/revision/export_version),                        │
     │ hyrule_knowledge_not_found,                                             │
     │ hyrule_knowledge_deprecated_reference_skipped,                          │
     │ knowledge_candidate_created/promoted/rejected,                          │
     │ handoff_skipped_existing_issue, handoff_created_issue, case_snoozed,    │
     │ case_suppression_expired, case_resolved_positive_clean,                 │
     │ operator_feedback_recorded, eval_trace_recorded; plus meta-case events  │
     │ (storm_candidate_detected, meta_case_created/updated,                   │
     │ child_case_attached/detached, meta_case_merged/split,                   │
     │ root_cause_hypothesis_set/changed, blast_radius_expanded/reduced,       │
     │ child_report_suppressed_by_meta_case,                                   │
     │ child_investigation_skipped_covered_by_meta_case,                       │
     │ meta_case_reported/handed_off, self_healing_detected,                   │
     │ reconvergence_suspected, meta_case_entered_monitoring_recovery,         │
     │ meta_case_stabilized, meta_case_resolved_positive_clean,                │
     │ operator_confirmed/rejected_grouping, storm_pattern_candidate_created,  │
     │ storm_pattern_promoted_to_hyrule_knowledge). Enough to debug flapping,  │
     │ dup work, bad suppression, stale-knowledge reuse, missed retrieval, dup │
     │ tickets, false all-clears, model-swap regressions.                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 11. Rollout / Commit Plan (small, reviewable PRs)                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Strangler migration: 1A–1C are non-breaking scaffolding; 1D–1J are      │
     │ individually revertible flips behind config flags. Each bullet is its   │
     │ own small PR.                                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Phase 0 — Preserve #31. Confirm main carry-forward fix + reactive     │
     │ recovery/expiry semantics are untouched; add the false-all-clear        │
     │ regression test as the guard rail.                                      │
     │ - Phase 1A — Postgres schema + store (no behavior change). app/db/,     │
     │ alembic, app/cases/store.py (CaseStore + PostgresCaseStore), Postgres   │
     │ LangGraph checkpointer, config. Dormant. (Foundational.)                │
     │ - Phase 1B — Inbox + Outbox + substrate (no behavior change).           │
     │ observation_inbox, side_effect_outbox, case_events,                     │
     │ case_identity_aliases, meta_case_correlation_evidence, CasePolicy;      │
     │ workers built but unused.                                               │
     │ - Phase 1C — Shadow write + compare. Shadow-write                       │
     │ observations/case_events/traces to Postgres while the old runtime stays │
     │ authoritative; compare old decisions vs CaseService candidate           │
     │ decisions; emit metrics, no side effects.                               │
     │ - Phase 1D — Flip observe/resolve to CaseService (retire                │
     │ _last_deep_hotspots/_last_effective; preserve #31; refactor             │
     │ IncidentMemory to delegate; LangGraph becomes a read-only consumer      │
     │ returning InvestigationResult).                                         │
     │ - Phase 1E — Flip report dedup/reassert to CaseService + outbox (retire │
     │ A/_last_report_signature).                                              │
     │ - Phase 1F — Flip investigation reuse to CaseService (retire            │
     │ B/investigations.json; graph stays consumer).                           │
     │ - Phase 1G — Flip suppression/ack/snooze to CaseService (D → read-only  │
     │ fallback).                                                              │
     │ - Phase 1H — Flip handoff idempotency to issue_url/issue_id + outbox (C │
     │ → marker fallback).                                                     │
     │ - Phase 1I — Meta-case correlation in shadow (CorrelationService;       │
     │ deterministic layers; no child suppression / no meta reports yet).      │
     │ - Phase 1J — Enable meta-case reporting/handoff after storm tests pass  │
     │ (child suppression on; one meta report; one meta issue; existing child  │
     │ issues linked).                                                         │
     │ - Phase 2 — Trace store + operator-feedback attachment points +         │
     │ meta-case operator verbs (Postgres).                                    │
     │ - Phase 3 — Knowledge retrieval bridge (pinned export + citations +     │
     │ authority rules; optional MCP noc role).                                │
     │ - Phase 4 — Candidate knowledge extraction (app/knowledge/promotion.py  │
     │ via outbox → review-gated ledger).                                      │
     │ - Phase 5 — Private eval/replay fixtures from                           │
     │ case_events/observations/traces + frozen knowledge revisions.           │
     │ - Phase 6 — Remove/quarantine old side stores once boundary tests pass. │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 12. Risks and Open Questions                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Ownership leakage (guardrail). Case lifecycle, suppression,           │
     │ resolution, reporting dedup, and meta-case correlation must live only   │
     │ in CaseService/CorrelationService — never in ProactiveLoop (scheduler)  │
     │ or the LangGraph graph (investigation consumer/producer). Enforce with  │
     │ tests asserting the graph performs no                                   │
     │ case-status/suppression/handoff/resolve writes, and that proactive +    │
     │ reactive share one service.                                             │
     │ - Postgres is net-new in noc-agent (only                                │
     │ redis/langgraph-checkpoint-redis exist today). Phase 1 is the largest   │
     │ and gates everything; needs DB provisioning on the NOC VM and an        │
     │ async-SQLAlchemy concurrency model replicating the current Redis        │
     │ noc:intake:lock atomicity (incident_memory.py:_intake_alert_redis).     │
     │ - Fingerprint duality. Proactive hotspot fp vs alert-identity case fp;  │
     │ grounding must define one durable mapping (extend                       │
     │ hotspot_to_alert_payload/_case_for_hotspot) so side-store keys and case │
     │ keys finally coincide.                                                  │
     │ - Ephemeral→durable shift. Today cases TTL out (CASE_HISTORY_SECONDS);  │
     │ Postgres makes them durable — define explicit retention/close policy so │
     │ expired vs resolved stays meaningful and tables don't grow unbounded.   │
     │ - Storm correlation precision. Topology data comes from                 │
     │ infra:parent:*/topology_parents; sparse topology risks mis-grouping →   │
     │ keep confidence thresholds + operator split/merge as first-class        │
     │ corrections.                                                            │
     │ - Knowledge pin freshness. Export-authoritative retrieval can serve     │
     │ stale knowledge; surface export_version/repo_revision in traces and add │
     │ a staleness warning + deliberate refresh.                               │
     │ - Sensitive-data leakage into candidates — enforce                      │
     │ learning-event.schema.json data-class screening + redaction before any  │
     │ ledger write; promotion stays human-gated.                              │
     │ - Scope. Sections 8–11 of the prompt (meta-cases) are large; Phases     │
     │ 8–12 may each split further. Confirm whether meta-cases must ship this  │
     │ cycle or can trail the operational consolidation.                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 13. Acceptance Criteria                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - The ProactiveLoop is a scheduler and the LangGraph graph an           │
     │ investigation consumer/producer; a shared                               │
     │ CaseService/CorrelationService (over a Postgres CaseStore) is the sole  │
     │ owner of case lifecycle, suppression, resolution, reporting dedup, and  │
     │ correlation for both proactive and reactive inputs.                     │
     │ - IncidentMemory cases (Postgres-backed) are authoritative for active   │
     │ concerns; a missed/skipped/degraded scan never causes false all-clear;  │
     │ resolve only on positive clean / recovery / operator close / explicit   │
     │ stale policy.                                                           │
     │ - Duplicate reports prevented by case state; reassertions               │
     │ case-grounded; investigations skipped on recent same-signature          │
     │ diagnosis and reinvestigations include prior context.                   │
     │ - Handoff never duplicates when issue_url/issue_id exists;              │
     │ snooze/ack/suppression live on the case with TTL semantics.             │
     │ - The five side stores are removed or reduced to temporary fallbacks;   │
     │ no new anti-dup mechanism introduced; no production behavior depends on │
     │ Redis as a second source of truth.                                      │
     │ - Case events + decision traces are replay/eval-ready; operator         │
     │ feedback attaches to case+trace ids.                                    │
     │ - Notification storms produce one durable meta-case (first-class        │
     │ IncidentMemory record) with linked children; self-healing handled       │
     │ without premature all-clear; operators can                              │
     │ merge/split/attach/detach/confirm/reject and those corrections become   │
     │ learning signal.                                                        │
     │ - hyrule-knowledge is retrieved during                                  │
     │ correlation/investigation/report/handoff from a pinned export, cited in │
     │ traces with path/id/status/section/revision/export_version,             │
     │ reproducible with MCP unavailable; resolved/confirmed cases yield       │
     │ review-gated OKF/learning_ledger_v1 candidates; approved knowledge      │
     │ survives a model swap.                                                  │
     │ - Tests cover scan jitter, clean resolve, dedup, investigation reuse,   │
     │ handoff idempotency, suppression TTL, migration, Postgres durability,   │
     │ storms, knowledge retrieval+candidates, and model-swap.                 │
     │ - The Architecture Invariants hold and are enforced by §8 boundary      │
     │ tests.                                                                  │
     │ - Observation Inbox provides idempotent, durable ingestion; Side-Effect │
     │ Outbox makes reports/handoffs/knowledge candidates crash-safe and       │
     │ idempotent.                                                             │
     │ - case_identity_aliases resolves proactive/reactive/source/external     │
     │ identity drift to one stable case_id.                                   │
     │ - case_events are append-only; projections written atomically with      │
     │ events; replay rebuildable from events + observations.                  │
     │ - Postgres advisory locks / unique constraints / FOR UPDATE / SKIP      │
     │ LOCKED provide production concurrency; no silent in-memory fallback.    │
     │ - Meta-case child suppression is reversible and evidence-based;         │
     │ monitoring-source degradation cannot create false clean evidence.       │
     │ - policy_version is recorded on case events/traces and is replayable;   │
     │ thresholds/TTLs are policy-driven.                                      │
     │ - Retention/partitioning/payload storage are explicit; sensitive-data   │
     │ redaction precedes trace/candidate emission.                            │
     │ - Knowledge authority tiers are enforced during retrieval (approved     │
     │ authoritative; candidate non-authoritative; deprecated/rejected not     │
     │ used as guidance).                                                      │
     │ - Operator merge/split/attach/detach/root-cause corrections are         │
     │ first-class feedback on case_id/meta_case_id.                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ Verification (how to test end-to-end)                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Unit/integration: cd /home/svag/Dev/hyrule-noc-agent && uv run pytest │
     │ (focused: tests/test_proactive_loop.py,                                 │
     │ test_proactive_suppressions.py, test_proactive_handoff.py,              │
     │ test_proactive_investigate.py, new tests/test_case_grounding.py,        │
     │ tests/test_meta_case.py, tests/test_knowledge_retrieval.py,             │
     │ tests/test_db_backend.py); lint/type per CI (ruff, mypy --strict).      │
     │ - Replay: uv run nocctl replay evals/replay/<fixture> and assert        │
     │ metrics (false-all-clear=0, grouping precision/recall, citation         │
     │ presence) vs baseline.                                                  │
     │ - Knowledge loop: point retrieval at the pinned                         │
     │ knowledge/exports/knowledge.sqlite; run an investigation; confirm trace │
     │ citations; generate a candidate and dry-run cd                          │
     │ /home/svag/Dev/knowledge && uv run hyrule-knowledge ledger --review     │
     │ <id> (no auto-promote); run uv run hyrule-knowledge eval --check.       │
     │ - Live smoke (shadow): NOC_PROACTIVE_ENABLED=1 NOC_PROACTIVE_SHADOW=1   │
     │ against a Postgres DATABASE_URL with no NOC_REDIS_URL; drive a          │
     │ synthetic Alertmanager/Icinga storm at /webhook/*; confirm one          │
     │ meta-case, no dup tickets, durable cases across a restart.              │
