● Plan refined and coherent. Summary of this pass:

  Agentic orchestration
  - New top-level Agentic Orchestration Layer section + matching Architecture 
  Invariants: ProactiveLoop stays a deterministic runtime that may invoke
  NOCDutyOfficerAgent; the agent is advisory-only and never mutates
  lifecycle/suppression/handoff/resolve/report/correlation/knowledge truth.
  Persona = Senior Network/Service Reliability Engineer (role profile, not
  authority). Coherence fixed: the loop "drives work; side effects execute via 
  outbox workers" everywhere (Context, §5 table, Rank/gate line).
  - Deployment modes disabled → shadow → advise → guarded_act (+ manual_only),
  with "don't skip shadow; no guarded_act until eval passes."

  Role model
  - NOCDutyOfficerAgent brain + 11 role profiles (EventCorrelation,
  TopologyAnalyst, Investigation, KnowledgeLibrarian, SourceHealth,
  IncidentScribe, EscalationCoordinator, ChangeContext, LearningCurator,
  PolicyGuard, ReplayEval) as a table; start as one agent with internal role 
  prompts, split later.

  Data contracts
  - Typed CycleSnapshot (frozen input, extends today's DecisionContext),
  CyclePlan (agent output), ActionIntent (proposal), ValidatedIntent (service
  output). Hard rule: only ValidatedIntent may create case_events/outbox rows.

  Validation boundaries
  - Per-stage overlay table in §5 (agent proposes →
  CaseService/CorrelationService/KnowledgeAuthorityFilter/PolicyGuard validate);
  the deterministic stages remain the law. Agent failure/timeout →
  deterministic safe baseline.

  Testing and replay
  - §8 Agentic layer tests (shadow no-writes, outage fallback, invalid
  resolve/dup-handoff/suppression rejected+traced, storm-proposal validation,
  child-hidden reversal, knowledge-authority enforcement, drafting separation,
  replay reproducibility, role-prompt smoke). §9 Agent replay & metrics (freeze
  snapshot/policy/export/model/prompt/mode + fixtures; metrics like
  rejected_resolve_intent_rate, storm_hypothesis_precision/recall,
  deterministic_fallback_rate, deprecated_knowledge_misuse_rate).

  Rollout updates
  - Inserted Agent-0 → Agent-6 phases between eval/replay and cleanup (contracts
  → disabled → shadow → role prompts → advise → guarded_act low-risk →
  guarded_act higher-risk), plus an explicit "never ungated autonomous" list
  (resolve w/o positive-clean, knowledge promotion, in-memory fallback,
  duplicate handoff).

  Risks/open questions
  - Added: authority creep, over-agentification, latency/budget,
  confident-but-wrong, knowledge
  misuse/over-grouping/operator-trust/replay-nondeterminism. Open questions:
  role name in config, first guarded_act intents, cycle-time budget, split
  EventCorrelation vs internal prompt, operator UI surface, approval confidence
  threshold. §10 observability + §13 acceptance extended to match.

  Repo-consistency note (no contradiction): the role model is anchored to what
  already exists — app/agents/ (today mail.py, triage.py), app/model_config.py
  (FallbackModel/model_chain), and the investigation graph's existing routing
  (supervisor_route) as the seed for InvestigationAgent — so this is additive,
  not a parallel agent framework.

     ╭─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────╮
     │ Case-Grounded Self-Learning Loop Refactor Plan                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Context                                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Why this change. The NOC Agent's proactive loop                         │
     │ (hyrule-noc-agent/app/proactive/loop.py) re-derives state every cycle   │
     │ (scan → rank → gate → investigate → report → handoff/resolve) and has   │
     │ accreted five separate anti-duplication side stores to stop flapping,   │
     │ duplicate reports, duplicate tickets, and false all-clears. None of     │
     │ them share one notion of "the current state of a concern," and —        │
     │ critically — they are keyed by hotspot fingerprint                      │
     │ (sha256(rule_id|key)[:16], models.py:Hotspot.fingerprint) while the     │
     │ durable case is keyed by alert-identity fingerprint                     │
     │ (incident_memory.py:fingerprint_alert). The proactive loop therefore    │
     │ makes its don't-duplicate decisions outside the case.                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Meanwhile the reactive path already has the state machine we want:      │
     │ IncidentMemory (app/incident_memory.py) keeps durable cases with a real │
     │ lifecycle, parent↔child topology linking, and                           │
     │ resolve-only-on-positive-recovery semantics. The refactor's thesis —    │
     │ the case is the authoritative state machine — is already half-true; we  │
     │ must extend the case to own the proactive stages too, add meta-cases    │
     │ for notification storms, and wire a replayable, governed                │
     │ hyrule-knowledge learning loop so institutional NOC judgment survives a │
     │ model swap.                                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Targets (confirmed cross-repo). This plan is implemented against:       │
     │ - /home/svag/Dev/hyrule-noc-agent (remote AS215932/noc-agent) — the     │
     │ loop, cases, side stores.                                               │
     │ - /home/svag/Dev/knowledge (remote AS215932/knowledge) — the            │
     │ institutional repo the prompt calls "hyrule-knowledge".                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Confirmed decisions shaping this plan:                                  │
     │ 1. Proceed cross-repo now; this plan file stays in the current project. │
     │ 2. Sequence: preserve #31 → operational consolidation (5 side stores    │
     │ onto the case) → meta-cases/storms → knowledge loop.                    │
     │ 3. Postgres is the authoritative production backend for IncidentMemory, │
     │ meta-cases, observations, case events, handoffs, suppressions,          │
     │ feedback, trace references, and LangGraph checkpoints. Redis/Valkey is  │
     │ optional hot-path only (queues, pub/sub, short-lived dedup/rate-limit   │
     │ windows, storm correlation). No production behavior may silently depend │
     │ on Redis as a second source of truth.                                   │
     │ 4. Knowledge retrieval is export-authoritative + replayable: production │
     │ correlation/investigation reads a pinned deterministic SQLite/JSONL     │
     │ export of hyrule-knowledge; the knowledge MCP server is optional        │
     │ noc-role enrichment only. Every trace records the exact document path,  │
     │ document id, approval status, section, and repo revision / export       │
     │ version used.                                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Architectural principle (ownership). The ProactiveLoop is demoted to a  │
     │ scheduler/orchestrator — it paces cycles, runs scanners, builds the     │
     │ CycleSnapshot, and drives work — side effects execute via outbox        │
     │ workers, not the loop — but owns no durable case lifecycle. It may      │
     │ invoke an advisory NOCDutyOfficerAgent (see Agentic Orchestration       │
     │ Layer) that only proposes. The authoritative state machine lives in a   │
     │ shared case/correlation service layer (CaseService/CorrelationService   │
     │ over a CaseStore) used identically by proactive scan observations and   │
     │ reactive webhook alerts, so there is one notion of a concern. LangGraph │
     │ investigation is a consumer of case/meta-case/knowledge context and a   │
     │ producer of structured investigation results — it must not own case     │
     │ status, suppression, handoff, resolve, reporting dedup, or correlation  │
     │ truth. Do not bury any of that in the loop or the graph.                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Discrepancies vs. the original prompt (repo wins):                      │
     │ - OKF, not ODF. hyrule-knowledge stores Markdown + YAML frontmatter     │
     │ with deterministic JSONL/SQLite exports (knowledge/okf/,                │
     │ knowledge/exports/knowledge.sqlite). There are no .odt/.ods/.fodt       │
     │ files. "Candidate ODF artifact" → OKF concept + learning_ledger_v1 JSON │
     │ event.                                                                  │
     │ - Cases are not on-disk files. NOC-20260617-006 is a case_number        │
     │ display string; cases live in Redis (prod today) or in-memory           │
     │ (dev/test). We are moving authority to Postgres.                        │
     │ - #31 is already merged to main (234a92d, ee55528). We preserve it, not │
     │ re-merge it. The reactive path already embodies its principle (resolve  │
     │ only on positive recovery + cooldown).                                  │
     │ - No meta-cases exist today — but parent/child linking +                │
     │ IncidentMemory.correlate() are the seed.                                │
     │ - ProactiveMemory is already non-authoritative                          │
     │ (lessons/proposals/observations/journal) — it does not need demoting,   │
     │ only wiring into the knowledge promotion bridge.                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ Architecture Invariants                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Hard rules every PR and test must enforce (mirrored in §8 boundary      │
     │ tests and §13 acceptance):                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - ProactiveLoop may orchestrate cycles, run scanners, call services,    │
     │ and do scheduled work — it must not own durable case lifecycle state.   │
     │ - LangGraph may investigate and return structured InvestigationResult   │
     │ objects — it must not mutate case status, suppression, handoff,         │
     │ resolve, report-dedup, or correlation truth.                            │
     │ - Reporters may render/send notifications only from CaseService report  │
     │ intents (via the outbox).                                               │
     │ - Handoff code may create/update external issues only from CaseService  │
     │ handoff intents (via the outbox).                                       │
     │ - CaseService is the only owner of atomic case lifecycle state.         │
     │ - CorrelationService is the only owner of meta-case grouping,           │
     │ attach/detach, merge/split, and storm lifecycle state.                  │
     │ - CaseStore/Postgres is the authoritative production state store.       │
     │ - Any Redis/Valkey use is optional and transient only (hot-path         │
     │ cache/queue/dedup-window) — never a second source of truth.             │
     │ - No new JSON/file/local-cache side store may become an                 │
     │ anti-duplication mechanism.                                             │
     │ - ProactiveLoop is a deterministic agent runtime/orchestrator, not an   │
     │ agentic state owner; it may invoke NOCDutyOfficerAgent to produce       │
     │ planning proposals.                                                     │
     │ - NOCDutyOfficerAgent must not directly mutate case lifecycle,          │
     │ suppression, handoff, resolve, reporting, correlation, or               │
     │ knowledge-authority state. All its outputs are proposals.               │
     │ - CaseService validates atomic-case proposals before they become        │
     │ case_events/outbox intents; CorrelationService validates meta-case,     │
     │ storm-correlation, attach/detach, merge/split, and stabilization        │
     │ proposals likewise.                                                     │
     │ - Knowledge-authority filters validate knowledge citations before any   │
     │ agent recommendation may rely on them.                                  │
     │ - Side effects still happen only through the Side-Effect Outbox.        │
     │ - Agent failure, timeout, or disabled mode must not stop the            │
     │ deterministic safe baseline loop. (This is an additive reasoning layer, │
     │ not a replacement for deterministic state-machine ownership.)           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ Agentic Orchestration Layer                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ProactiveLoop stays a deterministic runtime/clock/worker/supervisor; it │
     │ may host an agentic planning stage that invokes the                     │
     │ NOCDutyOfficerAgent, but the agent only proposes — deterministic        │
     │ services remain the law.                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ▎ NOCDutyOfficerAgent is the senior-engineer brain.                     │
     │ ▎ CaseService/CorrelationService are the law. Outbox workers are the    │
     │ ▎ hands. hyrule-knowledge is the institution. Replay/evals are the      │
     │ ▎ memory of whether the brain is improving.                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Role profile (persona, not authority): Senior Network / Service         │
     │ Reliability Engineer — prefer Senior Network Reliability Engineer /     │
     │ Senior SRE (Network Reliability) for ISP/NOC contexts; NOC shift lead.  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Mission: act like the senior engineer on NOC duty — read current        │
     │ case/meta-case state, understand what changed, recognize notification   │
     │ storms, retrieve+use approved hyrule-knowledge, decide what deserves    │
     │ attention, propose a safe CyclePlan, surface uncertainty, and ask for   │
     │ operator approval when needed.                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Authority — advisory/planning only. It never directly mutates           │
     │ operational truth: never resolves, suppresses, marks reported, creates  │
     │ tickets, attaches/detaches child cases, or promotes knowledge. All      │
     │ outputs are proposals.                                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Validation. CaseService, CorrelationService, the                        │
     │ KnowledgeAuthorityFilter, and the PolicyGuard validate every proposed   │
     │ action against deterministic policy, current case/meta-case state,      │
     │ positive-clean evidence rules, idempotency rules, source-health rules,  │
     │ and knowledge-authority rules.                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Repo consistency: builds on the existing app/agents/ package (today     │
     │ mail.py, triage.py) and app/model_config.py (FallbackModel,             │
     │ model_chain); the investigation graph's existing routing                │
     │ (supervisor_route, specialist routing) is the seed for                  │
     │ InvestigationAgent.                                                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Deployment modes                                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - disabled: deterministic policy only; agent not invoked.               │
     │ - shadow: agent produces CyclePlan proposals recorded to traces/evals;  │
     │ no side effects or state changes from the plan.                         │
     │ - advise: proposals visible to operators; operators may approve/act     │
     │ manually; no automatic side effects.                                    │
     │ - guarded_act: proposals may create CaseService/CorrelationService      │
     │ intents only after deterministic validation; side effects still run via │
     │ the outbox.                                                             │
     │ - manual_only: every agent-proposed side effect requires operator       │
     │ approval.                                                               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Initial rollout disabled → shadow → advise → guarded_act. Do not skip   │
     │ shadow; do not enable guarded_act until replay/eval metrics pass.       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Agent planning data contracts                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Conceptual typed contracts (plan, not code). Only ValidatedIntent may   │
     │ create case_events or outbox rows.                                      │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - CycleSnapshot (frozen input): cycle_id, observed_at, policy_version,  │
     │ knowledge_export_version, model_chain, prompt_version, budget_state,    │
     │ new_observations, active_atomic_cases, active_meta_cases,               │
     │ recently_resolved_cases, suppressed_cases,                              │
     │ cases_in_monitoring_recovery, handoff_state, investigation_freshness,   │
     │ source_health_summary, recent_operator_feedback,                        │
     │ retrieved_hyrule_knowledge, prior_cycle_summary, open_outbox_intents,   │
     │ uncertainty_flags. (Extends today's DecisionContext.)                   │
     │ - CyclePlan (agent output): cycle_id, plan_id, agent_role_profile,      │
     │ policy_version, knowledge_export_version, priority_order,               │
     │ proposed_actions, storm_hypotheses, root_cause_hypotheses,              │
     │ investigation_plans, report_recommendations, handoff_recommendations,   │
     │ suppression_recommendations, operator_questions,                        │
     │ knowledge_candidate_recommendations, reasoning_summary,                 │
     │ uncertainty_summary, knowledge_citations, confidence, token_cost,       │
     │ tool_calls.                                                             │
     │ - ActionIntent (one proposal): intent_id, intent_type∈{investigate,repo │
     │ rt,handoff,suppress,ack,ask_operator,attach_child_to_meta_case,detach_c │
     │ hild_from_meta_case,merge_meta_cases,split_meta_case,mark_independent_a │
     │ ction_required,set_root_cause_hypothesis,create_knowledge_candidate},   │
     │ target_case_id, target_meta_case_id, rationale, evidence_refs,          │
     │ observation_refs, case_event_refs, knowledge_citations, confidence,     │
     │ requires_operator_approval, idempotency_key.                            │
     │ - ValidatedIntent (service output): intent_id,                          │
     │ validation_status∈{accepted,rejected,requires_operator_approval},       │
     │ rejection_reason, validator∈{CaseService,CorrelationService,KnowledgeAu │
     │ thorityFilter,PolicyGuard}, committed_case_event_id, outbox_id,         │
     │ created_trace_id.                                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Rule: the agent emits CyclePlan; services produce ValidatedIntent; only │
     │ ValidatedIntent creates case_events/outbox rows.                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Agent Role Model                                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Role profiles/interfaces — the first implementation is one              │
     │ NOCDutyOfficerAgent invoking role-specific internal prompts/tools;      │
     │ split into separate agents only when isolation improves reliability,    │
     │ testing, or replay. None write truth directly.                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Role: NOCDutyOfficerAgent                                               │
     │ Human analogue: Senior NRE/SRE, NOC shift lead                          │
     │ Purpose: Top-level planning brain; prioritize cases/meta-cases; produce │
     │                                                                         │
     │   CyclePlan                                                             │
     │ Writes truth?: No                                                       │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Role: EventCorrelationAgent                                             │
     │ Human analogue: Event/storm analyst                                     │
     │ Purpose: Detect storms/cascades; propose meta-case grouping,            │
     │ parent/root, blast                                                      │
     │   radius, confidence                                                    │
     │ Writes truth?: No — CorrelationService validates                        │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Role: TopologyAnalystAgent                                              │
     │ Human analogue: Network topology engineer                               │
     │ Purpose: Reason over                                                    │
     │   routers/switches/POPs/sites/circuits/peers/dependencies/reconvergence │
     │ +                                                                       │
     │   affected customers/services                                           │
     │ Writes truth?: No                                                       │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Role: InvestigationAgent                                                │
     │ Human analogue: Incident investigator                                   │
     │ Purpose: Deep diagnosis from case state + prior diagnosis + tools +     │
     │ approved                                                                │
     │   knowledge; return InvestigationResult                                 │
     │ Writes truth?: No — CaseService records if valid                        │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Role: KnowledgeLibrarianAgent                                           │
     │ Human analogue: Runbook/knowledge engineer                              │
     │ Purpose: Retrieve approved hyrule-knowledge from pinned export; label   │
     │   candidate/deprecated/stale; ensure full citations                     │
     │ Writes truth?: No                                                       │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Role: SourceHealthAgent                                                 │
     │ Human analogue: Monitoring reliability engineer                         │
     │ Purpose: Classify sources healthy/degraded/failed/uncertain; block      │
     │ unreliable                                                              │
     │   clears/missing alerts/outages as clean evidence                       │
     │ Writes truth?: No — CaseService applies policy                          │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Role: IncidentScribeAgent                                               │
     │ Human analogue: Incident comms lead                                     │
     │ Purpose: Draft reports / handoff summaries / reassertions / timelines / │
     │                                                                         │
     │   resolution summaries                                                  │
     │ Writes truth?: No — does not decide to send                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Role: EscalationCoordinatorAgent                                        │
     │ Human analogue: Escalation/routing lead                                 │
     │ Purpose: Propose handoff yes/no, route, title/body, labels, severity,   │
     │   escalation target                                                     │
     │ Writes truth?: No — CaseService validates                               │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Role: ChangeContextAgent                                                │
     │ Human analogue: Change/maintenance coordinator                          │
     │ Purpose: Check known maintenance, planned changes, expected             │
     │ reconvergence                                                           │
     │   windows, maintenance suppressions, change-induced storms              │
     │ Writes truth?: No                                                       │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Role: LearningCuratorAgent                                              │
     │ Human analogue: Postmortem/knowledge curator                            │
     │ Purpose: Convert resolved/operator-confirmed cases into sanitized       │
     │ review-gated                                                            │
     │   learning_ledger_v1 candidates                                         │
     │ Writes truth?: No — never promotes directly                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Role: PolicyGuardAgent                                                  │
     │ Human analogue: Safety/reliability reviewer                             │
     │ Purpose: Check proposals vs invariants (no resolve w/o positive clean;  │
     │ no dup                                                                  │
     │   handoff when issue_url/issue_id exists; no authoritative use of       │
     │   deprecated/candidate knowledge; no hidden child when independent      │
     │ action                                                                  │
     │   required; no non-authoritative production fallback; no                │
     │ source-degraded clear)                                                  │
     │ Writes truth?: Prefer deterministic validation; LLM may explain, not    │
     │ override                                                                │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Role: ReplayEvalAgent                                                   │
     │ Human analogue: Eval analyst                                            │
     │ Purpose: Offline-only comparison of traces, policy/prompt/model         │
     │ variants,                                                               │
     │   replay fixtures                                                       │
     │ Writes truth?: Offline only                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 1. Current Architecture Map                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Entry points / orchestration                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Mount: app/main.py:lifespan constructs ProactiveLoop(...) and calls   │
     │ .start() (singleton-guarded by _try_acquire_proactive_lock). The loop   │
     │ is a bare asyncio task (loop.py:_run → run_once), not LangGraph.        │
     │ LangGraph (app/graph/) is used only inside an investigation.            │
     │ - Reactive ingress: app/main.py POST /webhook/alertmanager and POST     │
     │ /webhook/icinga (_icinga_to_alert_payload) →                            │
     │ graph_runtime.intake_alert() → IncidentMemory.intake_alert() →          │
     │ investigation graph.                                                    │
     │ - Per cycle: loop.py:run_once → scan → _merge_with_carried →            │
     │ _auto_snooze → _apply_suppressions → build_decision_context →           │
     │ evaluate_gate → _investigate → update_ledger → _persist_memory →        │
     │ _safe_report.                                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Stage functions / classes                                               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ┌────────────┬───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┐                                                                    │
     │ │   Stage    │                            Code                          │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ ├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ Scan /     │ app/proactive/scanner.py:scan, ScanContext;              │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │ hotspots   │ DEEP_RULE_IDS={"disk_fill","tls_expiry"};                │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │            │ models.py:Hotspot                                        │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ ├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ Rank /     │ app/proactive/governance.py:eligible_hotspots,           │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │ gate       │ evaluate_gate, GateDecision;                             │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │            │ build_decision_context→models.py:DecisionContext         │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ ├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ Investigat │ loop.py:_investigate;                                    │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │ e          │ app/proactive/investigate.py:build_investigator (wraps   │
     │ the │                                                                   │
     │ │            │  graph via synthetic alert)                              │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ ├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ Report     │ loop.py:_report_decision, _safe_report, _default_report, │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │            │ _hotspot_field, _case_for_hotspot                        │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ ├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ Handoff    │                                                          │
     │ app/proactive/handoff.py:GitHubHandoff.ensure_candidate_is │            │
     │ │            │ sue (issue #-marker search)                              │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ ├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ Resolve /  │ loop.py:_merge_with_carried + _report_decision           │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │ all-clear  │ (proactive); incident_memory.py:_expire_*_cases          │
     │ (reactive) │                                                            │
     │ ├────────────┼───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┤                                                                    │
     │ │ Snooze /   │ app/proactive/suppressions.py:SuppressionStore;          │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │ ack /      │ loop.py:_apply_suppressions, _auto_snooze;               │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ │ suppress   │ app/icinga_ack.py                                        │
     │   │                                                                     │
     │ └────────────┴───────────────────────────────────────────────────────── │
     │ ───┘                                                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Memory / state                                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - IncidentMemory (app/incident_memory.py): Redis or in-memory           │
     │ _LocalIncidentMemory. Case dict from _new_case (incident_id,            │
     │ case_number, fingerprint, identity, resource_id, status,                │
     │ downstream_victims, linked_parent_case, recovered_at,                   │
     │ latest_transition, event_count, source_excerpt, …). Indices:            │
     │ fingerprint_index, case_number_index, resource_open_cases,              │
     │ topology_parents, noc:case:expiry zset. Statuses:                       │
     │ OPEN_CASE_STATUSES={investigating,waiting_approval,recovered_pending}   │
     │ plus resolved/expired/linked.                                           │
     │ - ProactiveMemory (app/proactive/memory.py): lessons/ (md), proposals/  │
     │ (CandidateLesson json), observations.jsonl, journal/. A learning        │
     │ flywheel (evaluate_outcomes), not operational truth — correct already.  │
     │ - Budget ledger (app/proactive/ledger.py): per-day ledger-{day}.json    │
     │ (cycles/investigations/cost/handoffs) — cost control, not learning.     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Fingerprint logic                                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Hotspot: models.py:Hotspot.fingerprint =                              │
     │ sha256(f"{rule_id}|{key}")[:16].                                        │
     │ - Case: incident_memory.py:fingerprint_alert(payload)=sha256(alert_iden │
     │ tity(payload)). A hotspot becomes a case via                            │
     │ models.py:hotspot_to_alert_payload (source="proactive") → intake_alert. │
     │ The two keyspaces never meet except in loop.py:_case_for_hotspot        │
     │ (advisory digest linking).                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Eval / trace / feedback / model abstraction (what exists)               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Decision context: models.py:DecisionContext (decision_id, cycle_id,   │
     │ manifest_hash, ruleset_version, model_chain, budget_state,              │
     │ injected_lesson_ids) — built per cycle, but only decision_id is         │
     │ persisted (onto the report); no queryable trace store.                  │
     │ - Journal/observations: per-cycle journal/{cycle_id}.md +               │
     │ observations.jsonl + evaluate_outcomes (predictions vs reactive         │
     │ alerts).                                                                │
     │ - Feedback: graph_runtime.record_operator_decision via Discord          │
     │ /noc_decide, web POST /control/incidents/{id}/decision, app/nocctl.py.  │
     │ - Model abstraction: app/model_config.py (AgentModelConfig,             │
     │ FallbackModel, active_model_chain), app/model_metrics.py (token usage,  │
     │ fallback counters). Versioned via ruleset_version, manifest_hash,       │
     │ model_chain. No prompt_version/policy_version yet.                      │
     │ - Knowledge integration: fixtures only — app/knowledge_shadow.py        │
     │ validates evals/knowledge_shadow/ context-pack + learning_ledger_v1     │
     │ fixtures. No live retrieval, no live promotion.                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ hyrule-knowledge (current)                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ OKF Markdown + YAML frontmatter under okf/{curated,generated,observed}; │
     │ deterministic exports                                                   │
     │ exports/{knowledge.sqlite,*.jsonl,manifest.json};                       │
     │ schema/{frontmatter,learning-event,…}.schema.json; knowledge-policy.yml │
     │ (roles incl. noc_shadow); ledger/{fixtures,proposed,reviews};           │
     │ src/hyrule_knowledge/{retrieval,context_pack,store,learning_ledger,prom │
     │ otion,policy,mcp_server}.py; CI request-promotion/ingest open           │
     │ review-gated PRs (never auto-merge). Authority tiers A0–A5.             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 2. Existing Side-Store Inventory                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ #: A                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Report dedup                                                 │
     │ File / structure: loop.py _last_report_signature,_last_report_ts        │
     │ (in-mem                                                                 │
     │   frozenset[(fp,sev)])                                                  │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp+sev                                                  │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: process lifetime; reassert report_reassert_s=3600         │
     │ Gates: whether to post digest                                           │
     │ Failure mode: restart loses dedup → re-post; per-cycle set jitter       │
     │ Replacement on the case: case.last_reported_signature/at,               │
     │ last_reasserted_at;                                                     │
     │   report-worthiness derived from case transitions                       │
     │ Removal: Migrate (Phase 3)                                              │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: B                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Investigation cooldown                                       │
     │ File / structure: investigations.json {fp:ts}                           │
     │   (_recent_investigation_fps/_record_investigations)                    │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp                                                      │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: investigation_cooldown_s=21600                            │
     │ Gates: skip re-investigation                                            │
     │ Failure mode: file loss → re-investigate; not case-aware                │
     │ Replacement on the case: case.last_investigated_at +                    │
     │ diagnosis_signature +                                                   │
     │   reinvestigate_after                                                   │
     │ Removal: Migrate→remove (Phase 4)                                       │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: C                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Handoff idempotency                                          │
     │ File / structure: handoff.py GitHub search for body marker              │
     │   proactive-fingerprint:{fp} + label loop:candidate                     │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp (in issue body)                                      │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: GitHub lifetime                                           │
     │ Gates: create vs refresh issue                                          │
     │ Failure mode: GitHub search miss/rate-limit → dup issue; no local       │
     │ record                                                                  │
     │ Replacement on the case: case.issue_url/issue_id/handoff_status; marker │
     │ search                                                                  │
     │   demoted to fallback                                                   │
     │ Removal: Migrate→fallback (Phase 5)                                     │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: D                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Suppression                                                  │
     │ File / structure: suppressions.json via SuppressionStore                │
     │ Keying: hotspot fp prefix                                               │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: expires_at (timed) or until-resolved                      │
     │ Gates: drop from digest+investigation                                   │
     │ Failure mode: file is the only record; not on case; prefix matching     │
     │ Replacement on the case:                                                │
     │ case.suppressed_until/snoozed_until/suppression_source/reason           │
     │   + suppression events                                                  │
     │ Removal: Migrate→fallback (Phase 6)                                     │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ #: E                                                                    │
     │ Mechanism: Resolve carry-forward (#31)                                  │
     │ File / structure: loop.py _last_deep_hotspots,_last_effective (in-mem   │
     │ lists)                                                                  │
     │ Keying: rule_id / hotspot fp                                            │
     │ Lifetime/TTL: process lifetime                                          │
     │ Gates: merge deep/degraded scans; block false all-clear                 │
     │ Failure mode: restart loses carry → transient false all-clear window    │
     │ Replacement on the case: case.last_evaluated_at vs last_observed_clean; │
     │ absence                                                                 │
     │   never resolves                                                        │
     │ Removal: Replace by observation events (Phase 2); keep in-mem as        │
     │   belt-and-braces until Phase 2 lands                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Additional state discovered (not in the "five"):                        │
     │ - app/proactive/ledger.py daily budget JSON — keep (cost control), but  │
     │ mirror into Postgres for replay.                                        │
     │ - IncidentMemory Redis keys / _LocalIncidentMemory — the durable case   │
     │ store itself; becomes Postgres (D3).                                    │
     │ - app/graph/checkpointing.py LangGraph saver (Redis/in-mem) — becomes   │
     │ Postgres saver (D3).                                                    │
     │ - app/golden_state.py + app/prompts/golden_state_manifest.json — static │
     │ intended-state context (orthogonal; manifest_hash already recorded).    │
     │ - ProactiveMemory lessons/proposals/observations/journal — learning     │
     │ flywheel (keep; bridge to knowledge).                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 3. Proposed Case State Model                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Approach: keep the existing reactive case shape and extend it;          │
     │ introduce a kind discriminator so atomic and meta cases are one durable │
     │ family. Persist in Postgres (D3). Map to existing fields wherever they  │
     │ exist (do not duplicate). The model is owned by the shared CaseService  │
     │ over a CaseStore (app/cases/), not by the loop or the LangGraph graph;  │
     │ introduce typed models in app/cases/models.py and keep dict             │
     │ round-tripping for back-compat during migration.                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ AtomicCase (extends today's _new_case dict)                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Identity (exists): incident_id, case_number, fingerprint, identity,   │
     │ resource_id, title. Add: kind="atomic", origin∈{reactive,proactive},    │
     │ rule_id, detector (proactive rule_id/reactive alertname),               │
     │ customer/site/service (best-effort from labels/topology).               │
     │ - Observation state (add): first_seen(=created_at),                     │
     │ last_seen(=last_event_at), last_observed_unhealthy,                     │
     │ last_observed_clean, last_evaluated_at, last_scan_cycle_id,             │
     │ signal_snapshot(evidence dict), signal_signature(hash of evidence),     │
     │ prev_signal_signature, severity. Absence of evaluation must never set   │
     │ last_observed_clean.                                                    │
     │ - Lifecycle (exists): status, created_at/opened_at, updated_at,         │
     │ recovered_at, plus add resolved_at, closed_at, resolution_reason.       │
     │ - Reporting (add): last_reported_at, last_reported_signature,           │
     │ last_reasserted_at, child_reports_suppressed_count; history via case    │
     │ events.                                                                 │
     │ - Investigation (add): last_investigated_at, last_diagnosis,            │
     │ diagnosis_signature, recommendations, investigation_status,             │
     │ investigation_error, reinvestigate_after, prior_diagnosis_refs,         │
     │ covered_by_meta_case(bool).                                             │
     │ - Handoff (add): issue_url, issue_id, handoff_status, last_handoff_at.  │
     │ - Suppression (add): acknowledged_by, acknowledged_at, snoozed_until,   │
     │ suppressed_until, suppression_reason,                                   │
     │ suppression_source∈{operator,agent}.                                    │
     │ - Learning (add): trace_ids[], feedback_ids[], eval_case_ids[],         │
     │ lesson_ids[], knowledge_citations[] (each: doc_path, doc_id,            │
     │ review_status, section, repo_revision, export_version),                 │
     │ candidate_knowledge_update_ids[], model_chain, prompt_version,          │
     │ policy_version, ruleset_version, tool_version, token_cost,              │
     │ operator_outcome_label, post_resolution_outcome.                        │
     │ - Relationship (exists+extend): downstream_victims, linked_parent_case  │
     │ → reused; add meta_case_id (zero or one active meta-case).              │
     │ - History/schema: append-only case events (exists, case_events); add    │
     │ schema_version.                                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ MetaCase (new kind="meta")                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ - Identity: meta_case_id, event_fingerprint, title, summary,            │
     │ suspected_primary_entity, suspected_site/customer/service,              │
     │ event_type∈{router_down,link_failure,routing_reconvergence,monitoring_f │
     │ ailure,power_event,unknown}.                                            │
     │ - Scope: child_case_ids[] (reuse downstream_victims machinery),         │
     │ notification_ids[], observation_ids[],                                  │
     │ affected_entities/sites/customers/interfaces[], blast_radius_summary.   │
     │ - Correlation: correlation_reason, correlation_confidence,              │
     │ correlation_features[], root_cause_hypothesis, supporting_evidence[],   │
     │ disconfirming_evidence[], manually_attached_by/detached_by,             │
     │ split_from_meta_case_id, merged_into_meta_case_id.                      │
     │ - Lifecycle: status (see §4), opened_at, first_notification_at,         │
     │ last_notification_at, last_child_update_at, stabilized_at, resolved_at, │
     │ closed_at, resolution_reason.                                           │
     │ - Storm: notification_count, child_case_count, peak_rate,               │
     │ storm_started_at, storm_last_seen_at, storm_quiet_since,                │
     │ stabilization_window_until.                                             │
     │ - Investigation/Reporting/Handoff/Learning: event-level mirrors of the  │
     │ atomic fields (event_level_diagnosis, recommended_event_level_action,   │
     │ last_event_reported_at/signature, issue_url/issue_id,                   │
     │ child_issue_urls[], relevant_knowledge_citations[], storm_pattern_id,   │
     │ candidate_knowledge_update_ids[], final_root_cause_label,               │
     │ final_correlation_quality_label).                                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Durable substrate (Postgres tables)                                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Beyond the cases/meta_cases projections, the authoritative store        │
     │ includes an ingestion inbox, an append-only event log, an identity      │
     │ alias registry, a side-effect outbox, and correlation evidence. All     │
     │ writes for one observation happen in one transaction (§7 concurrency).  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ observation_inbox — durable landing zone for every raw webhook /        │
     │ scanner result / notification, so duplicate delivery, retries, source   │
     │ replay, and crash-before-apply are safe: inbox_id, source,              │
     │ source_event_id, source_fingerprint, dedup_key (unique), received_at,   │
     │ payload_ref (or compact raw payload), normalization_status,             │
     │ normalized_observation_id, error, schema_version.                       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ observations — normalized evidence fed to CaseService: observation_id,  │
     │ source, detector (rule/check),                                          │
     │ entity/resource/interface/service/site/customer, severity,              │
     │ status∈{firing,clean,resolved,unknown}, observed_at, received_at,       │
     │ signal_snapshot, signal_signature,                                      │
     │ observation_confidence∈{high,medium,low}, scan_cycle_id?,               │
     │ source_health∈{healthy,degraded,unknown,failed}. A skipped detector     │
     │ produces no row; a clean observation must be explicit (status=clean),   │
     │ never inferred from absence.                                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ case_events — append-only audit/replay truth; cases/meta_cases are      │
     │ query-optimized projections written atomically with the event:          │
     │ event_id, case_id?, meta_case_id?, event_type,                          │
     │ actor_type∈{system,operator,monitor,graph,migration,replay}, actor_id,  │
     │ source, occurred_at, observed_at, correlation_id, causation_id,         │
     │ policy_version, payload, schema_version. (No full event-sourcing        │
     │ required — but every lifecycle-relevant change appends an event, and    │
     │ replay/eval is built from case_events + observations + traces.)         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ case_identity_aliases — resolves fingerprint/identity drift so case_id  │
     │ is stable and fingerprints are matching evidence / compat aliases:      │
     │ alias_id, case_id, alias_type∈{hotspot_fp,alert_fp,source_fp,source_eve │
     │ nt_id,rule_entity,issue_marker,legacy_case_number,external_issue_id},   │
     │ alias_value, source, confidence, created_at, retired_at. Absorbs old    │
     │ investigations.json/suppressions.json keys, GitHub issue markers,       │
     │ Alertmanager/Icinga fingerprints, proactive hotspot fps, legacy case    │
     │ numbers, and future detector/rule renames.                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ side_effect_outbox (see §5) — outbox_id, intent_type∈{report,meta_repor │
     │ t,handoff,knowledge_candidate,issue_comment,discord_update}, case_id?,  │
     │ meta_case_id?, idempotency_key (unique), state_signature, payload,      │
     │ status∈{pending,in_progress,succeeded,failed,abandoned}, attempts,      │
     │ next_attempt_at, created_at, completed_at, external_id/external_url?,   │
     │ error.                                                                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ meta_case_correlation_evidence (see §4) — meta_case_id,                 │
     │ observation_id?, case_id?, evidence_type, feature, value, confidence,   │
     │ source, created_at.                                                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Policy model (versioned)                                                │
     │                                                                         │
     │ All thresholds/TTLs are policy-driven and versioned (new                │
     │ app/cases/policy.py:CasePolicy + policy_version): report-reassert TTL,  │
     │ investigation cooldown, reinvestigate-stale window, storm correlation   │
     │ window, storm confidence threshold, stabilization window, suppression   │
     │ TTL, auto-snooze policy, handoff threshold, knowledge authority filter, │
     │ source-health confidence policy, child-suppression-under-meta-case      │
     │ policy. Every case_event and decision trace records the active          │
     │ policy_version; replay/eval compares behavior by policy_version (§9).   │
     │ This is the single versioned source that replaces the scattered         │
     │ constants in config.py:ProactiveLoopSettings.                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 4. Proposed State Machine                                               │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Implemented in CaseService (over CaseStore) as the single owner of      │
     │ these transitions for both proactive scans and reactive webhooks. The   │
     │ loop, webhook ingress, and the LangGraph graph are clients that submit  │
     │ observations/results and read context — never status.                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Atomic case (reconcile with existing statuses; do not invent a parallel │
     │ enum)                                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Keep investigating → waiting_approval → recovered_pending → resolved,   │
     │ plus expired, linked, and add acknowledged/snoozed as suppression       │
     │ attributes (not lifecycle status) and handed_off as a handoff_status    │
     │ attribute. Key transitions:                                             │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Trigger: Unhealthy observation                                          │
     │ Evidence: rule evaluated unhealthy                                      │
     │ Case writes: last_observed_unhealthy, signal_snapshot/signature,        │
     │ severity; open                                                          │
     │   if new                                                                │
     │ Event: case_observed_unhealthy                                          │
     │ Report?: on open / sev / signature change                               │
     │ Investigate?: yes (if gate)                                             │
     │ Handoff?: if warrants_change                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Clean observation                                              │
     │ Evidence: rule evaluated clean                                          │
     │ Case writes: last_observed_clean, last_evaluated_at                     │
     │ Event: case_observed_clean                                              │
     │ Report?: on transition                                                  │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Skipped rule / no observation                                  │
     │ Evidence: rule not evaluated                                            │
     │ Case writes: last_scan_cycle_id only (optional                          │
     │ case_not_observed_this_cycle) —                                         │
     │   never touch lifecycle                                                 │
     │ Event: low-noise                                                        │
     │ Report?: no                                                             │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: optional                                                        │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Signal changed                                                 │
     │ Evidence: signal_signature≠prev                                         │
     │ Case writes: update snapshot/sev                                        │
     │ Event: case_signal_changed                                              │
     │ Report?: yes                                                            │
     │ Investigate?: re-eligible                                               │
     │ Handoff?: maybe                                                         │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Stale diagnosis                                                │
     │ Evidence: now>reinvestigate_after                                       │
     │ Case writes: —                                                          │
     │ Event: —                                                                │
     │ Report?: no                                                             │
     │ Investigate?: re-eligible                                               │
     │ Handoff?: —                                                             │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Operator ack/snooze/close                                      │
     │ Evidence: operator action                                               │
     │ Case writes: suppression fields / closed_at                             │
     │ Event: case_snoozed/case_closed                                         │
     │ Report?: confirm                                                        │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes (+feedback)                                                 │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Issue created / exists                                         │
     │ Evidence: handoff result                                                │
     │ Case writes: issue_url/issue_id / no-op                                 │
     │ Event: handoff_created_issue / handoff_skipped_existing_issue           │
     │ Report?: maybe                                                          │
     │ Investigate?: —                                                         │
     │ Handoff?: idempotent                                                    │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Suppression expiry                                             │
     │ Evidence: now>suppressed_until                                          │
     │ Case writes: clear fields                                               │
     │ Event: case_suppression_expired                                         │
     │ Report?: re-eligible                                                    │
     │ Investigate?: re-eligible                                               │
     │ Handoff?: —                                                             │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Reassert TTL                                                   │
     │ Evidence: now-last_reported_at≥report_reassert_s                        │
     │ Case writes: last_reasserted_at                                         │
     │ Event: case_reasserted                                                  │
     │ Report?: yes                                                            │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Investigation skipped (same signature)                         │
     │ Evidence: recent diagnosis + unchanged                                  │
     │ Case writes: prior_diagnosis_refs                                       │
     │ Event: investigation_skipped_recent_same_signature                      │
     │ Report?: no                                                             │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: no                                                            │
     │ Trace?: yes                                                             │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: Resolve (positive clean)                                       │
     │ Evidence: clean observation + (recovery cooldown)                       │
     │ Case writes: resolved_at, resolution_reason                             │
     │ Event: case_resolved_positive_clean                                     │
     │ Report?: once                                                           │
     │ Investigate?: no                                                        │
     │ Handoff?: close issue                                                   │
     │ Trace?: yes → lesson candidate                                          │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Trigger: False positive / false all-clear                               │
     │ Evidence: operator label                                                │
     │ Case writes: operator_outcome_label                                     │
     │ Event: operator_feedback_recorded                                       │
     │ Report?: maybe                                                          │
     │ Investigate?: —                                                         │
     │ Handoff?: —                                                             │
     │ Trace?: yes → eval + candidate                                          │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Invariant (subsumes #31): resolve requires positive clean observation   │
     │ (proactive) or recovery event + RECOVERY_COOLDOWN_SECONDS (reactive) or │
     │ operator close or an explicit, named stale policy. Absence from a scan  │
     │ set, a skipped deep rule, or a degraded scan must not resolve or        │
     │ all-clear.                                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Meta-case states                                                        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ candidate_event → active_event → investigating_event →                  │
     │ monitoring_recovery → stabilized → resolved → closed, plus split /      │
     │ merged. Transitions per the prompt; enforced rules: (a) active_event    │
     │ only when correlation confidence ≥ threshold or operator-confirmed; (b) │
     │ monitoring_recovery → stabilized only after all required positive       │
     │ clean observations or a stability window with no recurrence; (c) a      │
     │ meta-case must not resolve merely because notifications stopped — root  │
     │ child stays active while the asset is down; (d) child cases may resolve │
     │ individually while the meta-case persists.                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Meta-case correlation (deterministic-first, LLM-second)                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ CorrelationService groups via layered evidence, each layer written to   │
     │ meta_case_correlation_evidence; the LLM is explanatory only and is      │
     │ never the sole authority for durable attach/detach:                     │
     │                                                                         │
     │ 1. Source-native: Alertmanager group labels, Icinga host/service        │
     │ relationships, source fingerprints, firing/clear pairs.                 │
     │ 2. Topology/dependency: same router/switch/site/customer/service,       │
     │ parent/child (topology_parents/infra:parent:*), upstream/downstream,    │
     │ interface bundle/LAG, circuit, peer, route adjacency.                   │
     │ 3. Temporal storm heuristics: burst windows, peak rate, notification    │
     │ sequence, simultaneous fire/clear patterns.                             │
     │ 4. Approved hyrule-knowledge patterns: known reconvergence windows,     │
     │ router/link/site failure runbooks, monitoring-cascade notes,            │
     │ customer/site patterns (retrieved + cited per §6).                      │
     │ 5. LLM hypothesis: grouping/root-cause proposal only; cannot by itself  │
     │ create durable attach/detach.                                           │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Every attach records correlation_reason, correlation_confidence, and    │
     │ correlation_features.                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Child suppression under a meta-case (reversible, evidence-based)        │
     │                                                                         │
     │ An attached child may carry covered_by_meta_case=true,                  │
     │ independent_action_required=false,                                      │
     │ child_report_suppressed_reason="explained_by_meta_case". It must become │
     │ independently reportable/investigable again when any of: severity       │
     │ increases; signal materially changes; child persists after the          │
     │ meta-case stabilizes; a new customer/site/service is affected; the      │
     │ root-cause hypothesis is rejected; operator marks                       │
     │ independent_action_required; correlation confidence drops below         │
     │ threshold; the child no longer fits the meta-case evidence. (Tests per  │
     │ §8.)                                                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Source-health / monitoring-failure awareness                            │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Storms can come from the network or from monitoring itself.             │
     │ Observations carry source_health + observation_confidence; meta-cases   │
     │ support event_type=monitoring_failure. Rules: if                        │
     │ source_health∈{degraded,failed}, absence of alerts or sudden clears is  │
     │ not strong clean evidence and lowers auto-resolution confidence; a      │
     │ monitoring-region failure can itself open a meta-case; clean            │
     │ observations are source-aware and detector-aware. (Tests:               │
     │ monitoring-system outage; source-degraded false all-clear prevention.)  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ ---                                                                     │
     │ 5. Stage-by-Stage Refactor Plan                                         │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Layering (the spine). The authoritative state machine lives in a new    │
     │ shared case/correlation service — app/cases/service.py:CaseService and  │
     │ app/cases/correlation.py:CorrelationService, over                       │
     │ app/cases/store.py:CaseStore (Postgres). Everything else is a thin      │
     │ client:                                                                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Component: app/proactive/loop.py:ProactiveLoop                          │
     │ Role: Deterministic runtime/scheduler: paces cycles, runs scanners,     │
     │ builds the                                                              │
     │   CycleSnapshot, may invoke NOCDutyOfficerAgent, drives work. Side      │
     │ effects  run                                                            │
     │    via outbox workers, not the loop. No durable decision state.         │
     │ Writes case truth?: No — calls CaseService                              │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Component: app/main.py:/webhook/* (reactive)                            │
     │ Role: Ingress: normalizes notifications                                 │
     │ Writes case truth?: No — calls CaseService.observe_notification         │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Component: app/graph/* (LangGraph)                                      │
     │ Role: Investigation consumer/producer: reads case+meta-case+knowledge   │
     │ context,                                                                │
     │   returns a structured InvestigationResult                              │
     │ Writes case truth?: No — results applied via                            │
     │   CaseService.record_investigation_result                               │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Component: app/cases/service.py:CaseService                             │
     │ Role: Owns lifecycle, observation truth, reporting dedup, investigation │
     │ reuse,                                                                  │
     │   suppression, handoff idempotency, resolve                             │
     │ Writes case truth?: Yes (sole owner)                                    │
     │ ────────────────────────────────────────                                │
     │ Component: app/cases/correlation.py:CorrelationService                  │
     │ Role: Owns storm detection + meta-case                                  │
     │   create/attach/detach/merge/split/stabilize                            │
     │ Writes case truth?: Yes (sole owner)                                    │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Both proactive scan observations and reactive webhook alerts enter      │
     │ through the same CaseService.observe* API and the same                  │
     │ CorrelationService — one concern, one record. The LangGraph graph never │
     │ flips case status/suppression/handoff/resolve/correlation; today's      │
     │ in-graph correlate_and_dedupe and intake-driven status transitions move │
     │ into the service. Each stage is therefore a service interaction (loop   │
     │ = caller):                                                              │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Observe / scan — the loop scans, then writes each result to the durable │
     │ observation_inbox (idempotent on dedup_key); a normalizer produces      │
     │ observations that CaseService.observe(...) applies in one transaction   │
     │ (unhealthy/clean). A skipped rule writes no inbox row → no clean        │
     │ observation. The service maps the observation to a case, appends an     │
     │ observation event, updates last_observed_*/signal_signature, and        │
     │ decides lifecycle. This replaces the loop's _merge_with_carried carry   │
     │ (E): a deep rule not scanned has no fresh clean observation, so its     │
     │ case stays active in the service — no in-memory list, preserving #31.   │
     │ Observation events are the replay/eval substrate (§9).                  │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Rank / gate — governance.evaluate_gate becomes a pure function over     │
     │ CaseService.eligible(...) (status/severity/signal_signature/suppression │
     │ /handoff/reinvestigate_after); suppressed/handed-off/recently-diagnosed │
     │ cases drop out without losing visibility. Relevant hyrule-knowledge     │
     │ (§6) and ProactiveMemory patterns are advisory inputs only. The loop    │
     │ drives the budgeted subset (kicks off investigations); side effects     │
     │ still run via the outbox, and the service records the gate trace.       │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Investigate — the loop asks CaseService.eligible_for_investigation();   │
     │ for each it runs the LangGraph graph as a consumer (seeded by the       │
     │ service with prior diagnosis + knowledge citations) and hands the       │
     │ structured result back via CaseService.record_investigation_result().   │
     │ The skip/reuse decision (recent last_investigated_at and                │
     │ diagnosis_signature==signal_signature; replaces B/investigations.json)  │
     │ and the investigation_skipped_recent_same_signature trace live in the   │
     │ service, not the loop or graph. Result schema: root cause, confidence,  │
     │ supporting/disconfirming evidence, citations, recommended actions,      │
     │ escalation, unresolved questions, model/prompt/policy versions, token   │
     │ cost.                                                                   │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Report — CaseService.report_decisions(cycle) returns report-worthy      │
     │ transitions (open/sev/status/material-signal/reassert-TTL/resolution/ha │
     │ ndoff/suppression/recommendation-change) and owns last_reported_*       │
     │ (replaces A). It enqueues a side_effect_outbox report intent            │
     │ (idempotency report:{case_id}:{state_signature}) inside the             │
     │ transaction; an outbox worker renders + sends and records the result    │
     │ via CaseService.mark_reported(...) — a crash/retry never double-posts.  │
     │ Child reports under an active meta-case are suppressed by               │
     │ CorrelationService. Each report trace links case state, signals, reused │
     │ diagnosis, knowledge citations, and versions; operator                  │
     │ accept/ignore/correct/reject attaches back as feedback.                 │
     │                                                                         │
     │ Handoff — CaseService.handoff_intent(case) returns create/comment/skip  │
