     Case-Grounded Self-Learning Loop Refactor Plan

     Context

     Why this change. The NOC Agent's proactive loop
     (hyrule-noc-agent/app/proactive/loop.py) re-derives state every cycle (scan
     → rank → gate → investigate → report → handoff/resolve) and has accreted
     five separate anti-duplication side stores to stop flapping, duplicate
     reports, duplicate tickets, and false all-clears. None of them share one
     notion of "the current state of a concern," and — critically — they are
     keyed by hotspot fingerprint (sha256(rule_id|key)[:16],
     models.py:Hotspot.fingerprint) while the durable case is keyed by
     alert-identity fingerprint (incident_memory.py:fingerprint_alert). The
     proactive loop therefore makes its don't-duplicate decisions outside the
     case.

     Meanwhile the reactive path already has the state machine we want:
     IncidentMemory (app/incident_memory.py) keeps durable cases with a real
     lifecycle, parent↔child topology linking, and
     resolve-only-on-positive-recovery semantics. The refactor's thesis — the 
     case is the authoritative state machine — is already half-true; we must
     extend the case to own the proactive stages too, add meta-cases for
     notification storms, and wire a replayable, governed hyrule-knowledge 
     learning loop so institutional NOC judgment survives a model swap.

     Targets (confirmed cross-repo). This plan is implemented against:
     - /home/svag/Dev/hyrule-noc-agent (remote AS215932/noc-agent) — the loop,
     cases, side stores.
     - /home/svag/Dev/knowledge (remote AS215932/knowledge) — the institutional
     repo the prompt calls "hyrule-knowledge".

     Confirmed decisions shaping this plan:
     1. Proceed cross-repo now; this plan file stays in the current project.
     2. Sequence: preserve #31 → operational consolidation (5 side stores onto
     the case) → meta-cases/storms → knowledge loop.
     3. Postgres is the authoritative production backend for IncidentMemory,
     meta-cases, observations, case events, handoffs, suppressions, feedback,
     trace references, and LangGraph checkpoints. Redis/Valkey is optional 
     hot-path only (queues, pub/sub, short-lived dedup/rate-limit windows, storm
     correlation). No production behavior may silently depend on Redis as a
     second source of truth.
     4. Knowledge retrieval is export-authoritative + replayable: production
     correlation/investigation reads a pinned deterministic SQLite/JSONL export
     of hyrule-knowledge; the knowledge MCP server is optional noc-role 
     enrichment only. Every trace records the exact document path, document id, 
     approval status, section, and repo revision / export version used.

     Architectural principle (ownership). The ProactiveLoop is demoted to a 
     scheduler/orchestrator — it paces cycles, runs scanners, builds the
     CycleSnapshot, and drives work — side effects execute via outbox workers,
     not the loop — but owns no durable case lifecycle. It may invoke an
     advisory NOCDutyOfficerAgent (see Agentic Orchestration Layer) that only
     proposes. The authoritative state machine lives in a shared 
     case/correlation service layer (CaseService/CorrelationService over a
     CaseStore) used identically by proactive scan observations and reactive
     webhook alerts, so there is one notion of a concern. LangGraph
     investigation is a consumer of case/meta-case/knowledge context and a
     producer of structured investigation results — it must not own case status,
     suppression, handoff, resolve, reporting dedup, or correlation truth. Do
     not bury any of that in the loop or the graph.

     Discrepancies vs. the original prompt (repo wins):
     - OKF, not ODF. hyrule-knowledge stores Markdown + YAML frontmatter with
     deterministic JSONL/SQLite exports (knowledge/okf/,
     knowledge/exports/knowledge.sqlite). There are no .odt/.ods/.fodt files.
     "Candidate ODF artifact" → OKF concept + learning_ledger_v1 JSON event.
     - Cases are not on-disk files. NOC-20260617-006 is a case_number display
     string; cases live in Redis (prod today) or in-memory (dev/test). We are
     moving authority to Postgres.
     - #31 is already merged to main (234a92d, ee55528). We preserve it, not
     re-merge it. The reactive path already embodies its principle (resolve only
     on positive recovery + cooldown).
     - No meta-cases exist today — but parent/child linking +
     IncidentMemory.correlate() are the seed.
     - ProactiveMemory is already non-authoritative
     (lessons/proposals/observations/journal) — it does not need demoting, only
     wiring into the knowledge promotion bridge.

     ---
     Architecture Invariants

     Hard rules every PR and test must enforce (mirrored in §8 boundary tests
     and §13 acceptance):

     - ProactiveLoop may orchestrate cycles, run scanners, call services, and do
     scheduled work — it must not own durable case lifecycle state.
     - LangGraph may investigate and return structured InvestigationResult
     objects — it must not mutate case status, suppression, handoff, resolve,
     report-dedup, or correlation truth.
     - Reporters may render/send notifications only from CaseService report 
     intents (via the outbox).
     - Handoff code may create/update external issues only from CaseService 
     handoff intents (via the outbox).
     - CaseService is the only owner of atomic case lifecycle state.
     - CorrelationService is the only owner of meta-case grouping,
     attach/detach, merge/split, and storm lifecycle state.
     - CaseStore/Postgres is the authoritative production state store.
     - Any Redis/Valkey use is optional and transient only (hot-path
     cache/queue/dedup-window) — never a second source of truth.
     - No new JSON/file/local-cache side store may become an anti-duplication
     mechanism.
     - ProactiveLoop is a deterministic agent runtime/orchestrator, not an
     agentic state owner; it may invoke NOCDutyOfficerAgent to produce planning
     proposals.
     - NOCDutyOfficerAgent must not directly mutate case lifecycle, suppression,
     handoff, resolve, reporting, correlation, or knowledge-authority state.
     All its outputs are proposals.
     - CaseService validates atomic-case proposals before they become
     case_events/outbox intents; CorrelationService validates meta-case,
     storm-correlation, attach/detach, merge/split, and stabilization proposals
     likewise.
     - Knowledge-authority filters validate knowledge citations before any agent
     recommendation may rely on them.
     - Side effects still happen only through the Side-Effect Outbox.
     - Agent failure, timeout, or disabled mode must not stop the deterministic 
     safe baseline loop. (This is an additive reasoning layer, not a replacement
     for deterministic state-machine ownership.)

     ---
     Agentic Orchestration Layer

     ProactiveLoop stays a deterministic runtime/clock/worker/supervisor; it may
     host an agentic planning stage that invokes the NOCDutyOfficerAgent, but
     the agent only proposes — deterministic services remain the law.

     ▎ NOCDutyOfficerAgent is the senior-engineer brain. 
     ▎ CaseService/CorrelationService are the law. Outbox workers are the hands.
     ▎ hyrule-knowledge is the institution. Replay/evals are the memory of 
     ▎ whether the brain is improving.

     Role profile (persona, not authority): Senior Network / Service Reliability
     Engineer — prefer Senior Network Reliability Engineer / Senior SRE 
     (Network Reliability) for ISP/NOC contexts; NOC shift lead.

     Mission: act like the senior engineer on NOC duty — read current
     case/meta-case state, understand what changed, recognize notification
     storms, retrieve+use approved hyrule-knowledge, decide what deserves
     attention, propose a safe CyclePlan, surface uncertainty, and ask for
     operator approval when needed.

     Authority — advisory/planning only. It never directly mutates operational
     truth: never resolves, suppresses, marks reported, creates tickets,
     attaches/detaches child cases, or promotes knowledge. All outputs are
     proposals.

     Validation. CaseService, CorrelationService, the KnowledgeAuthorityFilter,
     and the PolicyGuard validate every proposed action against deterministic
     policy, current case/meta-case state, positive-clean evidence rules,
     idempotency rules, source-health rules, and knowledge-authority rules.

     Repo consistency: builds on the existing app/agents/ package (today
     mail.py, triage.py) and app/model_config.py (FallbackModel, model_chain);
     the investigation graph's existing routing (supervisor_route, specialist
     routing) is the seed for InvestigationAgent.

     Deployment modes

     - disabled: deterministic policy only; agent not invoked.
     - shadow: agent produces CyclePlan proposals recorded to traces/evals; no
     side effects or state changes from the plan.
     - advise: proposals visible to operators; operators may approve/act
     manually; no automatic side effects.
     - guarded_act: proposals may create CaseService/CorrelationService intents
     only after deterministic validation; side effects still run via the outbox.
     - manual_only: every agent-proposed side effect requires operator approval.

     Initial rollout disabled → shadow → advise → guarded_act. Do not skip
     shadow; do not enable guarded_act until replay/eval metrics pass.

     Agent planning data contracts

     Conceptual typed contracts (plan, not code). Only ValidatedIntent may
     create case_events or outbox rows.

     - CycleSnapshot (frozen input): cycle_id, observed_at, policy_version,
     knowledge_export_version, model_chain, prompt_version, budget_state,
     new_observations, active_atomic_cases, active_meta_cases,
     recently_resolved_cases, suppressed_cases, cases_in_monitoring_recovery,
     handoff_state, investigation_freshness, source_health_summary,
     recent_operator_feedback, retrieved_hyrule_knowledge, prior_cycle_summary,
     open_outbox_intents, uncertainty_flags. (Extends today's DecisionContext.)
     - CyclePlan (agent output): cycle_id, plan_id, agent_role_profile,
     policy_version, knowledge_export_version, priority_order, proposed_actions,
     storm_hypotheses, root_cause_hypotheses, investigation_plans,
     report_recommendations, handoff_recommendations,
     suppression_recommendations, operator_questions,
     knowledge_candidate_recommendations, reasoning_summary,
     uncertainty_summary, knowledge_citations, confidence, token_cost,
     tool_calls.
     - ActionIntent (one proposal): intent_id, intent_type∈{investigate,report,h
     andoff,suppress,ack,ask_operator,attach_child_to_meta_case,detach_child_fro
     m_meta_case,merge_meta_cases,split_meta_case,mark_independent_action_requir
     ed,set_root_cause_hypothesis,create_knowledge_candidate}, target_case_id,
     target_meta_case_id, rationale, evidence_refs, observation_refs,
     case_event_refs, knowledge_citations, confidence,
     requires_operator_approval, idempotency_key.
     - ValidatedIntent (service output): intent_id,
     validation_status∈{accepted,rejected,requires_operator_approval},
     rejection_reason, validator∈{CaseService,CorrelationService,KnowledgeAuthor
     ityFilter,PolicyGuard}, committed_case_event_id, outbox_id,
     created_trace_id.

     Rule: the agent emits CyclePlan; services produce ValidatedIntent; only
     ValidatedIntent creates case_events/outbox rows.

     Agent Role Model

     Role profiles/interfaces — the first implementation is one 
     NOCDutyOfficerAgent invoking role-specific internal prompts/tools; split
     into separate agents only when isolation improves reliability, testing, or
     replay. None write truth directly.

     Role: NOCDutyOfficerAgent
     Human analogue: Senior NRE/SRE, NOC shift lead
     Purpose: Top-level planning brain; prioritize cases/meta-cases; produce
       CyclePlan
     Writes truth?: No
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Role: EventCorrelationAgent
     Human analogue: Event/storm analyst
     Purpose: Detect storms/cascades; propose meta-case grouping, parent/root,
     blast
       radius, confidence
     Writes truth?: No — CorrelationService validates
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Role: TopologyAnalystAgent
     Human analogue: Network topology engineer
     Purpose: Reason over
       routers/switches/POPs/sites/circuits/peers/dependencies/reconvergence +
       affected customers/services
     Writes truth?: No
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Role: InvestigationAgent
     Human analogue: Incident investigator
     Purpose: Deep diagnosis from case state + prior diagnosis + tools +
     approved
       knowledge; return InvestigationResult
     Writes truth?: No — CaseService records if valid
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Role: KnowledgeLibrarianAgent
     Human analogue: Runbook/knowledge engineer
     Purpose: Retrieve approved hyrule-knowledge from pinned export; label
       candidate/deprecated/stale; ensure full citations
     Writes truth?: No
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Role: SourceHealthAgent
     Human analogue: Monitoring reliability engineer
     Purpose: Classify sources healthy/degraded/failed/uncertain; block
     unreliable
       clears/missing alerts/outages as clean evidence
     Writes truth?: No — CaseService applies policy
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Role: IncidentScribeAgent
     Human analogue: Incident comms lead
     Purpose: Draft reports / handoff summaries / reassertions / timelines /
       resolution summaries
     Writes truth?: No — does not decide to send
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Role: EscalationCoordinatorAgent
     Human analogue: Escalation/routing lead
     Purpose: Propose handoff yes/no, route, title/body, labels, severity,
       escalation target
     Writes truth?: No — CaseService validates
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Role: ChangeContextAgent
     Human analogue: Change/maintenance coordinator
     Purpose: Check known maintenance, planned changes, expected reconvergence
       windows, maintenance suppressions, change-induced storms
     Writes truth?: No
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Role: LearningCuratorAgent
     Human analogue: Postmortem/knowledge curator
     Purpose: Convert resolved/operator-confirmed cases into sanitized
     review-gated
       learning_ledger_v1 candidates
     Writes truth?: No — never promotes directly
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Role: PolicyGuardAgent
     Human analogue: Safety/reliability reviewer
     Purpose: Check proposals vs invariants (no resolve w/o positive clean; no
     dup
       handoff when issue_url/issue_id exists; no authoritative use of
       deprecated/candidate knowledge; no hidden child when independent action
       required; no non-authoritative production fallback; no source-degraded
     clear)
     Writes truth?: Prefer deterministic validation; LLM may explain, not
     override
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Role: ReplayEvalAgent
     Human analogue: Eval analyst
     Purpose: Offline-only comparison of traces, policy/prompt/model variants,
       replay fixtures
     Writes truth?: Offline only

     ---
     1. Current Architecture Map

     Entry points / orchestration

     - Mount: app/main.py:lifespan constructs ProactiveLoop(...) and calls
     .start() (singleton-guarded by _try_acquire_proactive_lock). The loop is a
     bare asyncio task (loop.py:_run → run_once), not LangGraph. LangGraph
     (app/graph/) is used only inside an investigation.
     - Reactive ingress: app/main.py POST /webhook/alertmanager and POST 
     /webhook/icinga (_icinga_to_alert_payload) → graph_runtime.intake_alert() →
     IncidentMemory.intake_alert() → investigation graph.
     - Per cycle: loop.py:run_once → scan → _merge_with_carried → _auto_snooze →
     _apply_suppressions → build_decision_context → evaluate_gate →
     _investigate → update_ledger → _persist_memory → _safe_report.

     Stage functions / classes

     ┌────────────┬────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
     │   Stage    │                            Code                            │
     ├────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
     │ Scan /     │ app/proactive/scanner.py:scan, ScanContext;                │
     │ hotspots   │ DEEP_RULE_IDS={"disk_fill","tls_expiry"};                  │
     │            │ models.py:Hotspot                                          │
     ├────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
     │ Rank /     │ app/proactive/governance.py:eligible_hotspots,             │
     │ gate       │ evaluate_gate, GateDecision;                               │
     │            │ build_decision_context→models.py:DecisionContext           │
     ├────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
     │ Investigat │ loop.py:_investigate;                                      │
     │ e          │ app/proactive/investigate.py:build_investigator (wraps the │
     │            │  graph via synthetic alert)                                │
     ├────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
     │ Report     │ loop.py:_report_decision, _safe_report, _default_report,   │
     │            │ _hotspot_field, _case_for_hotspot                          │
     ├────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
     │ Handoff    │ app/proactive/handoff.py:GitHubHandoff.ensure_candidate_is │
     │            │ sue (issue #-marker search)                                │
     ├────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
     │ Resolve /  │ loop.py:_merge_with_carried + _report_decision             │
     │ all-clear  │ (proactive); incident_memory.py:_expire_*_cases (reactive) │
     ├────────────┼────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
     │ Snooze /   │ app/proactive/suppressions.py:SuppressionStore;            │
     │ ack /      │ loop.py:_apply_suppressions, _auto_snooze;                 │
     │ suppress   │ app/icinga_ack.py                                          │
     └────────────┴────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘

     Memory / state

     - IncidentMemory (app/incident_memory.py): Redis or in-memory
     _LocalIncidentMemory. Case dict from _new_case (incident_id, case_number,
     fingerprint, identity, resource_id, status, downstream_victims,
     linked_parent_case, recovered_at, latest_transition, event_count,
     source_excerpt, …). Indices: fingerprint_index, case_number_index,
     resource_open_cases, topology_parents, noc:case:expiry zset. Statuses:
     OPEN_CASE_STATUSES={investigating,waiting_approval,recovered_pending} plus
     resolved/expired/linked.
     - ProactiveMemory (app/proactive/memory.py): lessons/ (md), proposals/
     (CandidateLesson json), observations.jsonl, journal/. A learning flywheel
     (evaluate_outcomes), not operational truth — correct already.
     - Budget ledger (app/proactive/ledger.py): per-day ledger-{day}.json
     (cycles/investigations/cost/handoffs) — cost control, not learning.

     Fingerprint logic

     - Hotspot: models.py:Hotspot.fingerprint = sha256(f"{rule_id}|{key}")[:16].
     - Case: incident_memory.py:fingerprint_alert(payload)=sha256(alert_identity
     (payload)). A hotspot becomes a case via models.py:hotspot_to_alert_payload
     (source="proactive") → intake_alert. The two keyspaces never meet except
     in loop.py:_case_for_hotspot (advisory digest linking).

     Eval / trace / feedback / model abstraction (what exists)

     - Decision context: models.py:DecisionContext (decision_id, cycle_id,
     manifest_hash, ruleset_version, model_chain, budget_state,
     injected_lesson_ids) — built per cycle, but only decision_id is persisted
     (onto the report); no queryable trace store.
     - Journal/observations: per-cycle journal/{cycle_id}.md +
     observations.jsonl + evaluate_outcomes (predictions vs reactive alerts).
     - Feedback: graph_runtime.record_operator_decision via Discord /noc_decide,
     web POST /control/incidents/{id}/decision, app/nocctl.py.
     - Model abstraction: app/model_config.py (AgentModelConfig, FallbackModel,
     active_model_chain), app/model_metrics.py (token usage, fallback counters).
     Versioned via ruleset_version, manifest_hash, model_chain. No
     prompt_version/policy_version yet.
     - Knowledge integration: fixtures only — app/knowledge_shadow.py validates
     evals/knowledge_shadow/ context-pack + learning_ledger_v1 fixtures. No live
     retrieval, no live promotion.

     hyrule-knowledge (current)

     OKF Markdown + YAML frontmatter under okf/{curated,generated,observed};
     deterministic exports exports/{knowledge.sqlite,*.jsonl,manifest.json};
     schema/{frontmatter,learning-event,…}.schema.json; knowledge-policy.yml
     (roles incl. noc_shadow); ledger/{fixtures,proposed,reviews};
     src/hyrule_knowledge/{retrieval,context_pack,store,learning_ledger,promotio
     n,policy,mcp_server}.py; CI request-promotion/ingest open review-gated PRs
     (never auto-merge). Authority tiers A0–A5.

     ---
     2. Existing Side-Store Inventory

     #: A
     Mechanism: Report dedup
     File / structure: loop.py _last_report_signature,_last_report_ts (in-mem
       frozenset[(fp,sev)])
     Keying: hotspot fp+sev
     Lifetime/TTL: process lifetime; reassert report_reassert_s=3600
     Gates: whether to post digest
     Failure mode: restart loses dedup → re-post; per-cycle set jitter
     Replacement on the case: case.last_reported_signature/at,
     last_reasserted_at;
       report-worthiness derived from case transitions
     Removal: Migrate (Phase 3)
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     #: B
     Mechanism: Investigation cooldown
     File / structure: investigations.json {fp:ts}
       (_recent_investigation_fps/_record_investigations)
     Keying: hotspot fp
     Lifetime/TTL: investigation_cooldown_s=21600
     Gates: skip re-investigation
     Failure mode: file loss → re-investigate; not case-aware
     Replacement on the case: case.last_investigated_at + diagnosis_signature +
       reinvestigate_after
     Removal: Migrate→remove (Phase 4)
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     #: C
     Mechanism: Handoff idempotency
     File / structure: handoff.py GitHub search for body marker
       proactive-fingerprint:{fp} + label loop:candidate
     Keying: hotspot fp (in issue body)
     Lifetime/TTL: GitHub lifetime
     Gates: create vs refresh issue
     Failure mode: GitHub search miss/rate-limit → dup issue; no local record
     Replacement on the case: case.issue_url/issue_id/handoff_status; marker
     search
       demoted to fallback
     Removal: Migrate→fallback (Phase 5)
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     #: D
     Mechanism: Suppression
     File / structure: suppressions.json via SuppressionStore
     Keying: hotspot fp prefix
     Lifetime/TTL: expires_at (timed) or until-resolved
     Gates: drop from digest+investigation
     Failure mode: file is the only record; not on case; prefix matching
     Replacement on the case:
     case.suppressed_until/snoozed_until/suppression_source/reason
       + suppression events
     Removal: Migrate→fallback (Phase 6)
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     #: E
     Mechanism: Resolve carry-forward (#31)
     File / structure: loop.py _last_deep_hotspots,_last_effective (in-mem
     lists)
     Keying: rule_id / hotspot fp
     Lifetime/TTL: process lifetime
     Gates: merge deep/degraded scans; block false all-clear
     Failure mode: restart loses carry → transient false all-clear window
     Replacement on the case: case.last_evaluated_at vs last_observed_clean;
     absence
       never resolves
     Removal: Replace by observation events (Phase 2); keep in-mem as
       belt-and-braces until Phase 2 lands

     Additional state discovered (not in the "five"):
     - app/proactive/ledger.py daily budget JSON — keep (cost control), but
     mirror into Postgres for replay.
     - IncidentMemory Redis keys / _LocalIncidentMemory — the durable case store
     itself; becomes Postgres (D3).
     - app/graph/checkpointing.py LangGraph saver (Redis/in-mem) — becomes
     Postgres saver (D3).
     - app/golden_state.py + app/prompts/golden_state_manifest.json — static
     intended-state context (orthogonal; manifest_hash already recorded).
     - ProactiveMemory lessons/proposals/observations/journal — learning
     flywheel (keep; bridge to knowledge).

     ---
     3. Proposed Case State Model

     Approach: keep the existing reactive case shape and extend it; introduce a
     kind discriminator so atomic and meta cases are one durable family. Persist
     in Postgres (D3). Map to existing fields wherever they exist (do not
     duplicate). The model is owned by the shared CaseService over a CaseStore
     (app/cases/), not by the loop or the LangGraph graph; introduce typed
     models in app/cases/models.py and keep dict round-tripping for back-compat
     during migration.

     AtomicCase (extends today's _new_case dict)

     - Identity (exists): incident_id, case_number, fingerprint, identity,
     resource_id, title. Add: kind="atomic", origin∈{reactive,proactive},
     rule_id, detector (proactive rule_id/reactive alertname),
     customer/site/service (best-effort from labels/topology).
     - Observation state (add): first_seen(=created_at),
     last_seen(=last_event_at), last_observed_unhealthy, last_observed_clean,
     last_evaluated_at, last_scan_cycle_id, signal_snapshot(evidence dict),
     signal_signature(hash of evidence), prev_signal_signature, severity.
     Absence of evaluation must never set last_observed_clean.
     - Lifecycle (exists): status, created_at/opened_at, updated_at,
     recovered_at, plus add resolved_at, closed_at, resolution_reason.
     - Reporting (add): last_reported_at, last_reported_signature,
     last_reasserted_at, child_reports_suppressed_count; history via case
     events.
     - Investigation (add): last_investigated_at, last_diagnosis,
     diagnosis_signature, recommendations, investigation_status,
     investigation_error, reinvestigate_after, prior_diagnosis_refs,
     covered_by_meta_case(bool).
     - Handoff (add): issue_url, issue_id, handoff_status, last_handoff_at.
     - Suppression (add): acknowledged_by, acknowledged_at, snoozed_until,
     suppressed_until, suppression_reason, suppression_source∈{operator,agent}.
     - Learning (add): trace_ids[], feedback_ids[], eval_case_ids[],
     lesson_ids[], knowledge_citations[] (each: doc_path, doc_id, review_status,
     section, repo_revision, export_version), candidate_knowledge_update_ids[],
     model_chain, prompt_version, policy_version, ruleset_version,
     tool_version, token_cost, operator_outcome_label, post_resolution_outcome.
     - Relationship (exists+extend): downstream_victims, linked_parent_case →
     reused; add meta_case_id (zero or one active meta-case).
     - History/schema: append-only case events (exists, case_events); add
     schema_version.

     MetaCase (new kind="meta")

     - Identity: meta_case_id, event_fingerprint, title, summary,
     suspected_primary_entity, suspected_site/customer/service,
     event_type∈{router_down,link_failure,routing_reconvergence,monitoring_failu
     re,power_event,unknown}.
     - Scope: child_case_ids[] (reuse downstream_victims machinery),
     notification_ids[], observation_ids[],
     affected_entities/sites/customers/interfaces[], blast_radius_summary.
     - Correlation: correlation_reason, correlation_confidence,
     correlation_features[], root_cause_hypothesis, supporting_evidence[],
     disconfirming_evidence[], manually_attached_by/detached_by,
     split_from_meta_case_id, merged_into_meta_case_id.
     - Lifecycle: status (see §4), opened_at, first_notification_at,
     last_notification_at, last_child_update_at, stabilized_at, resolved_at,
     closed_at, resolution_reason.
     - Storm: notification_count, child_case_count, peak_rate, storm_started_at,
     storm_last_seen_at, storm_quiet_since, stabilization_window_until.
     - Investigation/Reporting/Handoff/Learning: event-level mirrors of the
     atomic fields (event_level_diagnosis, recommended_event_level_action,
     last_event_reported_at/signature, issue_url/issue_id, child_issue_urls[],
     relevant_knowledge_citations[], storm_pattern_id,
     candidate_knowledge_update_ids[], final_root_cause_label,
     final_correlation_quality_label).

     Durable substrate (Postgres tables)

     Beyond the cases/meta_cases projections, the authoritative store includes
     an ingestion inbox, an append-only event log, an identity alias registry, a
     side-effect outbox, and correlation evidence. All writes for one
     observation happen in one transaction (§7 concurrency).

     observation_inbox — durable landing zone for every raw webhook / scanner
     result / notification, so duplicate delivery, retries, source replay, and
     crash-before-apply are safe: inbox_id, source, source_event_id,
     source_fingerprint, dedup_key (unique), received_at, payload_ref (or
     compact raw payload), normalization_status, normalized_observation_id,
     error, schema_version.

     observations — normalized evidence fed to CaseService: observation_id,
     source, detector (rule/check),
     entity/resource/interface/service/site/customer, severity,
     status∈{firing,clean,resolved,unknown}, observed_at, received_at,
     signal_snapshot, signal_signature,
     observation_confidence∈{high,medium,low}, scan_cycle_id?,
     source_health∈{healthy,degraded,unknown,failed}. A skipped detector 
     produces no row; a clean observation must be explicit (status=clean), never
     inferred from absence.

     case_events — append-only audit/replay truth; cases/meta_cases are
     query-optimized projections written atomically with the event: event_id,
     case_id?, meta_case_id?, event_type,
     actor_type∈{system,operator,monitor,graph,migration,replay}, actor_id,
     source, occurred_at, observed_at, correlation_id, causation_id,
     policy_version, payload, schema_version. (No full event-sourcing required —
     but every lifecycle-relevant change appends an event, and replay/eval is
     built from case_events + observations + traces.)

     case_identity_aliases — resolves fingerprint/identity drift so case_id is 
     stable and fingerprints are matching evidence / compat aliases: alias_id,
     case_id, alias_type∈{hotspot_fp,alert_fp,source_fp,source_event_id,rule_ent
     ity,issue_marker,legacy_case_number,external_issue_id}, alias_value,
     source, confidence, created_at, retired_at. Absorbs old
     investigations.json/suppressions.json keys, GitHub issue markers,
     Alertmanager/Icinga fingerprints, proactive hotspot fps, legacy case
     numbers, and future detector/rule renames.

     side_effect_outbox (see §5) — outbox_id, intent_type∈{report,meta_report,ha
     ndoff,knowledge_candidate,issue_comment,discord_update}, case_id?,
     meta_case_id?, idempotency_key (unique), state_signature, payload,
     status∈{pending,in_progress,succeeded,failed,abandoned}, attempts,
     next_attempt_at, created_at, completed_at, external_id/external_url?,
     error.

     meta_case_correlation_evidence (see §4) — meta_case_id, observation_id?,
     case_id?, evidence_type, feature, value, confidence, source, created_at.

     Policy model (versioned)

     All thresholds/TTLs are policy-driven and versioned (new
     app/cases/policy.py:CasePolicy + policy_version): report-reassert TTL,
     investigation cooldown, reinvestigate-stale window, storm correlation
     window, storm confidence threshold, stabilization window, suppression TTL,
     auto-snooze policy, handoff threshold, knowledge authority filter,
     source-health confidence policy, child-suppression-under-meta-case policy.
     Every case_event and decision trace records the active policy_version;
     replay/eval compares behavior by policy_version (§9). This is the single
     versioned source that replaces the scattered constants in
     config.py:ProactiveLoopSettings.

     ---
     4. Proposed State Machine

     Implemented in CaseService (over CaseStore) as the single owner of these
     transitions for both proactive scans and reactive webhooks. The loop,
     webhook ingress, and the LangGraph graph are clients that submit
     observations/results and read context — never status.

     Atomic case (reconcile with existing statuses; do not invent a parallel 
     enum)

     Keep investigating → waiting_approval → recovered_pending → resolved, plus
     expired, linked, and add acknowledged/snoozed as suppression attributes
     (not lifecycle status) and handed_off as a handoff_status attribute. Key
     transitions:

     Trigger: Unhealthy observation
     Evidence: rule evaluated unhealthy
     Case writes: last_observed_unhealthy, signal_snapshot/signature, severity;
     open
       if new
     Event: case_observed_unhealthy
     Report?: on open / sev / signature change
     Investigate?: yes (if gate)
     Handoff?: if warrants_change
     Trace?: yes
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Trigger: Clean observation
     Evidence: rule evaluated clean
     Case writes: last_observed_clean, last_evaluated_at
     Event: case_observed_clean
     Report?: on transition
     Investigate?: no
     Handoff?: no
     Trace?: yes
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Trigger: Skipped rule / no observation
     Evidence: rule not evaluated
     Case writes: last_scan_cycle_id only (optional
     case_not_observed_this_cycle) —
       never touch lifecycle
     Event: low-noise
     Report?: no
     Investigate?: no
     Handoff?: no
     Trace?: optional
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Trigger: Signal changed
     Evidence: signal_signature≠prev
     Case writes: update snapshot/sev
     Event: case_signal_changed
     Report?: yes
     Investigate?: re-eligible
     Handoff?: maybe
     Trace?: yes
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Trigger: Stale diagnosis
     Evidence: now>reinvestigate_after
     Case writes: —
     Event: —
     Report?: no
     Investigate?: re-eligible
     Handoff?: —
     Trace?: yes
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Trigger: Operator ack/snooze/close
     Evidence: operator action
     Case writes: suppression fields / closed_at
     Event: case_snoozed/case_closed
     Report?: confirm
     Investigate?: no
     Handoff?: no
     Trace?: yes (+feedback)
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Trigger: Issue created / exists
     Evidence: handoff result
     Case writes: issue_url/issue_id / no-op
     Event: handoff_created_issue / handoff_skipped_existing_issue
     Report?: maybe
     Investigate?: —
     Handoff?: idempotent
     Trace?: yes
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Trigger: Suppression expiry
     Evidence: now>suppressed_until
     Case writes: clear fields
     Event: case_suppression_expired
     Report?: re-eligible
     Investigate?: re-eligible
     Handoff?: —
     Trace?: yes
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Trigger: Reassert TTL
     Evidence: now-last_reported_at≥report_reassert_s
     Case writes: last_reasserted_at
     Event: case_reasserted
     Report?: yes
     Investigate?: no
     Handoff?: no
     Trace?: yes
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Trigger: Investigation skipped (same signature)
     Evidence: recent diagnosis + unchanged
     Case writes: prior_diagnosis_refs
     Event: investigation_skipped_recent_same_signature
     Report?: no
     Investigate?: no
     Handoff?: no
     Trace?: yes
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Trigger: Resolve (positive clean)
     Evidence: clean observation + (recovery cooldown)
     Case writes: resolved_at, resolution_reason
     Event: case_resolved_positive_clean
     Report?: once
     Investigate?: no
     Handoff?: close issue
     Trace?: yes → lesson candidate
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Trigger: False positive / false all-clear
     Evidence: operator label
     Case writes: operator_outcome_label
     Event: operator_feedback_recorded
     Report?: maybe
     Investigate?: —
     Handoff?: —
     Trace?: yes → eval + candidate

     Invariant (subsumes #31): resolve requires positive clean observation
     (proactive) or recovery event + RECOVERY_COOLDOWN_SECONDS (reactive) or
     operator close or an explicit, named stale policy. Absence from a scan set,
     a skipped deep rule, or a degraded scan must not resolve or all-clear.

     Meta-case states

     candidate_event → active_event → investigating_event → monitoring_recovery 
     → stabilized → resolved → closed, plus split / merged. Transitions per the
     prompt; enforced rules: (a) active_event only when correlation confidence ≥
     threshold or operator-confirmed; (b) monitoring_recovery → stabilized only
     after all required positive clean observations or a stability window with
     no recurrence; (c) a meta-case must not resolve merely because 
     notifications stopped — root child stays active while the asset is down;
     (d) child cases may resolve individually while the meta-case persists.

     Meta-case correlation (deterministic-first, LLM-second)

     CorrelationService groups via layered evidence, each layer written to
     meta_case_correlation_evidence; the LLM is explanatory only and is never 
     the sole authority for durable attach/detach:

     1. Source-native: Alertmanager group labels, Icinga host/service
     relationships, source fingerprints, firing/clear pairs.
     2. Topology/dependency: same router/switch/site/customer/service,
     parent/child (topology_parents/infra:parent:*), upstream/downstream,
     interface bundle/LAG, circuit, peer, route adjacency.
     3. Temporal storm heuristics: burst windows, peak rate, notification
     sequence, simultaneous fire/clear patterns.
     4. Approved hyrule-knowledge patterns: known reconvergence windows,
     router/link/site failure runbooks, monitoring-cascade notes, customer/site
     patterns (retrieved + cited per §6).
     5. LLM hypothesis: grouping/root-cause proposal only; cannot by itself
     create durable attach/detach.

     Every attach records correlation_reason, correlation_confidence, and
     correlation_features.

     Child suppression under a meta-case (reversible, evidence-based)

     An attached child may carry covered_by_meta_case=true,
     independent_action_required=false,
     child_report_suppressed_reason="explained_by_meta_case". It must become 
     independently reportable/investigable again when any of: severity
     increases; signal materially changes; child persists after the meta-case
     stabilizes; a new customer/site/service is affected; the root-cause
     hypothesis is rejected; operator marks independent_action_required;
     correlation confidence drops below threshold; the child no longer fits the
     meta-case evidence. (Tests per §8.)

     Source-health / monitoring-failure awareness

     Storms can come from the network or from monitoring itself. Observations
     carry source_health + observation_confidence; meta-cases support
     event_type=monitoring_failure. Rules: if source_health∈{degraded,failed},
     absence of alerts or sudden clears is not strong clean evidence and lowers 
     auto-resolution confidence; a monitoring-region failure can itself open a
     meta-case; clean observations are source-aware and detector-aware. (Tests:
     monitoring-system outage; source-degraded false all-clear prevention.)

     ---
     5. Stage-by-Stage Refactor Plan

     Layering (the spine). The authoritative state machine lives in a new shared
     case/correlation service — app/cases/service.py:CaseService and
     app/cases/correlation.py:CorrelationService, over
     app/cases/store.py:CaseStore (Postgres). Everything else is a thin client:

     Component: app/proactive/loop.py:ProactiveLoop
     Role: Deterministic runtime/scheduler: paces cycles, runs scanners, builds
     the
       CycleSnapshot, may invoke NOCDutyOfficerAgent, drives work. Side effects 
     run
        via outbox workers, not the loop. No durable decision state.
     Writes case truth?: No — calls CaseService
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Component: app/main.py:/webhook/* (reactive)
     Role: Ingress: normalizes notifications
     Writes case truth?: No — calls CaseService.observe_notification
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Component: app/graph/* (LangGraph)
     Role: Investigation consumer/producer: reads case+meta-case+knowledge
     context,
       returns a structured InvestigationResult
     Writes case truth?: No — results applied via
       CaseService.record_investigation_result
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Component: app/cases/service.py:CaseService
     Role: Owns lifecycle, observation truth, reporting dedup, investigation
     reuse,
       suppression, handoff idempotency, resolve
     Writes case truth?: Yes (sole owner)
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Component: app/cases/correlation.py:CorrelationService
     Role: Owns storm detection + meta-case
       create/attach/detach/merge/split/stabilize
     Writes case truth?: Yes (sole owner)

     Both proactive scan observations and reactive webhook alerts enter through
     the same CaseService.observe* API and the same CorrelationService — one
     concern, one record. The LangGraph graph never flips case
     status/suppression/handoff/resolve/correlation; today's in-graph
     correlate_and_dedupe and intake-driven status transitions move into the
     service. Each stage is therefore a service interaction (loop = caller):

     Observe / scan — the loop scans, then writes each result to the durable
     observation_inbox (idempotent on dedup_key); a normalizer produces
     observations that CaseService.observe(...) applies in one transaction
     (unhealthy/clean). A skipped rule writes no inbox row → no clean
     observation. The service maps the observation to a case, appends an
     observation event, updates last_observed_*/signal_signature, and decides
     lifecycle. This replaces the loop's _merge_with_carried carry (E): a deep
     rule not scanned has no fresh clean observation, so its case stays active
     in the service — no in-memory list, preserving #31. Observation events are
     the replay/eval substrate (§9).

     Rank / gate — governance.evaluate_gate becomes a pure function over
     CaseService.eligible(...)
     (status/severity/signal_signature/suppression/handoff/reinvestigate_after);
     suppressed/handed-off/recently-diagnosed cases drop out without losing
     visibility. Relevant hyrule-knowledge (§6) and ProactiveMemory patterns are
     advisory inputs only. The loop drives the budgeted subset (kicks off
     investigations); side effects still run via the outbox, and the service
     records the gate trace.

     Investigate — the loop asks CaseService.eligible_for_investigation(); for
     each it runs the LangGraph graph as a consumer (seeded by the service with
     prior diagnosis + knowledge citations) and hands the structured result back
     via CaseService.record_investigation_result(). The skip/reuse decision
     (recent last_investigated_at and diagnosis_signature==signal_signature;
     replaces B/investigations.json) and the
     investigation_skipped_recent_same_signature trace live in the service, not
     the loop or graph. Result schema: root cause, confidence,
     supporting/disconfirming evidence, citations, recommended actions,
     escalation, unresolved questions, model/prompt/policy versions, token cost.

     Report — CaseService.report_decisions(cycle) returns report-worthy
     transitions (open/sev/status/material-signal/reassert-TTL/resolution/handof
     f/suppression/recommendation-change) and owns last_reported_* (replaces A).
     It enqueues a side_effect_outbox report intent (idempotency
     report:{case_id}:{state_signature}) inside the transaction; an outbox
     worker renders + sends and records the result via
     CaseService.mark_reported(...) — a crash/retry never double-posts. Child
     reports under an active meta-case are suppressed by CorrelationService.
     Each report trace links case state, signals, reused diagnosis, knowledge
     citations, and versions; operator accept/ignore/correct/reject attaches
     back as feedback.

     Handoff — CaseService.handoff_intent(case) returns create/comment/skip from
     case.issue_url/issue_id (replaces C); it enqueues a side_effect_outbox
     handoff intent (idempotency handoff:{case_id}:{handoff_policy_version}); an
     outbox worker performs the GitHub call and records the result via
     CaseService.record_handoff(...), which atomically stores issue_url/issue_id
     + appends handoff_created_issue. Body-marker search is a safety fallback
     only. Meta-case handoff is one issue; existing child issues are linked, not
     duplicated. Outcomes (accepted/closed-dup/edited/re-severitied/routed)
     become eval signal.

     Snooze / ack / suppress — operator and agent suppression go through
     CaseService.suppress(...)/ack(...) (replaces D); SuppressionStore becomes a
     read-fallback shim. Operator vs agent via suppression_source; TTL via
     suppressed_until/snoozed_until; expiry evaluated in the service from the
     case (no side-store cleanup). _auto_snooze calls the service. Reasons feed
     candidate known-benign/maintenance knowledge.

     Resolve — CaseService.resolve(...) requires a positive clean observation
     (proactive) or recovery+RECOVERY_COOLDOWN_SECONDS (reactive), reusing the
     existing recovered_pending→resolved machinery now hosted in the service
     (incident_memory.py:_expire_*_cases moves under CaseStore/CaseService);
     expired (idle) stays distinct. The loop never resolves.

     Correlate (storm) — after observe, both the loop and the webhook path call
     CorrelationService.correlate(observations); meta-case
     creation/attachment/stabilization is entirely service-owned (§4 meta-case
     states).

     Knowledge extraction — on resolve/operator-confirm, CaseService (not the
     loop or graph) emits a sanitized learning_ledger_v1 candidate via a
     knowledge_candidate outbox intent (idempotency
     knowledge_candidate:{case_id|meta_case_id}:{event_id}) →
     app/knowledge/promotion.py (event_type
     lesson_candidate/noc_shadow_eval_summary, producer noc_shadow, status
     proposed, authority A4) → review-gated import into
     knowledge/ledger/proposed/ (§6). Never auto-promoted.

     Ingestion & side effects (inbox → service → outbox)

     One transactional spine for both proactive scans and reactive webhooks:
     raw webhook / scanner result / notification → observation_inbox (durable, 
     dedup_key) → normalized observation → CaseService transaction {update 
     projection + append case_event + insert outbox intent} → outbox worker 
     performs side effect (FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED) → result written back via 
     CaseService.
     The inbox absorbs duplicate delivery, retries, source replay,
     crash-before-apply, bursts, and storm-replay fixtures, and preserves
     raw-vs-normalized for audit. The outbox makes reports/tickets/candidates
     idempotent across crashes/retries (keys above). Neither service performs a 
     network side effect inside a state transition.

     Operator control surfaces

     Every correction attaches to case_id/meta_case_id, trace_id?, actor,
     reason, timestamp and becomes a case_event (+ feedback), mutating state
     only via CaseService/CorrelationService. Map to existing surfaces where
     present (today: nocctl decide; Discord /noc_ack /noc_unack /noc_acks
     /noc_pending /noc_status /noc_decide /noc_investigate; HTTP
     /control/proactive/ack|unack, /control/incidents/{id}/decision); add
     meta-case verbs:
     - CLI (nocctl): case merge|split|attach|detach|confirm-root-cause|reject-ro
     ot-cause|mark-independent-action-required|suppress|ack|close.
     - Discord:
     /noc_case_merge|split|attach|detach|confirm|reject|independent_action.
     - HTTP: POST /control/cases/{id}/merge|split|attach|detach|feedback.

     Agentic planning in the cycle (additive)

     The deterministic stages above remain the validated law. When the agent
     layer is enabled, ProactiveLoop.run_once becomes:
     drain observation_inbox / run scans → CaseService applies observations → 
     CorrelationService updates meta-cases → build frozen CycleSnapshot → 
     (optionally) invoke NOCDutyOfficerAgent → record CyclePlan in the trace 
     store → CaseService/CorrelationService validate proposed ActionIntents → 
     accepted ValidatedIntents become case_events and/or side_effect_outbox rows
     → deterministic outbox workers execute → results written back through the 
     services.

     Per-stage overlay (proposal → deterministic validation):

     Stage: Observe/scan
     Agent proposes: nothing (truth is deterministic); may reason over the
     resulting
       snapshot
     Validated by: normalization + CaseService.observe stay deterministic
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Stage: Rank/gate
     Agent proposes: priority_order, investigation/report/handoff focus
     Validated by: CaseService vs budget/suppression/policy/lifecycle
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Stage: Correlate
     Agent proposes: storm_hypotheses, grouping, parent/root
     Validated by: CorrelationService (evidence/confidence/operator); LLM never
     sole
       authority
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Stage: Investigate
     Agent proposes: investigation plans; InvestigationAgent/LangGraph runs from

       approved context
     Validated by: CaseService records InvestigationResult; agent can't mark
       diagnosed/resolved
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Stage: Report
     Agent proposes: IncidentScribeAgent drafts text
     Validated by: CaseService decides report-worthiness; send is outbox-only
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Stage: Handoff
     Agent proposes: EscalationCoordinatorAgent drafts title/body/route/severity
     Validated by: CaseService idempotency + issue_url/issue_id; create is
       outbox-only
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Stage: Snooze/ack/suppress
     Agent proposes: recommend suppression or operator question
     Validated by: CaseService policy or operator approval; no silent suppress
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Stage: Resolve
     Agent proposes: "appears recovered"
     Validated by: CaseService requires positive clean / recovery / operator
     close /
       explicit stale; invalid proposal rejected + traced
     ────────────────────────────────────────
     Stage: Knowledge extraction
     Agent proposes: LearningCuratorAgent drafts candidate
     Validated by: review-gated promotion; agent never writes approved knowledge

     ---
     6. hyrule-knowledge Integration Plan

     Repository shape (confirmed). OKF Markdown+frontmatter (okf/); exports
     exports/knowledge.sqlite (tables concepts, concept_fts FTS5,
     source_refs(repo,path,commit_sha,url), claims, context_packs,
     learning_events, …) + *.jsonl + manifest.json
     (retrieval_version=retrieval_v1, policy_version=knowledge_policy_v1,
     run_id, source_shas); policy knowledge-policy.yml; ledger lifecycle +
     promotion.py; CI opens review-gated PRs.

     Retrieval bridge (export-authoritative + replayable, D4). New
     app/knowledge/retrieval.py in noc-agent:
     - Pin a knowledge export at a known revision: vendor/sync knowledge.sqlite
     (+ manifest.json) to a path the agent reads read-only; record
     export_version = manifest.run_id + knowledge git commit. A small
     app/knowledge/sync.py (or CI artifact) refreshes the pin deliberately.
     - Query concepts/concept_fts/source_refs scoped by case context
     (fingerprint, rule_id, resource/site/customer, vendor/platform, symptoms,
     signal_signature, topology, issue labels). Return candidates with
     doc_path(concepts.path), doc_id(concepts.id), review_status, authority,
     source_refs.commit_sha, FTS score. Filter to approved/authoritative tiers;
     mark deprecated/stale as non-authoritative.
     - Cite in every trace: doc_path, doc_id, review_status, section,
     repo_revision, export_version. Production decisions + replay/evals are
     reproducible from the pin alone.
     - Optional enrichment: add the knowledge MCP server as a noc MCP source (a
     new read-only noc role in knowledge-policy.yml, modeled on noc_shadow) for
     richer context_pack.generate/resolve. If MCP is unavailable, only optional
     enrichment degrades — never core behavior.

     Promotion bridge (review-gated). app/knowledge/promotion.py emits
     learning_ledger_v1 events (validated against
     knowledge/schema/learning-event.schema.json; forbidden data classes
     screened:
     secret/credential/raw_log/packet_capture/command_output/live_trace)
     carrying case ids, sanitized timeline, suspected/final root cause, blast
     radius, what was symptom vs action, stabilization window, counterexamples,
     operator feedback, confidence, source citations. Flow: resolved/confirmed
     case → sanitized event → knowledge/ledger/proposed/ → human ledger --review
     / promote-pr → okf/curated/{lessons,summaries} (A1/A2). Statuses live in
     frontmatter + learning-event metadata (existing convention) — no new
     metadata scheme.

     Safety / model sovereignty. Unreviewed events stay A4 and are never
     retrieved as authoritative; promotion is PR-gated; retrieval and citation
     are model-agnostic and reproducible from the pinned export, so a model swap
     keeps identical institutional inputs.

     Retrieval authority rules

     - Approved/curated OKF (authority∈{canonical,advisory},
     review_status=approved) may influence operational recommendations.
     - Candidate/shadow knowledge (A4, proposed) may be retrieved only as 
     non-authoritative context, labeled as such.
     - Deprecated/rejected knowledge must not be used as guidance except to
     avoid known-bad recommendations.
     - Every retrieved item cites doc_path, doc_id, review_status, authority
     tier, section, repo_revision, export_version. (Test §8: deprecated/rejected
     present but never used authoritatively.)

     ---
     7. Migration Plan

     1. Stand up Postgres (net-new). Add app/db/{engine,models}.py (async
     SQLAlchemy 2.0 + asyncpg), alembic/ migrations, DATABASE_URL/NOC_PG_*
     config in app/config.py. Tables: cases (atomic+meta via kind), case_events,
     observations, handoffs, suppressions, feedback, traces,
     knowledge_citations, plus LangGraph checkpoint tables
     (langgraph-checkpoint-postgres).
     2. Add the shared case service + Postgres backend. Introduce
     app/cases/{store,service,correlation,models}.py: a CaseStore protocol +
     PostgresCaseStore (authoritative; local/in-mem for dev/test) and the
     CaseService/CorrelationService that own the state machine. Refactor
     IncidentMemory to delegate to CaseStore/CaseService; route reactive
     intake_alert and proactive observe through CaseService. No production path 
     depends on Redis. One-shot importer backfills any open Redis/in-mem cases
     on first boot.
     3. Postgres LangGraph checkpointer. Extend
     app/graph/checkpointing.py:build_checkpointer to prefer a Postgres saver
     (DATABASE_URL), Redis/in-mem only as fallback.
     4. Fold side stores (transitional dual-read). New writes go to case state;
     old investigations.json/suppressions.json/in-mem signatures are read as 
     fallback until Phases 3–6 land, then removed. Handoff issue_url backfilled
     by one marker-search per open proactive case.
     5. Classify ProactiveMemory entries: operational state (none) / candidate
     lesson (proposals/ → ledger candidates) / durable knowledge (validated
     lessons → OKF promotion) / stale-noisy (drop). No bulk write to approved
     knowledge.
     6. Schema versioning: schema_version on every case; lazy upgrade on load;
     alembic for DB. Keep back-compat dict round-trip through the transition.

     Postgres concurrency & locking

     - Replace app/main.py:_try_acquire_proactive_lock with a Postgres advisory 
     lock (pg_advisory_lock) for the single-cycle guard.
     - Unique constraints for observation idempotency
     (observation_inbox.dedup_key) and source dedup; outbox idempotency_key
     unique.
     - SELECT … FOR UPDATE for case/meta-case projection updates;
     row_version/updated_at compare-and-swap for optimistic concurrency where
     contended.
     - FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED for outbox workers.
     - Explicit transaction boundaries around observation → case_event → 
     projection → outbox (replaces the Redis noc:intake:lock semantics in
     incident_memory.py:_intake_alert_redis).
     - Never silently fall back to in-memory state in production — fail loud if
     DATABASE_URL is unset. Tests for crash/retry/idempotency.

     Retention, partitioning & payload storage

     Postgres durability replaces Redis TTLs, so retention is explicit:
     - cases/meta_cases: durable, long retention.
     - case_events: durable; partition by month/time window if volume warrants.
     - observations: retain normalized for the replay window; compact/archive
     older routine data.
     - Raw payloads: do not store large blobs in core tables — keep in
     object/file storage or compressed archive, referenced by payload_ref.
     - traces: retain eval-worthy long-term; compact routine.
     - side_effect_outbox: short retention after success, longer for failures.
     - Knowledge candidates: governed by the knowledge repo review policy.
     - Sensitive-data redaction runs before any trace or knowledge candidate is
     emitted (reuse the learning-event.schema.json data-class screening).

     ---
     Production Hardening

     Postgres production readiness

     - Backup/PITR: WAL archiving + base backups (pgBackRest or managed PITR);
     documented RPO/RTO; cases/case_events are the protected crown jewels.
     - Restore drills: scheduled restore-to-scratch verifying
     cases/case_events/observations integrity and that alembic is at head; drill
     is an ops checklist item.
     - Migrations: every alembic migration ships a dry-run (alembic upgrade 
     --sql) and a tested downgrade; runs in a maintenance window with the loop
     paused; boot schema-readiness check (alembic at head, required
     tables/constraints present) or fail loud.
     - Connection pool: bounded async pool (size/overflow/pool_timeout) with
     statement + lock timeouts shared by store and outbox workers.
     - DB unavailable / degraded mode: if Postgres is unreachable the loop
     enters degraded mode — no observation application, no side effects,
     heartbeat reports degraded, alerts fire; it never falls back to in-memory
     truth and never resolves/all-clears. Fail loud if DATABASE_URL is unset in
     prod.

     Dead-letter & reconciliation

     - observation_inbox: after max_attempts → normalization_failed/dead-letter
     with dead_letter_reason; operator-visible failed-inbox count; nocctl inbox 
     reprocess re-runs normalization after an adapter fix.
     - side_effect_outbox: in_progress past a timeout is reclaimed; after
     max_attempts → abandoned/dead-letter; a reconciliation worker reconciles
     external state (GitHub/Discord) so there are no duplicate external side 
     effects after a crash. Handles: (a) issue created but issue_url unrecorded
     — reconcile by querying GitHub for the idempotency marker before
     re-creating; (b) report sent but mark_reported failed — state_signature
     dedup prevents re-send; (c) knowledge candidate written but completion 
     failed — event_id idempotency prevents a duplicate ledger entry.

     Monitoring source adapter contract

     Each adapter (Alertmanager, Icinga, future) declares: source_name,
     source_type, dedup_key strategy, source_event_id mapping, firing/clear
     semantics, whether clear events are authoritative/advisory/unreliable,
     severity mapping, entity/resource/site/customer/service mapping, timestamp
     fields + time-skew tolerance, grouping labels, native correlation IDs,
     source_health mapping, payload redaction rules. The contract drives
     observation_inbox normalization and the source-health policy (§4); a clear
     marked unreliable never becomes strong clean evidence.

     Topology / dependency versioning

     CycleSnapshot, traces, and meta_case_correlation_evidence gain
     topology_snapshot_id, topology_source, topology_revision,
     golden_state_manifest_hash, dependency_graph_version. Replay must freeze 
     topology/dependency inputs alongside case state, policy_version,
     model_chain, prompt_version, and knowledge_export_version, so a correlation
     decision is reproducible.

     Operator RBAC & audit

     Every operator action records actor_id, actor_role, auth_source, reason,
     approval_required, approval_granted_by, timestamp, trace_id?,
     case_id/meta_case_id. Role boundaries: viewer (read-only); operator (ack,
     short snooze, add note); senior_operator (close, longer-TTL suppress, mark
     independent action); incident_commander (merge/split meta-cases,
     confirm/reject root cause); admin (policy changes, migrations,
     replay-fixture promotion). Unauthorized merge/split/close/suppress is
     rejected + audited (tests §8).

     Service API boundary & uniqueness invariants

     CaseService commands: observe, record_investigation_result, request_report,
     request_handoff, suppress, ack, resolve, record_operator_feedback,
     record_outbox_result. Queries: get_case, eligible_cases,
     build_case_context, reportable_transitions, investigation_candidates.
     CorrelationService commands: correlate, attach_child, detach_child,
     merge_meta_cases, split_meta_case, mark_independent_action_required,
     set_root_cause_hypothesis, stabilize_meta_case. Queries: active_meta_cases,
     children_for_meta_case, candidate_groupings, blast_radius.
     Uniqueness invariants (DB-enforced via partial unique indexes): at most one
     active atomic case per canonical active identity; a child belongs to at
     most one active meta-case; a handoff idempotency key maps to at most one
     external issue; a report state_signature maps to at most one sent report.
     Physical schema: prefer one cases table with kind∈{atomic,meta} unless a
     repo constraint says otherwise.

     Tool execution safety

     Investigation tools are read-only by default, allowlisted, timeout- and 
     budget-bounded, versioned (tool_version in traces), and redacted before
     traces/knowledge candidates. No remediation/write action runs without an
     explicit ValidatedIntent and the appropriate operator/policy approval.

     ---
     8. Testing Plan

     Add/extend under hyrule-noc-agent/tests/ (mirroring test_proactive_loop.py,
     test_incident_memory*, test_proactive_suppressions.py,
     test_proactive_handoff.py, test_proactive_investigate.py,
     test_knowledge_shadow.py):
     - False all-clear prevention: case exists; next cycle skips/degrades the
     rule → case stays active; no resolve/all-clear (regression-locks #31 at the
     case level).
     - Positive clean resolve: rule evaluated clean → resolves once; one resolve
     report.
     - Report dedup / reassert: stable unhealthy state → one report then
     reassert only after TTL; per-cycle jitter posts nothing.
     - Signal change: material signal change flips report/investigation
     eligibility.
     - Investigation reuse: same signal_signature+recent → skip with reused
     diagnosis; changed → reinvestigate with prior diagnosis in context.
     - Handoff idempotency: issue_url present → never duplicates; absent →
     creates+stores; partial-failure retry safe.
     - Snooze/ack TTL: snoozed until TTL; expiry restores visibility; operator
     ack survives scan jitter; repeated benign snooze → candidate lesson.
     - Meta-case suite: router-down cascade (one meta-case, children attached,
     one report, one issue); self-healing reconvergence
     (→monitoring_recovery/stabilized, root stays active, resolve only on
     clean); unrelated simultaneous alerts (no false grouping); operator
     split/merge captured as feedback+eval; existing child issue linked, no dup.
     - Knowledge retrieval: matching case retrieves approved doc; deprecated not
     authoritative; trace cites path/id/status/section/revision/export_version;
     stable across model adapters; reproducible from pinned export with MCP
     down.
     - Knowledge candidate: resolved meta-case emits A4 candidate with
     case/trace ids, timeline, blast radius, counterexamples; not approved
     without review; rejected not retrieved.
     - Migration: old JSON side stores read as fallback; existing cases
     readable; ProactiveMemory not blind-promoted; knowledge export indexed/read
     without mutation.
     - Postgres backend: CRUD + concurrency/atomicity (intake lock equivalent),
     no-Redis run is fully durable.
     - No sixth memory: assert no new ad-hoc anti-dup file is introduced.
     - Model-swap: same case state + same pinned knowledge + same policy →
     acceptable behavior under an alternate model_chain.
     - Service ownership: a proactive scan and a reactive webhook for the same
     concern converge on one case via CaseService; the LangGraph graph mutates
     no case truth (status/suppression/handoff/resolve), only returns
     InvestigationResult; the loop holds no durable decision state.
     - Observation inbox: duplicate webhook delivery / scanner retry / source
     replay yields one observation + one case effect; crash before apply
     re-processes safely.
     - Side-effect outbox: crash/retry never double-posts a report, ticket, or
     knowledge candidate; idempotency keys hold; failed intents retry with
     backoff.
     - Identity aliases: old investigations.json/suppressions.json keys, issue
     markers, and proactive/reactive fingerprints all resolve to one stable
     case_id.
     - Append-only events: projection + case_event written atomically; replay
     rebuilds state from case_events + observations.
     - Child suppression reversibility: each trigger (severity up, signal
     change, persists-after-stabilize, new site/customer, root-cause rejected,
     operator override, confidence drop, evidence mismatch) re-surfaces the
     child.
     - Monitoring-failure: source-degraded/failed → no false clean evidence;
     monitoring-region outage opens a monitoring_failure meta-case.
     - Policy version: decisions/events record policy_version; replay compares
     behavior across versions.
     - Deprecated knowledge: present but never used authoritatively; citations
     recorded.
     - Concurrency: advisory-lock single-cycle guard; FOR UPDATE SKIP LOCKED
     outbox; optimistic-concurrency conflict handling.

     Architecture boundary tests (regression guard)

     - ProactiveLoop cannot directly mutate case status.
     - LangGraph graph cannot mutate
     lifecycle/suppression/handoff/resolve/correlation state.
     - Reporter cannot send without a CaseService report intent; Handoff cannot
     create an issue without a CaseService handoff intent.
     - SuppressionStore and investigations.json are read-only fallbacks during
     migration.
     - No new anti-dup JSON side store appears; no local in-memory report
     signature is authoritative.
     - Proactive scan + reactive webhook for the same concern converge through
     CaseService; meta-case attach/detach only through CorrelationService.

     Agentic layer tests

     - Shadow mode: agent produces a CyclePlan but no case_events/outbox rows
     are created from it; trace records baseline-vs-agent diffs.
     - Outage fallback: model call fails/times out → loop continues the
     deterministic safe baseline; no state corruption.
     - Invalid resolve rejected: agent proposes resolve without positive clean →
     CaseService rejects; case stays active; rejection traced.
     - Invalid duplicate handoff rejected: agent proposes a ticket where
     issue_url/issue_id exists → rejected; no outbox handoff row.
     - Invalid suppression rejected: agent proposes silent suppression without
     policy/operator approval → rejected or requires_operator_approval.
     - Storm proposal validation: EventCorrelationAgent grouping accepted only
     with deterministic evidence/confidence/operator confirmation; else rejected
     + traced.
     - Child hidden incorrectly: agent suggests covered_by_meta_case →
     CorrelationService rejects/reverses when independent_action_required
     triggers exist.
     - Knowledge authority enforced: agent cites candidate/deprecated/rejected
     knowledge as authoritative → KnowledgeAuthorityFilter rejects/downgrades;
     violation traced.
     - Drafting separation: IncidentScribeAgent/EscalationCoordinatorAgent draft
     text, but Reporter/Handoff workers act only on a CaseService outbox
     intent.
     - Replay reproducibility: frozen CycleSnapshot + knowledge export +
     policy_version + model-output fixture reproduces the same ValidatedIntent
     results.
     - Role prompt smoke: each role profile returns its typed object shape and
     attempts no direct state mutation.

     Production-hardening tests

     - Backup restore: restore a backup to scratch; alembic at head;
     cases/case_events integrity holds.
     - Migration rollback: upgrade then downgrade leaves a consistent schema;
     dry-run SQL reviewed.
     - DB-unavailable degraded mode: Postgres down → loop degraded, no
     observation apply, no side effects, no resolve/all-clear, no in-memory 
     fallback; recovers on reconnect.
     - Inbox dead-letter + reprocess: repeated normalization failure →
     dead-letter; reprocess after fix succeeds exactly once.
     - Outbox reconciliation (crash-no-dup): issue created but issue_url
     unrecorded / report sent but mark_reported failed / candidate written but
     completion failed → reconciliation produces no duplicate external effect.
     - Adapter contract conformance: each adapter maps
     dedup/firing-clear/severity/entity/source_health per contract; an
     unreliable clear is not treated as clean evidence.
     - RBAC: unauthorized merge/split/close/suppress rejected + audited.
     - Uniqueness invariants: concurrent intake cannot create two active cases
     for one identity; a child cannot attach to two active meta-cases; a handoff
     key → one issue; a report state_signature → one send.
     - Tool safety: non-allowlisted/write tool blocked; timeout/budget enforced.

     ---
     9. Private Eval / Replay Plan

     Add hyrule-noc-agent/evals/replay/ and a nocctl replay path. A replay =
     time-ordered notification/observation stream + frozen case states + pinned 
     knowledge export revision + frozen ProactiveMemory → run through a
     candidate policy/model/prompt/toolchain → compare
     decisions/non-decisions/report/handoff/resolve and cost against expected.
     Build fixtures from real case_events + traces (sanitized). Metrics: false
     all-clear rate, duplicate report/handoff rate, investigation-reuse
     accuracy, correct reinvestigation on change, knowledge-use correctness,
     severity/blast accuracy, storm detection latency, grouping
     precision/recall/false-grouping/missed-grouping, premature-resolution rate,
     operator-correction rate, time-to-diagnosis, token/tool cost per useful
     case, regression on known incidents. This is the data+eval substrate for 
     later RL/prompt/policy optimization — no RL training in this refactor.
     Cross-check against the knowledge repo's own deterministic evals
     (knowledge/evals/, noc_shadow suite).

     Agent replay & metrics

     Replay must freeze: CycleSnapshot, policy_version,
     knowledge_export_version, model_chain, prompt_version, agent deployment
     mode, tool availability, and (where deterministic replay is required) an
     expected model-output fixture. Replay compares: deterministic baseline
     decision, NOCDutyOfficerAgent CyclePlan, ValidatedIntent results, final
     case/meta-case transitions, outbox intents, operator corrections, and
     token/tool cost. Metrics: useful_priority_order_rate,
     invalid_agent_intent_rate, rejected_resolve_intent_rate,
     rejected_duplicate_handoff_intent_rate, storm_hypothesis_precision/recall,
     operator_acceptance_rate, operator_override_rate, agent_timeout_rate,
     deterministic_fallback_rate, knowledge_citation_correctness,
     deprecated_knowledge_misuse_rate, token_cost_per_validated_intent.

     ---

     Structured app.log events (low-noise) + trace records: case_created,
     case_observed_unhealthy/clean, case_skipped_no_observation,
     case_report_suppressed_no_state_change, case_reasserted,
     investigation_skipped_recent_same_signature,
