     hyrule_knowledge_not_found, hyrule_knowledge_deprecated_reference_skipped,
     knowledge_candidate_created/promoted/rejected,
     handoff_skipped_existing_issue, handoff_created_issue, case_snoozed,
     case_suppression_expired, case_resolved_positive_clean,
     operator_feedback_recorded, eval_trace_recorded; plus meta-case events
     (storm_candidate_detected, meta_case_created/updated,
     child_case_attached/detached, meta_case_merged/split,
     root_cause_hypothesis_set/changed, blast_radius_expanded/reduced,
     child_report_suppressed_by_meta_case,
     child_investigation_skipped_covered_by_meta_case,
     meta_case_reported/handed_off, self_healing_detected,
     reconvergence_suspected, meta_case_entered_monitoring_recovery,
     meta_case_stabilized, meta_case_resolved_positive_clean,
     operator_confirmed/rejected_grouping, storm_pattern_candidate_created,
     storm_pattern_promoted_to_hyrule_knowledge). Enough to debug flapping, dup
     work, bad suppression, stale-knowledge reuse, missed retrieval, dup
     tickets, false all-clears, model-swap regressions.

     Agentic layer events

     cycle_snapshot_built, noc_duty_officer_invoked,
     noc_duty_officer_skipped_disabled, noc_duty_officer_timeout,
     cycle_plan_created, cycle_plan_recorded_shadow,
     agent_action_intent_proposed, agent_action_intent_accepted,
     agent_action_intent_rejected,
     agent_action_intent_requires_operator_approval,
     invalid_agent_resolve_rejected, invalid_agent_handoff_rejected,
     invalid_agent_suppression_rejected,
     agent_storm_hypothesis_proposed/accepted/rejected,
     agent_knowledge_citation_rejected, deterministic_fallback_used,
     operator_approved_agent_intent, operator_rejected_agent_intent. Each
     carries cycle_id, plan_id?, case_id/meta_case_id?, policy_version,
     model_chain, prompt_version, knowledge_export_version, deployment_mode,
     rejection_reason?.

     NOC agent self-monitoring

     Production metrics/alerts (extend the Icinga heartbeat _heartbeat +
     app/model_metrics.py counters): cycle duration; cycle failures; Postgres
     connection failures; advisory-lock acquisition failures; observation_inbox
     backlog + normalization failures; side_effect_outbox backlog + dead
     letters; report-send failures; handoff failures; agent timeout rate;
     deterministic fallback rate; knowledge export age + retrieval failures;
     meta-case grouping rate; operator override rate; duplicate-prevention hits.

     ---
     11. Rollout / Commit Plan (small, reviewable PRs)

     Strangler migration: 1A–1C are non-breaking scaffolding; 1D–1J are
     individually revertible flips behind config flags. Each bullet is its own
     small PR.

     - Phase 0 — Preserve #31. Confirm main carry-forward fix + reactive
     recovery/expiry semantics are untouched; add the false-all-clear regression
     test as the guard rail.
     - Phase 1A — Postgres schema + store (no behavior change). app/db/,
     alembic, app/cases/store.py (CaseStore + PostgresCaseStore), Postgres
     LangGraph checkpointer, config. Dormant. (Foundational.)
     - Phase 1B — Inbox + Outbox + substrate (no behavior change).
     observation_inbox, side_effect_outbox, case_events, case_identity_aliases,
     meta_case_correlation_evidence, CasePolicy; workers built but unused.
     - Phase 1C — Shadow write + compare. Shadow-write
     observations/case_events/traces to Postgres while the old runtime stays
     authoritative; compare old decisions vs CaseService candidate decisions;
     emit metrics, no side effects.
     - Phase 1D — Flip observe/resolve to CaseService (retire
     _last_deep_hotspots/_last_effective; preserve #31; refactor IncidentMemory
     to delegate; LangGraph becomes a read-only consumer returning
     InvestigationResult).
     - Phase 1E — Flip report dedup/reassert to CaseService + outbox (retire
     A/_last_report_signature).
     - Phase 1F — Flip investigation reuse to CaseService (retire
     B/investigations.json; graph stays consumer).
     - Phase 1G — Flip suppression/ack/snooze to CaseService (D → read-only
     fallback).
     - Phase 1H — Flip handoff idempotency to issue_url/issue_id + outbox (C →
     marker fallback).
     - Phase 1I — Meta-case correlation in shadow (CorrelationService;
     deterministic layers; no child suppression / no meta reports yet).
     - Phase 1J — Enable meta-case reporting/handoff after storm tests pass
     (child suppression on; one meta report; one meta issue; existing child
     issues linked).
     - Phase 2 — Trace store + operator-feedback attachment points + meta-case
     operator verbs (Postgres).
     - Phase 3 — Knowledge retrieval bridge (pinned export + citations +
     authority rules; optional MCP noc role).
     - Phase 4 — Candidate knowledge extraction (app/knowledge/promotion.py via
     outbox → review-gated ledger).
     - Phase 5 — Private eval/replay fixtures from
     case_events/observations/traces + frozen knowledge revisions.
     - Agentic phases (after Phase 2 trace store + Phase 3 knowledge retrieval;
     guarded_act gated by Phase 5 eval/replay):
       - Agent-0 — Contracts + plan trace storage. Define
     CycleSnapshot/CyclePlan/ActionIntent/ValidatedIntent; store CyclePlan in
     the trace store. No model calls.
       - Agent-1 — disabled mode. Add NOCDutyOfficerAgent; wire config +
     deployment mode; no live invocation.
       - Agent-2 — shadow mode. Build CycleSnapshot after service updates;
     invoke the agent; store CyclePlan and compare to the deterministic
     baseline; no side effects.
       - Agent-3 — Role prompts/tools (EventCorrelation, KnowledgeLibrarian,
     SourceHealth, IncidentScribe, EscalationCoordinator); still shadow/advise
     only.
       - Agent-4 — advise mode. Suggestions visible to operators; manual action
     only.
       - Agent-5 — guarded_act (low-risk only) after replay/eval pass:
     investigate, ask_operator, draft_report, create_knowledge_candidate. No
     autonomous resolve/suppress/handoff/merge/split/close.
       - Agent-6 — guarded_act (higher-risk) only after explicit human approval
     + extra eval gates: report, handoff, attach_child_to_meta_case,
     mark_independent_action_required.
       - Never ungated autonomous: resolve without deterministic positive-clean
     validation; knowledge promotion; production fallback to local/in-memory
     truth; duplicate handoff when issue_url/issue_id exists.
     - Phase 6 — Remove/quarantine old side stores once boundary tests pass.

     Phase gates / exit criteria

     - 1C → 1D: shadow CaseService decisions match old behavior for N cycles;
     false-all-clear test passes; no duplicate-report regression; Postgres
     restart-recovery passes.
     - Meta-case enable: router-down cascade fixture passes;
     unrelated-simultaneous-alert fixture passes; grouping precision/recall
     above threshold; operator split/merge feedback works.
     - Agent guarded_act: invalid_agent_intent_rate below threshold; agent
     timeout→fallback verified; deprecated_knowledge_misuse_rate=0; no
     autonomous resolve/suppress/handoff in initial guarded_act.

     Kill switches (config flags)

     NOC_CASESERVICE_ENABLED, NOC_META_CASES_ENABLED,
     NOC_OUTBOX_WORKERS_ENABLED, NOC_KNOWLEDGE_RETRIEVAL_ENABLED,
     NOC_DUTY_OFFICER_MODE=disabled|shadow|advise|guarded_act|manual_only,
     NOC_HANDOFF_ENABLED, NOC_REPORTING_ENABLED. Each disables its capability
     without a code change; with all off, the deterministic safe baseline still
     runs.

     ---
     12. Risks and Open Questions

     - Ownership leakage (guardrail). Case lifecycle, suppression, resolution,
     reporting dedup, and meta-case correlation must live only in
     CaseService/CorrelationService — never in ProactiveLoop (scheduler) or the
     LangGraph graph (investigation consumer/producer). Enforce with tests
     asserting the graph performs no case-status/suppression/handoff/resolve
     writes, and that proactive + reactive share one service.
     - Postgres is net-new in noc-agent (only redis/langgraph-checkpoint-redis
     exist today). Phase 1 is the largest and gates everything; needs DB
     provisioning on the NOC VM and an async-SQLAlchemy concurrency model
     replicating the current Redis noc:intake:lock atomicity
     (incident_memory.py:_intake_alert_redis).
     - Fingerprint duality. Proactive hotspot fp vs alert-identity case fp;
     grounding must define one durable mapping (extend
     hotspot_to_alert_payload/_case_for_hotspot) so side-store keys and case
     keys finally coincide.
     - Ephemeral→durable shift. Today cases TTL out (CASE_HISTORY_SECONDS);
     Postgres makes them durable — define explicit retention/close policy so
     expired vs resolved stays meaningful and tables don't grow unbounded.
     - Storm correlation precision. Topology data comes from
     infra:parent:*/topology_parents; sparse topology risks mis-grouping → keep
     confidence thresholds + operator split/merge as first-class corrections.
     - Knowledge pin freshness. Export-authoritative retrieval can serve stale
     knowledge; surface export_version/repo_revision in traces and add a
     staleness warning + deliberate refresh.
     - Sensitive-data leakage into candidates — enforce
     learning-event.schema.json data-class screening + redaction before any
     ledger write; promotion stays human-gated.
     - Scope. Sections 8–11 of the prompt (meta-cases) are large; Phases 8–12
     may each split further. Confirm whether meta-cases must ship this cycle or
     can trail the operational consolidation.
     - Agent authority creep. Future patches may let the LLM mutate lifecycle
     directly — mitigate with the §8 architecture boundary tests.
     - Over-agentification. Too many agents too early adds latency/complexity —
     start with one NOCDutyOfficerAgent + internal role prompts.
     - Latency/budget. Agent planning may exceed cycle budget — require timeout,
     budget policy, deterministic fallback.
     - Confident-but-wrong. The senior persona may sound authoritative when
     wrong — require uncertainty_summary, validation, and citations.
     - Knowledge misuse / storm over-grouping / operator trust / replay 
     nondeterminism — enforce authority filters; keep correlation
     deterministic-first + operator-correctable; advise mode must show
     rationale/evidence/citations/validation status; store CyclePlan and
     optionally use model-output fixtures.
     - Postgres availability is now critical-path. Mitigate with PITR, restore
     drills, degraded mode (no in-memory fallback), and self-monitoring;
     hard-down = degraded (no autonomy), never false all-clear.
     - Partial side effects / reconciliation gaps. External create then crash
     before record — mitigate with idempotency markers + reconciliation worker;
     residual risk is a dangling external object reconciled next pass.
     - Adapter misconfiguration (wrong clear semantics) could mask or fabricate
     clears — mitigate with the adapter contract + source-health policy + tests.
     - Topology drift between snapshot and reality — mitigate with
     topology_revision capture + replay freeze.
     - RBAC bypass / over-broad operators — mitigate with role boundaries +
     audit + tests.

     Open questions (agentic): primary role name in code/config (Senior Network
     Reliability Engineer vs Senior Service Reliability Engineer vs Senior
     SRE-Network)? which intents allowed in guarded_act first? acceptable agent
     cycle-time budget? split EventCorrelationAgent out first or keep as an
     internal role prompt? operator UI for suggestions (Discord / nocctl / HTTP
     / all three)? confidence threshold that forces operator approval?

     ---
     13. Acceptance Criteria

     - The ProactiveLoop is a scheduler and the LangGraph graph an investigation
     consumer/producer; a shared CaseService/CorrelationService (over a
     Postgres CaseStore) is the sole owner of case lifecycle, suppression,
     resolution, reporting dedup, and correlation for both proactive and
     reactive inputs.
     - IncidentMemory cases (Postgres-backed) are authoritative for active
     concerns; a missed/skipped/degraded scan never causes false all-clear;
     resolve only on positive clean / recovery / operator close / explicit stale
     policy.
     - Duplicate reports prevented by case state; reassertions case-grounded;
     investigations skipped on recent same-signature diagnosis and
     reinvestigations include prior context.
     - Handoff never duplicates when issue_url/issue_id exists;
     snooze/ack/suppression live on the case with TTL semantics.
     - The five side stores are removed or reduced to temporary fallbacks; no 
     new anti-dup mechanism introduced; no production behavior depends on Redis
     as a second source of truth.
     - Case events + decision traces are replay/eval-ready; operator feedback
     attaches to case+trace ids.
     - Notification storms produce one durable meta-case (first-class
     IncidentMemory record) with linked children; self-healing handled without
     premature all-clear; operators can merge/split/attach/detach/confirm/reject
     and those corrections become learning signal.
     - hyrule-knowledge is retrieved during
     correlation/investigation/report/handoff from a pinned export, cited in 
     traces with path/id/status/section/revision/export_version, reproducible
     with MCP unavailable; resolved/confirmed cases yield review-gated
     OKF/learning_ledger_v1 candidates; approved knowledge survives a model
     swap.
     - Tests cover scan jitter, clean resolve, dedup, investigation reuse,
     handoff idempotency, suppression TTL, migration, Postgres durability,
     storms, knowledge retrieval+candidates, and model-swap.
     - The Architecture Invariants hold and are enforced by §8 boundary tests.
     - Observation Inbox provides idempotent, durable ingestion; Side-Effect 
     Outbox makes reports/handoffs/knowledge candidates crash-safe and
     idempotent.
     - case_identity_aliases resolves proactive/reactive/source/external
     identity drift to one stable case_id.
     - case_events are append-only; projections written atomically with events;
     replay rebuildable from events + observations.
     - Postgres advisory locks / unique constraints / FOR UPDATE / SKIP LOCKED
     provide production concurrency; no silent in-memory fallback.
     - Meta-case child suppression is reversible and evidence-based;
     monitoring-source degradation cannot create false clean evidence.
     - policy_version is recorded on case events/traces and is replayable;
     thresholds/TTLs are policy-driven.
     - Retention/partitioning/payload storage are explicit; sensitive-data
     redaction precedes trace/candidate emission.
     - Knowledge authority tiers are enforced during retrieval (approved
     authoritative; candidate non-authoritative; deprecated/rejected not used as
     guidance).
     - Operator merge/split/attach/detach/root-cause corrections are first-class
     feedback on case_id/meta_case_id.
     - ProactiveLoop can invoke NOCDutyOfficerAgent but remains a deterministic
     scheduler/runtime, not a state owner; the agent produces typed CyclePlan
     proposals from a frozen CycleSnapshot and cannot mutate state directly.
     - CaseService/CorrelationService validate all agent proposals before any
     case_event/outbox intent; invalid resolve, duplicate handoff, unauthorized
     suppression, and deprecated-knowledge recommendations are rejected and
     traced.
     - disabled/shadow/advise/guarded_act modes exist as rollout controls; agent
     failure/timeout falls back to the deterministic safe baseline.
     - Role profiles are documented and initially implemented as one
     NOCDutyOfficerAgent with internal role prompts/tools; replay/eval captures
     CycleSnapshot/CyclePlan/ValidatedIntent +
     policy_version/prompt_version/model_chain/knowledge_export_version;
     operator-visible suggestions include rationale, evidence refs, citations,
     confidence, and validation status.
     - Postgres has PITR + tested restore/rollback; boot does a schema-readiness
     check and fails loud; DB-down is a degraded mode with no in-memory
     fallback and no false all-clear.
     - Inbox/outbox have dead-letter + reconciliation; no duplicate external
     side effect after a crash; failed rows are operator-visible and
     reprocessable.
     - Each monitoring source has a declared adapter contract (incl.
     clear-authority + source_health); topology/dependency inputs are versioned
     and replay-frozen.
     - Operator actions carry RBAC role + audit; unauthorized
     merge/split/close/suppress is rejected.
     - CaseService/CorrelationService expose the documented command/query
     boundary with DB-enforced uniqueness invariants; physical schema is one
     cases table with kind (unless the repo says otherwise).
     - Investigation tools are read-only/allowlisted/bounded/versioned/redacted;
     no write/remediation without a validated intent + approval.
     - Kill switches exist for CaseService, meta-cases, outbox workers,
     knowledge retrieval, duty-officer mode, handoff, and reporting; rollout
     phase gates are enforced before each flip.

     ---
     Verification (how to test end-to-end)

     - Unit/integration: cd /home/svag/Dev/hyrule-noc-agent && uv run pytest
     (focused: tests/test_proactive_loop.py, test_proactive_suppressions.py,
     test_proactive_handoff.py, test_proactive_investigate.py, new
     tests/test_case_grounding.py, tests/test_meta_case.py,
     tests/test_knowledge_retrieval.py, tests/test_db_backend.py); lint/type per
     CI (ruff, mypy --strict).
     - Replay: uv run nocctl replay evals/replay/<fixture> and assert metrics
     (false-all-clear=0, grouping precision/recall, citation presence) vs
     baseline.
     - Knowledge loop: point retrieval at the pinned
     knowledge/exports/knowledge.sqlite; run an investigation; confirm trace
     citations; generate a candidate and dry-run cd /home/svag/Dev/knowledge && 
     uv run hyrule-knowledge ledger --review <id> (no auto-promote); run uv run 
     hyrule-knowledge eval --check.
     - Live smoke (shadow): NOC_PROACTIVE_ENABLED=1 NOC_PROACTIVE_SHADOW=1
     against a Postgres DATABASE_URL with no NOC_REDIS_URL; drive a synthetic
     Alertmanager/Icinga storm at /webhook/*; confirm one meta-case, no dup
     tickets, durable cases across a restart.
     - Backup/restore drill: PITR/pg_dump restore to a scratch DB, run alembic 
     upgrade head (expect no-op), verify open cases/case_events round-trip.
     - Migration rollback: alembic upgrade head then alembic downgrade -1 on
     scratch; confirm a clean schema; review alembic upgrade --sql.
     - Degraded mode: stop Postgres while the loop runs (shadow); confirm a
     degraded heartbeat, no resolves, no side effects, and clean recovery on
     restart.
     - Reconciliation: kill the process between GitHub issue create and
     record_handoff; on restart confirm the reconciliation worker links the
     existing issue (no duplicate).
     - Kill switches: flip each NOC_*_ENABLED / NOC_DUTY_OFFICER_MODE and
     confirm the capability disables while the deterministic baseline keeps
     running.
